::centre
Namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddhassa
::

# Khuddakanikāye

## Suttanipātapāḷi

### 1. Uragavaggo

#### 1. Uragasuttaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
Yo {pb:M:0.0279}{pb:V:0.0087}{pb:P:0.0001}{pb:T:0.0324} {note:yo ve (syā.)} uppatitaṃ vineti kodhaṃ, visaṭaṃ sappavisaṃva osadhehi {note:osadhebhi (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
So bhikkhu jahāti orapāraṃ, urago jiṇṇamivattacaṃ {note:jiṇṇamiva tacaṃ (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.), jiṇṇamivā tacaṃ (?)} purāṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
Yo rāgamudacchidā asesaṃ, bhisapupphaṃva saroruhaṃ {note:sareruhaṃ (ka.)} vigayha;
::

::gathalast
So bhikkhu jahāti orapāraṃ, urago jiṇṇamivattacaṃ, purāṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
Yo {pb:V:0.0088} taṇhamudacchidā asesaṃ, saritaṃ sīghasaraṃ visosayitvā;
::

::gathalast
So {pb:T:0.0325} bhikkhu jahāti orapāraṃ, urago jiṇṇamivattacaṃ purāṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
Yo {pb:M:0.0280} mānamudabbadhī asesaṃ, naḷasetuṃva sudubbalaṃ mahogho;
::

::gathalast
So bhikkhu jahāti orapāraṃ, urago jiṇṇamivattacaṃ purāṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
Yo nājjhagamā bhavesu sāraṃ, vicinaṃ pupphamiva {note:pupphamiva (bahūsu)} udumbaresu;
::

::gathalast
So bhikkhu jahāti orapāraṃ, urago jiṇṇamivattacaṃ purāṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
Yassantarato na santi kopā, itibhavābhavatañca {note:itibbhavābhavatañca (ka.)} vītivatto;
::

::gathalast
So bhikkhu jahāti orapāraṃ, urago jiṇṇamivattacaṃ purāṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
Yassa {pb:P:0.0002} vitakkā vidhūpitā, ajjhattaṃ suvikappitā asesā;
::

::gathalast
So bhikkhu jahāti orapāraṃ, urago jiṇṇamivattacaṃ purāṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
Yo nāccasārī na paccasārī, sabbaṃ accagamā imaṃ papañcaṃ;
::

::gathalast
So {pb:T:0.0326} bhikkhu jahāti orapāraṃ, urago jiṇṇamivattacaṃ purāṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
Yo nāccasārī na paccasārī, sabbaṃ vitathamidanti ñatvā {note:utvā (syā. pī. ka.)} loke;
::

::gathalast
So bhikkhu jahāti orapāraṃ, urago jiṇṇamivattacaṃ purāṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
Yo nāccasārī na paccasārī, sabbaṃ vitathamidanti vītalobho;
::

::gathalast
So bhikkhu jahāti orapāraṃ, urago jiṇṇamivattacaṃ purāṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
Yo {pb:M:0.0281} nāccasārī na paccasārī, sabbaṃ vitathamidanti vītarāgo;
::

::gathalast
So bhikkhu jahāti orapāraṃ, urago jiṇṇamivattacaṃ purāṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
Yo nāccasārī na paccasārī, sabbaṃ vitathamidanti vītadoso;
::

::gathalast
So bhikkhu jahāti orapāraṃ, urago jiṇṇamivattacaṃ purāṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
Yo {pb:V:0.0089} nāccasārī na paccasārī, sabbaṃ vitathamidanti vītamoho;
::

::gathalast
So {pb:T:0.0327} bhikkhu jahāti orapāraṃ, urago jiṇṇamivattacaṃ purāṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
Yassānusayā na santi keci, mūlā ca akusalā samūhatāse;
::

::gathalast
So bhikkhu jahāti orapāraṃ, urago jiṇṇamivattacaṃ purāṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
Yassa darathajā na santi keci, oraṃ āgamanāya paccayāse;
::

::gathalast
So bhikkhu jahāti orapāraṃ, urago jiṇṇamivattacaṃ purāṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
Yassa vanathajā na santi keci, vinibandhāya bhavāya hetukappā;
::

::gathalast
So bhikkhu jahāti orapāraṃ, urago jiṇṇamivattacaṃ purāṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
Yo {pb:P:0.0003} nīvaraṇe pahāya pañca, anigho tiṇṇakathaṃkatho visallo;
::

::gathalast
So bhikkhu jahāti orapāraṃ, urago jiṇṇamivattacaṃ purāṇaṃ.
::

::centre
Uragasuttaṃ paṭhamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

#### 2. Dhaniyasuttaṃ

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pakkodano {pb:M:0.0282}{pb:T:0.0328} duddhakhīrohamasmi, (iti dhaniyo gopo)
::

::gatha2
Anutīre mahiyā samānavāso;
::

::gathalast
Channā kuṭi āhito gini, atha ce patthayasī pavassa deva’’.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Akkodhano vigatakhilohamasmi {note:vigatakhīlohamasmi (sī. pī.)}, (iti bhagavā)
::

::gatha2
Anutīre mahiyekarattivāso;
::

::gathalast
Vivaṭā kuṭi nibbuto gini, atha ce patthayasī pavassa deva’’.
::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Andhakamakasā {pb:V:0.0090} na vijjare, (iti dhaniyo gopo)
::

::gatha2
Kacche rūḷhatiṇe caranti gāvo;
::

::gathalast
Vuṭṭhimpi saheyyumāgataṃ, atha ce patthayasī pavassa deva’’.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Baddhāsi bhisī susaṅkhatā, (iti bhagavā)
::

::gatha2
Tiṇṇo pāragato vineyya oghaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Attho bhisiyā na vijjati, atha ce patthayasī pavassa deva’’.
::

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gopī {pb:P:0.0004} mama assavā alolā, (iti dhaniyo gopo)
::

::gatha2
Dīgharattaṃ {note:dīgharatta (ka.)} saṃvāsiyā manāpā;
::

::gathalast
Tassā {pb:T:0.0329} na suṇāmi kiñci pāpaṃ, atha ce patthayasī pavassa deva’’.
::

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cittaṃ mama assavaṃ vimuttaṃ, (iti bhagavā)
::

::gatha2
Dīgharattaṃ paribhāvitaṃ sudantaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pāpaṃ pana me na vijjati, atha ce patthayasī pavassa deva’’.
::

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Attavetanabhatohamasmi{pb:M:0.0283}, (iti dhaniyo gopo)
::

::gatha2
Puttā ca me samāniyā arogā;
::

::gathalast
Tesaṃ na suṇāmi kiñci pāpaṃ, atha ce patthayasī pavassa deva’’.
::

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nāhaṃ bhatakosmi kassaci, (iti bhagavā)
::

::gatha2
Nibbiṭṭhena carāmi sabbaloke;
::

::gathalast
Attho bhatiyā na vijjati, atha ce patthayasī pavassa deva’’.
::

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atthi vasā atthi dhenupā, (iti dhaniyo gopo)
::

::gatha2
Godharaṇiyo paveṇiyopi atthi;
::

::gathalast
Usabhopi gavampatīdha atthi, atha ce patthayasī pavassa deva’’.
::

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Natthi {pb:V:0.0091} vasā natthi dhenupā, (iti bhagavā)
::

::gatha2
Godharaṇiyo paveṇiyopi natthi;
::

::gathalast
Usabhopi {pb:P:0.0005}{pb:T:0.0330} gavampatīdha natthi, atha ce patthayasī pavassa deva’’.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Khilā nikhātā asampavedhī, (iti dhaniyo gopo)
::

::gatha2
Dāmā muñjamayā navā susaṇṭhānā;
::

::gathalast
Na hi sakkhinti dhenupāpi chettuṃ {note:chetuṃ (ka.)}, atha ce patthayasī pavassa deva’’.
::

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Usabhoriva chetva {note:chetvā (syā. ka.)} bandhanāni, (iti bhagavā)
::

::gatha2
Nāgo pūtilataṃva dālayitvā {note:pūtilataṃ padālayitvā (syā. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Nāhaṃ punupessaṃ {note:puna upessaṃ (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.), punupeyya (ka.)} gabbhaseyyaṃ, atha ce patthayasī pavassa deva’’.
::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ninnañca thalañca pūrayanto, mahāmegho pavassi tāvadeva;
::

::gathalast
Sutvā devassa vassato, imamatthaṃ dhaniyo abhāsatha.
::

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Lābhā {pb:M:0.0284} vata no anappakā, ye mayaṃ bhagavantaṃ addasāma;
::

::gathalast
Saraṇaṃ taṃ upema cakkhuma, satthā no hohi tuvaṃ mahāmuni.
::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gopī ca ahañca assavā, brahmacariyaṃ {note:brahmacariya (ka.)} sugate carāmase;
::

::gathalast
Jātimaraṇassa {pb:T:0.0331} pāragū {note:pāragā (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)}, dukkhassantakarā bhavāmase’’.
::

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nandati {pb:P:0.0006} puttehi puttimā, (iti māro pāpimā)
::

::gatha2
Gomā {note:gomiko (sī. pī.), gopiko (syā. kaṃ.), gopiyo (ka.)} gohi tatheva nandati;
::

::gathalast
Upadhī hi narassa nandanā, na hi so nandati yo nirūpadhi’’.
::

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Socati puttehi puttimā, (iti bhagavā)
::

::gatha2
Gopiyo gohi tatheva socati;
::

::gathalast
Upadhī hi narassa socanā, na hi so socati yo nirūpadhī’’ti.
::

::centre
Dhaniyasuttaṃ dutiyaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

#### 3. Khaggavisāṇasuttaṃ

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
Sabbesu {pb:V:0.0092} bhūtesu nidhāya daṇḍaṃ, aviheṭhayaṃ aññatarampi tesaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na puttamiccheyya kuto sahāyaṃ, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
Saṃsaggajātassa {pb:M:0.0285} bhavanti snehā, snehanvayaṃ {pb:T:0.0332} dukkhamidaṃ pahoti;
::

::gathalast
Ādīnavaṃ snehajaṃ pekkhamāno, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1
Mitte suhajje anukampamāno, hāpeti atthaṃ paṭibaddhacitto;
::

::gathalast
Etaṃ bhayaṃ santhave {note:sandhave (ka.)} pekkhamāno, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
Vaṃso visālova yathā visatto, puttesu dāresu ca yā apekkhā;
::

::gathalast
Vaṃsakkaḷīrova {pb:P:0.0007} {note:vaṃsakaḷīrova (sī.), vaṃsākaḷīrova (syā. kaṃ. pī.), vaṃsekaḷīrova (niddesa)} asajjamāno, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
Migo araññamhi yathā abaddho {note:abandho (syā. kaṃ.)}, yenicchakaṃ gacchati gocarāya;
::

::gathalast
Viññū naro seritaṃ pekkhamāno, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
Āmantanā hoti sahāyamajjhe, vāse ṭhāne gamane cārikāya;
::

::gathalast
Anabhijjhitaṃ seritaṃ pekkhamāno, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1
Khiḍḍā {pb:T:0.0333} ratī hoti sahāyamajjhe, puttesu ca vipulaṃ hoti pemaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Piyavippayogaṃ vijigucchamāno, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
Cātuddiso {pb:M:0.0286} appaṭigho ca hoti, santussamāno itarītarena;
::

::gathalast
Parissayānaṃ sahitā achambhī, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1
Dussaṅgahā pabbajitāpi eke, atho gahaṭṭhā gharamāvasantā;
::

::gathalast
Appossukko paraputtesu hutvā, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
Oropayitvā {pb:V:0.0093} gihibyañjanāni {note:gihivyañjanāni (syā. kaṃ. pī.)}, sañchinnapatto {note:saṃsīnapatto (sī.)} yathā koviḷāro;
::

::gathalast
Chetvāna {pb:P:0.0008} vīro gihibandhanāni, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
Sace labhetha nipakaṃ sahāyaṃ, saddhiṃ caraṃ sādhuvihāridhīraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Abhibhuyya sabbāni parissayāni, careyya tenattamano satīmā.
::

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
No {pb:T:0.0334} ce labhetha nipakaṃ sahāyaṃ, saddhiṃ caraṃ sādhuvihāridhīraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Rājāva raṭṭhaṃ vijitaṃ pahāya, eko care mātaṅgaraññeva nāgo.
::

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
Addhā pasaṃsāma sahāyasampadaṃ, seṭṭhā samā sevitabbā sahāyā;
::

::gathalast
Ete aladdhā anavajjabhojī, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
Disvā suvaṇṇassa pabhassarāni, kammāraputtena suniṭṭhitāni;
::

::gathalast
Saṅghaṭṭamānāni duve bhujasmiṃ, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
Evaṃ {pb:M:0.0287} dutiyena {note:dutiyena (sabbattha)} sahā mamassa, vācābhilāpo abhisajjanā vā;
::

::gathalast
Etaṃ bhayaṃ āyatiṃ pekkhamāno, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
Kāmā hi citrā madhurā manoramā, virūparūpena mathenti cittaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ādīnavaṃ kāmaguṇesu disvā, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
Ītī {pb:T:0.0335} ca gaṇḍo ca upaddavo ca, rogo ca sallañca bhayañca metaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Etaṃ bhayaṃ kāmaguṇesu disvā, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
Sītañca {pb:P:0.0009} uṇhañca khudaṃ pipāsaṃ, vātātape ḍaṃsasarīsape {note:ḍaṃsasiriṃsape (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} ca;
::

::gathalast
Sabbānipetāni abhisambhavitvā, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
Nāgova yūthāni vivajjayitvā, sañjātakhandho padumī uḷāro;
::

::gathalast
Yathābhirantaṃ viharaṃ {note:vihare (sī. pī. niddesa)} araññe, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
Aṭṭhānataṃ {pb:V:0.0094} saṅgaṇikāratassa, yaṃ phassaye {note:phussaye (syā.)} sāmayikaṃ vimuttiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ādiccabandhussa vaco nisamma, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
Diṭṭhīvisūkāni upātivatto, patto niyāmaṃ paṭiladdhamaggo;
::

::gathalast
Uppannañāṇomhi anaññaneyyo, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
Nillolupo {pb:M:0.0288}{pb:T:0.0336} nikkuho nippipāso, nimmakkho niddhantakasāvamoho;
::

::gathalast
Nirāsayo {note:nirāsāso (ka.)} sabbaloke bhavitvā, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
Pāpaṃ sahāyaṃ parivajjayetha, anatthadassiṃ visame niviṭṭhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sayaṃ na seve pasutaṃ pamattaṃ, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
Bahussutaṃ {pb:P:0.0010} dhammadharaṃ bhajetha, mittaṃ uḷāraṃ paṭibhānavantaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Aññāya atthāni vineyya kaṅkhaṃ, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
Khiḍḍaṃ ratiṃ kāmasukhañca loke, analaṅkaritvā anapekkhamāno;
::

::gathalast
Vibhūsanaṭṭhānā virato saccavādī, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
Puttañca dāraṃ pitarañca mātaraṃ, dhanāni dhaññāni ca bandhavāni {note:bandhavāni ca (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Hitvāna kāmāni yathodhikāni, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
Saṅgo {pb:T:0.0337} eso parittamettha sokhyaṃ, appassādo dukkhamettha bhiyyo;
::

::gathalast
Gaḷo eso iti ñatvā mutīmā {note:matīmā (syā. ka.)}, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
Sandālayitvāna {note:padālayitvāna (ka.)} saṃyojanāni, jālaṃva bhetvā salilambucārī;
::

::gathalast
Aggīva daḍḍhaṃ anivattamāno, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
Okkhittacakkhū {pb:M:0.0289} na ca pādalolo, guttindriyo rakkhitamānasāno;
::

::gathalast
Anavassuto apariḍayhamāno, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
Ohārayitvā {pb:V:0.0095} gihibyañjanāni, sañchannapatto {note:sañchinnapatto (syā. pī.), pacchinnapatto (ka.)} yathā pārichatto;
::

::gathalast
Kāsāyavattho {pb:P:0.0011} abhinikkhamitvā, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
Rasesu gedhaṃ akaraṃ alolo, anaññaposī sapadānacārī;
::

::gathalast
Kule kule appaṭibaddhacitto {note:appaṭibandhacitto (ka.)}, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
Pahāya {pb:T:0.0338} pañcāvaraṇāni cetaso, upakkilese byapanujja sabbe;
::

::gathalast
Anissito chetva {note:chetvā (syā. pī. ka.)} sinehadosaṃ {note:snehadosaṃ (ka.)}, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
Vipiṭṭhikatvāna sukhaṃ dukhañca, pubbeva ca somanassadomanassaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Laddhānupekkhaṃ samathaṃ visuddhaṃ, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
Āraddhavīriyo paramatthapattiyā, alīnacitto akusītavutti;
::

::gathalast
Daḷhanikkamo thāmabalūpapanno, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
Paṭisallānaṃ jhānamariñcamāno, dhammesu niccaṃ anudhammacārī;
::

::gathalast
Ādīnavaṃ sammasitā bhavesu, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
Taṇhakkhayaṃ {pb:M:0.0290} patthayamappamatto, aneḷamūgo {note:anelamūgo (syā. pī. ka.)} sutavā satīmā;
::

::gathalast
Saṅkhātadhammo niyato padhānavā, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
Sīhova {pb:P:0.0012}{pb:T:0.0339} saddesu asantasanto, vātova jālamhi asajjamāno;
::

::gathalast
Padumaṃva toyena alippamāno {note:alimpamāno (sī. syā. ka.)}, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
Sīho yathā dāṭhabalī pasayha, rājā migānaṃ abhibhuyya cārī;
::

::gathalast
Sevetha pantāni senāsanāni, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
Mettaṃ upekkhaṃ karuṇaṃ vimuttiṃ, āsevamāno muditañca kāle;
::

::gathalast
Sabbena lokena avirujjhamāno, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
Rāgañca {pb:V:0.0096} dosañca pahāya mohaṃ, sandālayitvāna saṃyojanāni;
::

::gathalast
Asantasaṃ jīvitasaṅkhayamhi, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
Bhajanti sevanti ca kāraṇatthā, nikkāraṇā dullabhā ajja mittā;
::

::gathalast
Attaṭṭhapaññā asucī manussā, eko care khaggavisāṇakappo.
::

::centre
Khaggavisāṇasuttaṃ tatiyaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

#### 4. Kasibhāradvājasuttaṃ

Evaṃ {pb:M:0.0291}{pb:T:0.0340} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā magadhesu viharati dakkhiṇāgirismiṃ {pb:P:0.0013} {note:dakkhiṇagirismiṃ (ka.)} ekanāḷāyaṃ brāhmaṇagāme. Tena kho pana samayena kasibhāradvājassa brāhmaṇassa pañcamattāni naṅgalasatāni payuttāni honti vappakāle. Atha kho bhagavā pubbaṇhasamayaṃ nivāsetvā pattacīvaramādāya yena kasibhāradvājassa brāhmaṇassa kammanto tenupasaṅkami. Tena kho pana samayena kasibhāradvājassa brāhmaṇassa parivesanā vattati. Atha kho bhagavā yena parivesanā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhāsi.

Addasā kho kasibhāradvājo brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ piṇḍāya ṭhitaṃ. Disvāna bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘ahaṃ kho, samaṇa, kasāmi ca vapāmi ca; kasitvā ca vapitvā ca bhuñjāmi. Tvampi, samaṇa, kasassu ca vapassu ca; kasitvā ca vapitvā ca bhuñjassū’’ti.

‘‘Ahampi kho, brāhmaṇa, kasāmi ca vapāmi ca; kasitvā ca vapitvā ca bhuñjāmī’’ti. ‘‘Na kho pana mayaṃ {note:na kho pana samaṇa (syā.)} passāma bhoto gotamassa yugaṃ vā naṅgalaṃ vā phālaṃ vā pācanaṃ vā balibadde {note:balivadde (sī. pī.), balībadde (?)} vā. Atha ca pana bhavaṃ gotamo evamāha – ‘ahampi kho, brāhmaṇa, kasāmi ca vapāmi {pb:T:0.0341} ca; kasitvā ca vapitvā ca bhuñjāmī’’’ti.

Atha kho kasibhāradvājo brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kassako {pb:V:0.0097} paṭijānāsi, na ca passāma te kasiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kasiṃ no pucchito brūhi, yathā jānemu te kasiṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saddhā bījaṃ tapo vuṭṭhi, paññā me yuganaṅgalaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Hirī īsā mano yottaṃ, sati me phālapācanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kāyagutto {pb:P:0.0014} vacīgutto, āhāre udare yato;
::

::gathalast
Saccaṃ karomi niddānaṃ, soraccaṃ me pamocanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
79\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vīriyaṃ me dhuradhorayhaṃ, yogakkhemādhivāhanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Gacchati anivattantaṃ, yattha gantvā na socati.
::

::hangnum
80\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evamesā {pb:M:0.0292} kasī kaṭṭhā, sā hoti amatapphalā;
::

::gathalast
Etaṃ kasiṃ kasitvāna, sabbadukkhā pamuccatī’’ti.
::

Atha kho kasibhāradvājo brāhmaṇo mahatiyā kaṃsapātiyā pāyasaṃ {note:pāyāsaṃ (sabbattha)} vaḍḍhetvā bhagavato upanāmesi – ‘‘bhuñjatu bhavaṃ gotamo pāyasaṃ. Kassako bhavaṃ; yaṃ hi bhavaṃ gotamo amatapphalaṃ {note:amatapphalampi (saṃ. ni. 1.197)} kasiṃ kasatī’’ti.

::hangnum
81\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gāthābhigītaṃ me abhojaneyyaṃ, sampassataṃ brāhmaṇa nesa dhammo;
::

::gathalast
Gāthābhigītaṃ panudanti buddhā, dhamme satī brāhmaṇa vuttiresā.
::

::hangnum
82\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aññena {pb:T:0.0342} ca kevalinaṃ mahesiṃ, khīṇāsavaṃ kukkuccavūpasantaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Annena pānena upaṭṭhahassu, khettaṃ hi taṃ puññapekkhassa hotī’’ti.
::

‘‘Atha {pb:P:0.0015} kassa cāhaṃ, bho gotama, imaṃ pāyasaṃ dammī’’ti? ‘‘Na khvāhaṃ taṃ, brāhmaṇa, passāmi sadevake loke samārake sabrahmake sassamaṇabrāhmaṇiyā pajāya sadevamanussāya, yassa so pāyaso bhutto sammā pariṇāmaṃ gaccheyya, aññatra tathāgatassa vā tathāgatasāvakassa vā. Tena hi tvaṃ, brāhmaṇa, taṃ pāyasaṃ appaharite vā chaḍḍehi appāṇake vā udake opilāpehī’’ti.

Atha {pb:V:0.0098} kho kasibhāradvājo brāhmaṇo taṃ pāyasaṃ appāṇake udake opilāpesi. Atha kho so pāyaso udake pakkhitto cicciṭāyati ciṭiciṭāyati sandhūpāyati sampadhūpāyati {note:sandhūmāyati sampadhūmāyati (syā.)}. Seyyathāpi nāma phālo divasaṃ santatto {note:divasasantatto (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} udake pakkhitto cicciṭāyati ciṭiciṭāyati sandhūpāyati sampadhūpāyati; evameva so pāyaso udake pakkhitto cicciṭāyati ciṭiciṭāyati sandhūpāyati sampadhūpāyati.

Atha kho kasibhāradvājo brāhmaṇo saṃviggo lomahaṭṭhajāto yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavato pādesu sirasā nipatitvā {pb:M:0.0293} bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘abhikkantaṃ, bho gotama, abhikkantaṃ{pb:T:0.0343}, bho gotama! Seyyathāpi, bho gotama, nikkujjitaṃ vā ukkujjeyya, paṭicchannaṃ vā vivareyya, mūḷhassa vā maggaṃ ācikkheyya, andhakāre vā telapajjotaṃ dhāreyya, cakkhumanto rūpāni dakkhantīti {note:dakkhintīti (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)}; evamevaṃ bhotā gotamena anekapariyāyena dhammo pakāsito. Esāhaṃ bhavantaṃ gotamaṃ saraṇaṃ gacchāmi {pb:P:0.0016} dhammañca bhikkhusaṅghañca, labheyyāhaṃ bhoto gotamassa santike pabbajjaṃ, labheyyaṃ upasampada’’nti.

Alattha kho kasibhāradvājo brāhmaṇo bhagavato santike pabbajjaṃ, alattha upasampadaṃ. Acirūpasampanno kho panāyasmā bhāradvājo eko vūpakaṭṭho appamatto ātāpī pahitatto viharanto nacirasseva – yassatthāya kulaputtā sammadeva agārasmā anagāriyaṃ pabbajanti, tadanuttaraṃ – brahmacariyapariyosānaṃ diṭṭheva dhamme sayaṃ abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja vihāsi. ‘‘Khīṇā jāti, vusitaṃ brahmacariyaṃ, kataṃ karaṇīyaṃ, nāparaṃ itthattāyā’’ti abbhaññāsi. Aññataro ca {note:aññataro ca kho (sī. pī.), aññataro kho (syā. kaṃ. ka.)} panāyasmā bhāradvājo arahataṃ ahosīti.

::centre
Kasibhāradvājasuttaṃ catutthaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

#### 5. Cundasuttaṃ

::hangnum
83\.

::gatha1
‘‘Pucchāmi {pb:T:0.0344} muniṃ pahūtapaññaṃ, (iti cundo kammāraputto)
::

::gatha2
Buddhaṃ dhammassāmiṃ vītataṇhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dvipaduttamaṃ {note:dipaduttamaṃ (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} sārathīnaṃ pavaraṃ, kati loke samaṇā tadiṅgha brūhi’’.
::

::hangnum
84\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Caturo {pb:V:0.0099} samaṇā na pañcamatthi, (cundāti bhagavā)
::

::gatha2
Te {pb:P:0.0017} te āvikaromi sakkhipuṭṭho;
::

::gathalast
Maggajino maggadesako ca, magge jīvati yo ca maggadūsī’’.
::

::hangnum
85\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kaṃ {pb:M:0.0294} maggajinaṃ vadanti buddhā, (iti cundo kammāraputto)
::

::gatha2
Maggakkhāyī kathaṃ atulyo hoti;
::

::gathalast
Magge jīvati me brūhi puṭṭho, atha me āvikarohi maggadūsiṃ’’ {note:maggadūsī (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
86\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo tiṇṇakathaṃkatho visallo, nibbānābhirato anānugiddho;
::

::gathalast
Lokassa sadevakassa netā, tādiṃ maggajinaṃ vadanti buddhā.
::

::hangnum
87\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paramaṃ paramanti yodha ñatvā, akkhāti {pb:T:0.0345} vibhajate idheva dhammaṃ;
::

::

::hangnum
88\.

::gatha1
‘‘Yo dhammapade sudesite, magge jīvati saññato satīmā;
::

::gatha2
Anavajjapadāni sevamāno, tatiyaṃ bhikkhunamāhu maggajīviṃ.
::

::hangnum
89\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Chadanaṃ katvāna subbatānaṃ, pakkhandī kuladūsako pagabbho;
::

::gathalast
Māyāvī asaññato palāpo, patirūpena caraṃ sa maggadūsī.
::

::hangnum
90\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ete ca paṭivijjhi yo gahaṭṭho, sutavā ariyasāvako sapañño;
::

::gatha2
Sabbe {pb:P:0.0018} netādisāti {note:sabbe ne tādisāti (sī. syā. pī.)} ñatvā, iti disvā na hāpeti tassa saddhā;
::

::gathalast
Kathaṃ hi duṭṭhena asampaduṭṭhaṃ, suddhaṃ asuddhena samaṃ kareyyā’’ti.
::

::centre
Cundasuttaṃ pañcamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

#### 6. Parābhavasuttaṃ

Evaṃ {pb:M:0.0295}{pb:V:0.0100}{pb:T:0.0346} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. Atha kho aññatarā devatā abhikkantāya rattiyā abhikkantavaṇṇā kevalakappaṃ jetavanaṃ obhāsetvā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhāsi. Ekamantaṃ ṭhitā kho sā devatā bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::hangnum
91\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Parābhavantaṃ purisaṃ, mayaṃ pucchāma gotama {note:gotamaṃ (sī. syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Bhagavantaṃ {note:bhavantaṃ (syā. ka.)} puṭṭhumāgamma, kiṃ parābhavato mukhaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
92\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Suvijāno bhavaṃ hoti, suvijāno {note:duvijāno (syā. ka.)} parābhavo;
::

::gathalast
Dhammakāmo bhavaṃ hoti, dhammadessī parābhavo’’.
::

::hangnum
93\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Iti hetaṃ vijānāma, paṭhamo so parābhavo;
::

::gathalast
Dutiyaṃ bhagavā brūhi, kiṃ parābhavato mukhaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
94\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Asantassa piyā honti, sante na kurute piyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Asataṃ dhammaṃ roceti, taṃ parābhavato mukhaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
95\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Iti hetaṃ vijānāma, dutiyo so parābhavo;
::

::gathalast
Tatiyaṃ bhagavā brūhi, kiṃ parābhavato mukhaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
96\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Niddāsīlī {pb:P:0.0019} sabhāsīlī, anuṭṭhātā ca yo naro;
::

::gathalast
Alaso kodhapaññāṇo, taṃ parābhavato mukhaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
97\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Iti {pb:T:0.0347} hetaṃ vijānāma, tatiyo so parābhavo;
::

::gathalast
Catutthaṃ bhagavā brūhi, kiṃ parābhavato mukhaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
98\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo {pb:V:0.0101} mātaraṃ {note:yo mātaraṃ vā (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} pitaraṃ vā, jiṇṇakaṃ gatayobbanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pahu santo na bharati, taṃ parābhavato mukhaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
99\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Iti hetaṃ vijānāma, catuttho so parābhavo;
::

::gathalast
Pañcamaṃ bhagavā brūhi, kiṃ parābhavato mukhaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
100\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo brāhmaṇaṃ {note:yo brāhmaṇaṃ vā (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} samaṇaṃ vā, aññaṃ vāpi vanibbakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Musāvādena vañceti, taṃ parābhavato mukhaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
101\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Iti {pb:M:0.0296} hetaṃ vijānāma, pañcamo so parābhavo;
::

::gathalast
Chaṭṭhamaṃ bhagavā brūhi, kiṃ parābhavato mukhaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
102\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pahūtavitto puriso, sahirañño sabhojano;
::

::gathalast
Eko bhuñjati sādūni, taṃ parābhavato mukhaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
103\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Iti hetaṃ vijānāma, chaṭṭhamo so parābhavo;
::

::

::

::gathalast
Saññātiṃ atimaññeti, taṃ parābhavato mukhaṃ’’.
::

105\.

‘‘Iti hetaṃ vijānāma, sattamo so parābhavo;
::

::gathalast
Aṭṭhamaṃ bhagavā brūhi, kiṃ parābhavato mukhaṃ’’.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Laddhaṃ laddhaṃ vināseti, taṃ parābhavato mukhaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
107\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Iti {pb:P:0.0020}{pb:T:0.0348} hetaṃ vijānāma, aṭṭhamo so parābhavo;
::

::gathalast

::

::

::gathalast

::

::

::gathalast

::

::

::hangnum

::

::gatha1
‘‘Appabhogo mahātaṇho, khattiye jāyate kule;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum

::

::gatha1
‘‘Ete parābhave loke, paṇḍito samavekkhiya;
::

::gathalast
Ariyo dassanasampanno, sa lokaṃ bhajate siva’’nti.
::

::centre
Parābhavasuttaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

#### 7. Vasalasuttaṃ

Evaṃ {pb:V:0.0103}{pb:P:0.0021}{pb:T:0.0349} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. Atha kho bhagavā pubbaṇhasamayaṃ nivāsetvā pattacīvaramādāya sāvatthiṃ piṇḍāya pāvisi. Tena kho pana samayena aggikabhāradvājassa brāhmaṇassa nivesane aggi pajjalito hoti āhuti paggahitā. Atha kho bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ sapadānaṃ piṇḍāya caramāno yena aggikabhāradvājassa brāhmaṇassa nivesanaṃ tenupasaṅkami.

Addasā kho aggikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ dūratova āgacchantaṃ. Disvāna bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘tatreva {note:atreva (syā. ka.)}, muṇḍaka; tatreva, samaṇaka; tatreva, vasalaka tiṭṭhāhī’’ti.

Evaṃ vutte, bhagavā aggikabhāradvājaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘jānāsi pana tvaṃ, brāhmaṇa, vasalaṃ vā vasalakaraṇe vā dhamme’’ti? ‘‘Na khvāhaṃ, bho gotama, jānāmi vasalaṃ vā vasalakaraṇe vā dhamme; sādhu me bhavaṃ gotamo tathā dhammaṃ desetu, yathāhaṃ jāneyyaṃ vasalaṃ vā vasalakaraṇe vā dhamme’’ti. ‘‘Tena hi, brāhmaṇa, suṇāhi, sādhukaṃ manasi karohi; bhāsissāmī’’ti. ‘‘Evaṃ, bho’’ti kho aggikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo bhagavato paccassosi. Bhagavā etadavoca –

::hangnum
116\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kodhano {pb:M:0.0298} upanāhī ca, pāpamakkhī ca yo naro;
::

::gathalast
Vipannadiṭṭhi {pb:T:0.0350} māyāvī, taṃ jaññā vasalo iti.
::

::hangnum
117\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekajaṃ vā dvijaṃ {note:dijaṃ (pī.)} vāpi, yodha pāṇaṃ vihiṃsati;
::

::gathalast

::gathalast

#### 10. Āḷavakasuttaṃ

Evaṃ me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā āḷaviyaṃ viharati āḷavakassa yakkhassa bhavane. Atha kho āḷavako yakkho yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘nikkhama, samaṇā’’ti. ‘‘Sādhāvuso’’ti {pb:M:0.0306} bhagavā nikkhami. ‘‘Pavisa, samaṇā’’ti. ‘‘Sādhāvuso’’ti bhagavā pāvisi.

Dutiyampi kho…pe… tatiyampi kho āḷavako yakkho bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘nikkhama, samaṇā’’ti. ‘‘Sādhāvuso’’ti {pb:T:0.0360} bhagavā nikkhami. ‘‘Pavisa, samaṇā’’ti. ‘‘Sādhāvuso’’ti bhagavā pāvisi.

Catutthampi kho āḷavako yakkho bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘nikkhama, samaṇā’’ti. ‘‘Na khvāhaṃ taṃ{pb:P:0.0032}, āvuso, nikkhamissāmi. Yaṃ te karaṇīyaṃ, taṃ karohī’’ti.

‘‘Pañhaṃ {pb:V:0.0112} taṃ, samaṇa, pucchissāmi. Sace me na byākarissasi, cittaṃ vā te khipissāmi, hadayaṃ vā te phālessāmi, pādesu vā gahetvā pāragaṅgāya khipissāmī’’ti.

‘‘Na khvāhaṃ taṃ, āvuso, passāmi sadevake loke samārake sabrahmake sassamaṇabrāhmaṇiyā pajāya sadevamanussāya yo me cittaṃ vā khipeyya hadayaṃ vā phāleyya pādesu vā gahetvā pāragaṅgāya khipeyya. Api ca tvaṃ, āvuso, puccha yadākaṅkhasī’’ti. Atha kho āḷavako yakkho bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::hangnum
183\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃ sūdha vittaṃ purisassa seṭṭhaṃ, kiṃ su suciṇṇaṃ sukhamāvahāti;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃ su {note:kiṃ sū (sī.)} have sādutaraṃ rasānaṃ, kathaṃ jīviṃ jīvitamāhu seṭṭhaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
184\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saddhīdha vittaṃ purisassa seṭṭhaṃ, dhammo suciṇṇo sukhamāvahāti;
::

::gathalast
Saccaṃ have sādutaraṃ rasānaṃ, paññājīviṃ jīvitamāhu seṭṭhaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
185\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kathaṃ su tarati oghaṃ, kathaṃ su tarati aṇṇavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kathaṃ {pb:T:0.0361} su dukkhamacceti, kathaṃ su parisujjhati’’.
::

::hangnum
186\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saddhā {pb:P:0.0033} tarati oghaṃ, appamādena aṇṇavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vīriyena {note:viriyena (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} dukkhamacceti, paññāya parisujjhati’’.
::

::hangnum
187\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kathaṃ {pb:M:0.0307} su labhate paññaṃ, kathaṃ su vindate dhanaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Kathaṃ su kittiṃ pappoti, kathaṃ mittāni ganthati;
::

::gathalast
Asmā lokā paraṃ lokaṃ, kathaṃ pecca na socati’’.
::

::hangnum
188\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saddahāno arahataṃ, dhammaṃ nibbānapattiyā;
::

::gathalast
Sussūsaṃ {note:sussūsā (sī. pī.)} labhate paññaṃ, appamatto vicakkhaṇo.
::

::hangnum
189\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Patirūpakārī dhuravā, uṭṭhātā vindate dhanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Saccena kittiṃ pappoti, dadaṃ mittāni ganthati.
::

::hangnum
190\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yassete {pb:V:0.0113} caturo dhammā, saddhassa gharamesino;
::

::gathalast
Saccaṃ dhammo {note:damo (?)} dhiti cāgo, sa ve pecca na socati.
::

::hangnum
191\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Iṅgha aññepi pucchassu, puthū samaṇabrāhmaṇe;
::

::gathalast
Yadi saccā damā cāgā, khantyā bhiyyodha vijjati’’.
::

::hangnum
192\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kathaṃ nu dāni puccheyyaṃ, puthū samaṇabrāhmaṇe;
::

::gathalast
Yohaṃ {note:sohaṃ (sī. pī.)} ajja pajānāmi, yo attho samparāyiko.
::

::hangnum
193\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atthāya vata me buddho, vāsāyāḷavimāgamā;
::

::gathalast
Yohaṃ {note:aṭṭhinhārūhi saṃyutto (syā. ka.)} ajja pajānāmi, yattha dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
194\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So ahaṃ vicarissāmi, gāmā gāmaṃ purā puraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Namassamāno sambuddhaṃ, dhammassa ca sudhammata’’nti.
::

::centre
Āḷavakasuttaṃ dasamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

#### 11. Vijayasuttaṃ

::hangnum
195\.
::

::gatha1
Caraṃ {pb:P:0.0034}{pb:T:0.0362} vā yadi vā tiṭṭhaṃ, nisinno uda vā sayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Samiñjeti pasāreti, esā kāyassa iñjanā.
::

::hangnum
196\.
::

::gatha1
Aṭṭhinahārusaṃyutto, tacamaṃsāvalepano;
::

::gathalast
Chaviyā kāyo paṭicchanno, yathābhūtaṃ na dissati.
::

::hangnum
197\.
::

::gatha1
Antapūro {pb:M:0.0308} udarapūro, yakanapeḷassa {note:yakapeḷassa (sī. syā.)} vatthino;
::

::gathalast
Hadayassa papphāsassa, vakkassa pihakassa ca.
::

::hangnum
198\.
::

::gatha1
Siṅghāṇikāya {pb:V:0.0114} kheḷassa, sedassa ca medassa ca;
::

::gathalast
Lohitassa lasikāya, pittassa ca vasāya ca.
::

::hangnum
199\.
::

::gatha1
Athassa navahi sotehi, asucī savati sabbadā;
::

::gathalast
Akkhimhā akkhigūthako, kaṇṇamhā kaṇṇagūthako.
::

::hangnum
200\.
::

::gatha1
Siṅghāṇikā ca nāsato, mukhena vamatekadā;
::

::gathalast
Pittaṃ semhañca vamati, kāyamhā sedajallikā.
::

::hangnum
201\.
::

::gatha1
Athassa susiraṃ sīsaṃ, matthaluṅgassa pūritaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Subhato naṃ maññati, bālo avijjāya purakkhato.
::

::hangnum
202\.
::

::gatha1
Yadā ca so mato seti, uddhumāto vinīlako;
::

::gathalast
Apaviddho susānasmiṃ, anapekkhā honti ñātayo.
::

::hangnum
203\.
::

::gatha1
Khādanti naṃ suvānā {note:supāṇā (pī.)} ca, siṅgālā {note:sigālā (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} vakā kimī;
::

::gathalast
Kākā {pb:T:0.0363} gijjhā ca khādanti, ye caññe santi pāṇino.
::

::hangnum
204\.
::

::gatha1
Sutvāna {pb:P:0.0035} buddhavacanaṃ, bhikkhu paññāṇavā idha;
::

::gathalast
So kho naṃ parijānāti, yathābhūtañhi passati.
::

::hangnum
205\.
::

::gatha1
Yathā idaṃ tathā etaṃ, yathā etaṃ tathā idaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ajjhattañca bahiddhā ca, kāye chandaṃ virājaye.
::

::hangnum
206\.
::

::gatha1
Chandarāgaviratto so, bhikkhu paññāṇavā idha;
::

::gathalast
Ajjhagā amataṃ santiṃ, nibbānaṃ padamaccutaṃ.
::

::hangnum
207\.
::

::gatha1
Dvipādakoyaṃ {note:dipādakoyaṃ (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} asuci, duggandho parihārati {note:parihīrati (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Nānākuṇapaparipūro, vissavanto tato tato.
::

::hangnum
208\.
::

::gatha1
Etādisena {pb:V:0.0115} kāyena, yo maññe uṇṇametave {note:unnametave (?)};
::

::gathalast
Paraṃ vā avajāneyya, kimaññatra adassanāti.
::

::centre
Vijayasuttaṃ ekādasamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

#### 12. Munisuttaṃ

::hangnum
209\.
::

::gatha1
Santhavāto {pb:M:0.0309} {note:sandhavato (ka.)} bhayaṃ jātaṃ, niketā jāyate rajo;
::

::gathalast
Aniketamasanthavaṃ, etaṃ ve munidassanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
210\.
::

::gatha1
Yo jātamucchijja na ropayeyya, jāyantamassa nānuppavecche;
::

::gathalast
Tamāhu ekaṃ muninaṃ carantaṃ, addakkhi {pb:T:0.0364} so santipadaṃ mahesi.
::

::hangnum
211\.
::

::gatha1
Saṅkhāya {pb:P:0.0036} vatthūni pamāya {note:pahāya (ka. sī. ka.), samāya (ka.) pa + mī + tvā = pamāya, yathā nissāyātipadaṃ} bījaṃ, sinehamassa nānuppavecche;
::

::gathalast
Sa ve munī jātikhayantadassī, takkaṃ pahāya na upeti saṅkhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
212\.
::

::gatha1
Aññāya sabbāni nivesanāni, anikāmayaṃ aññatarampi tesaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sa ve munī vītagedho agiddho, nāyūhatī pāragato hi hoti.
::

::hangnum
213\.
::

::gatha1
Sabbābhibhuṃ sabbaviduṃ sumedhaṃ, sabbesu dhammesu anūpalittaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbañjahaṃ taṇhakkhaye vimuttaṃ, taṃ vāpi dhīrā muni {note:muniṃ (sī. pī.)} vedayanti.
::

::hangnum
214\.
::

::gatha1
Paññābalaṃ sīlavatūpapannaṃ, samāhitaṃ jhānarataṃ satīmaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Saṅgā pamuttaṃ akhilaṃ anāsavaṃ, taṃ vāpi dhīrā muni vedayanti.
::

::hangnum
215\.
::

::gatha1
Ekaṃ {pb:M:0.0310} carantaṃ munimappamattaṃ, nindāpasaṃsāsu avedhamānaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Sīhaṃva saddesu asantasantaṃ, vātaṃva {pb:T:0.0365} jālamhi asajjamānaṃ;
::

::gatha3
Padmaṃva {pb:V:0.0116} {note:padumaṃva (sī. syā. pī.)} toyena alippamānaṃ {note:alimpamānaṃ (syā. ka.)}, netāramaññesamanaññaneyyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ vāpi dhīrā muni vedayanti.
::

::hangnum
216\.
::

::gatha1
Yo {pb:P:0.0037} ogahaṇe thambhorivābhijāyati, yasmiṃ pare vācāpariyantaṃ {note:vācaṃ pariyantaṃ (ka.)} vadanti;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ vītarāgaṃ susamāhitindriyaṃ, taṃ vāpi dhīrā muni vedayanti.
::

::hangnum
217\.
::

::gatha1
Yo ve ṭhitatto tasaraṃva ujju, jigucchati kammehi pāpakehi;
::

::gathalast
Vīmaṃsamāno visamaṃ samañca, taṃ vāpi dhīrā muni vedayanti.
::

::hangnum
218\.
::

::gatha1
Yo saññatatto na karoti pāpaṃ, daharo majjhimo ca muni {note:daharo ca majjho ca munī (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} yatatto;
::

::gathalast
Arosaneyyo na so roseti kañci {note:na roseti (syā.)}, taṃ vāpi dhīrā muni vedayanti.
::

::hangnum
219\.
::

::gatha1
Yadaggato majjhato sesato vā, piṇḍaṃ labhetha paradattūpajīvī;
::

::gathalast
Nālaṃ thutuṃ nopi nipaccavādī, taṃ vāpi dhīrā muni vedayanti.
::

::hangnum
220\.
::

::gatha1
Muniṃ {pb:T:0.0366} carantaṃ virataṃ methunasmā, yo yobbane nopanibajjhate kvaci;
::

::gathalast
Madappamādā virataṃ vippamuttaṃ, taṃ vāpi dhīrā muni vedayanti.
::

::hangnum
221\.
::

::gatha1
Aññāya {pb:M:0.0311} lokaṃ paramatthadassiṃ, oghaṃ samuddaṃ atitariya tādiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ {pb:P:0.0038} chinnaganthaṃ asitaṃ anāsavaṃ, taṃ vāpi dhīrā muni vedayanti.
::

::hangnum
222\.
::

::gatha1
Asamā ubho dūravihāravuttino, gihī {note:gihi (ka.)} dāraposī amamo ca subbato;
::

::gathalast
Parapāṇarodhāya gihī asaññato, niccaṃ munī rakkhati pāṇine {note:pāṇino (sī.)} yato.
::

::hangnum
223\.
::

::gatha1
Sikhī yathā nīlagīvo {note:nīlagivo (syā.)} vihaṅgamo, haṃsassa nopeti javaṃ kudācanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ gihī nānukaroti bhikkhuno, munino vivittassa vanamhi jhāyatoti.
::

::centre
Munisuttaṃ dvādasamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

::centre
Uragavaggo paṭhamo niṭṭhito.
::

Tassuddānaṃ {pb:V:0.0117} –

::gatha1
Urago dhaniyo ceva, visāṇañca tathā kasi;
::

::gathalast
Cundo parābhavo {pb:T:0.0367} ceva, vasalo mettabhāvanā.
::

::gatha1
Sātāgiro āḷavako, vijayo ca tathā muni;
::

::gathalast
Dvādasetāni suttāni, uragavaggoti vuccatīti.
::

### 2. Cūḷavaggo

#### 1. Ratanasuttaṃ

::hangnum
224\.
::

::gatha1
Yānīdha {pb:M:0.0312}{pb:V:0.0118}{pb:P:0.0039} bhūtāni samāgatāni, bhummāni {note:bhūmāni (ka.)} vā yāni va antalikkhe;
::

::gathalast
Sabbeva bhūtā sumanā bhavantu, athopi sakkacca suṇantu bhāsitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
225\.
::

::gatha1
Tasmā hi bhūtā nisāmetha sabbe, mettaṃ karotha mānusiyā pajāya;
::

::gathalast
Divā ca ratto ca haranti ye baliṃ, tasmā hi ne rakkhatha appamattā.
::

::hangnum
226\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ kiñci vittaṃ idha vā huraṃ vā, saggesu vā yaṃ ratanaṃ paṇītaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Na no samaṃ atthi tathāgatena, idampi buddhe ratanaṃ paṇītaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Etena saccena suvatthi hotu.
::

::hangnum
227\.
::

::gatha1
Khayaṃ virāgaṃ amataṃ paṇītaṃ, yadajjhagā {pb:T:0.0368} sakyamunī samāhito;
::

::gatha2
Na tena dhammena samatthi kiñci, idampi dhamme ratanaṃ paṇītaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Etena saccena suvatthi hotu.
::

::hangnum
228\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ buddhaseṭṭho parivaṇṇayī suciṃ, samādhimānantarikaññamāhu;
::

::gatha2
Samādhinā {pb:P:0.0040} tena samo na vijjati, idampi dhamme ratanaṃ paṇītaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Etena saccena suvatthi hotu.
::

::hangnum
229\.
::

::gatha1
Ye {pb:M:0.0313} puggalā aṭṭha sataṃ pasatthā, cattāri etāni yugāni honti;
::

::gatha2
Te dakkhiṇeyyā sugatassa sāvakā, etesu dinnāni mahapphalāni;
::

::gathalast
Idampi saṅghe ratanaṃ paṇītaṃ, etena {pb:T:0.0369} saccena suvatthi hotu.
::

::hangnum
230\.
::

::gatha1
Ye {pb:V:0.0119} suppayuttā manasā daḷhena, nikkāmino gotamasāsanamhi;
::

::gatha2
Te pattipattā amataṃ vigayha, laddhā mudhā nibbutiṃ {note:nibbuti (ka.)} bhuñjamānā;
::

::gathalast
Idampi saṅghe ratanaṃ paṇītaṃ, etena saccena suvatthi hotu.
::

::hangnum
231\.
::

::gatha1
Yathindakhīlo pathavissito {note:padavissito (ka. sī.), paṭhaviṃ sito (ka. sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} siyā, catubbhi vātehi asampakampiyo;
::

::gatha2
Tathūpamaṃ sappurisaṃ vadāmi, yo ariyasaccāni avecca passati;
::

::gathalast
Idampi saṅghe ratanaṃ paṇītaṃ, etena saccena suvatthi hotu.
::

::hangnum
232\.
::

::gatha1
Ye ariyasaccāni vibhāvayanti, gambhīrapaññena sudesitāni;
::

::gatha2
Kiñcāpi te honti bhusaṃ pamattā, na te bhavaṃ aṭṭhamamādiyanti;
::

::gathalast
Idampi saṅghe ratanaṃ paṇītaṃ, etena {pb:T:0.0370} saccena suvatthi hotu.
::

::hangnum
233\.
::

::gatha1
Sahāvassa dassanasampadāya {note:sahāvasaddassanasampadāya (ka.)}, tayassu dhammā jahitā bhavanti;
::

::gathalast
Sakkāyadiṭṭhi {pb:P:0.0041} vicikicchitañca, sīlabbataṃ vāpi yadatthi kiñci.

::hangnum
234\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gatha2
Abhabba {note:abhabbo (bahūsu)} so tassa paṭicchadāya {note:paṭicchādāya (sī.)}, abhabbatā diṭṭhapadassa vuttā;

::

::gatha2

::gatha2
Te khīṇabījā avirūḷhichandā, nibbanti {pb:P:0.0042}{pb:T:0.0371} dhīrā yathāyaṃ {note:yathayaṃ (ka.)} padīpo;

::gathalast

#### 2. Āmagandhasuttaṃ

::hangnum
242\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sāmākaciṅgūlakacīnakāni {pb:T:0.0372} ca, pattapphalaṃ mūlaphalaṃ gavipphalaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dhammena laddhaṃ satamasnamānā {note:satamasamānā (sī. pī.), satamassamānā (syā. kaṃ.)}, na kāmakāmā alikaṃ bhaṇanti.
::

::hangnum
243\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yadasnamāno sukataṃ suniṭṭhitaṃ, parehi dinnaṃ payataṃ paṇītaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sālīnamannaṃ {pb:P:0.0043} paribhuñjamāno, so bhuñjasī kassapa āmagandhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
244\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:M:0.0316} āmagandho mama kappatīti, icceva tvaṃ bhāsasi brahmabandhu;
::

::gatha2
Sālīnamannaṃ paribhuñjamāno, sakuntamaṃsehi susaṅkhatehi;
::

::gathalast
Pucchāmi taṃ kassapa etamatthaṃ, kathaṃ pakāro tava āmagandho’’.
::

::hangnum
245\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pāṇātipāto {pb:V:0.0121} vadhachedabandhanaṃ, theyyaṃ musāvādo nikativañcanāni ca;
::

::gathalast
Ajjhenakuttaṃ {note:ajjhena kujjaṃ (sī. pī.)} paradārasevanā, esāmagandho na hi maṃsabhojanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
246\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye {pb:T:0.0373} idha kāmesu asaññatā janā, rasesu giddhā asucibhāvamassitā {note:asucīkamissitā (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Natthikadiṭṭhī visamā durannayā, esāmagandho na hi maṃsabhojanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
247\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye lūkhasā dāruṇā piṭṭhimaṃsikā {note:ye lūkharasā dāruṇā parapiṭṭhimaṃsikā (ka.)}, mittadduno nikkaruṇātimānino;
::

::gathalast
Adānasīlā na ca denti kassaci, esāmagandho na hi maṃsabhojanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
248\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kodho {pb:P:0.0044} mado thambho paccupaṭṭhāpanā {note:paccuṭṭhāpanā ca (sī. syā.), paccuṭṭhāpanā (pī.)}, māyā usūyā bhassasamussayo ca;
::

::gathalast
Mānātimāno ca asabbhi santhavo, esāmagandho na hi maṃsabhojanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
249\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye pāpasīlā iṇaghātasūcakā, vohārakūṭā idha pāṭirūpikā {note:pātirūpikā (?)};
::

::gathalast
Narādhamā yedha karonti kibbisaṃ, esāmagandho na hi maṃsabhojanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
250\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye {pb:M:0.0317} idha pāṇesu asaññatā janā, paresamādāya vihesamuyyutā;
::

::gathalast
Dussīlaluddā pharusā anādarā, esāmagandho {pb:T:0.0374} na hi maṃsabhojanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
251\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Etesu giddhā viruddhātipātino, niccuyyutā pecca tamaṃ vajanti ye;
::

::gathalast
Patanti sattā nirayaṃ avaṃsirā, esāmagandho na hi maṃsabhojanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
252\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na macchamaṃsānamanāsakattaṃ {note:na macchamaṃsaṃ na anāsakattaṃ (sī. aṭṭha mūlapāṭho), na maṃcchamaṃsānānāsakattaṃ (syā. ka.)}, na naggiyaṃ na muṇḍiyaṃ jaṭājallaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Kharājināni nāggihuttassupasevanā, ye vāpi loke amarā bahū tapā;
::

::gathalast
Mantāhutī yaññamutūpasevanā, sodhenti maccaṃ avitiṇṇakaṅkhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
253\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo tesu {pb:P:0.0045} {note:sotesu (sī. pī.)} gutto viditindriyo care, dhamme ṭhito ajjavamaddave rato;
::

::gathalast
Saṅgātigo sabbadukkhappahīno, na lippati {note:na limpati (syā. kaṃ ka.)} diṭṭhasutesu dhīro’’.
::

::hangnum
254\.
::

::gatha1
Iccetamatthaṃ bhagavā punappunaṃ, akkhāsi naṃ {note:taṃ (sī. pī.)} vedayi mantapāragū;
::

::gathalast
Citrāhi gāthāhi munī pakāsayi, nirāmagandho asito durannayo.
::

::hangnum
255\.
::

::gatha1
Sutvāna {pb:V:0.0122} buddhassa subhāsitaṃ padaṃ, nirāmagandhaṃ {pb:T:0.0375} sabbadukkhappanūdanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nīcamano vandi tathāgatassa, tattheva pabbajjamarocayitthāti.
::

::centre
Āmagandhasuttaṃ dutiyaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

::hangnum

#### 4. Maṅgalasuttaṃ

Evaṃ {pb:V:0.0123} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. Atha kho aññatarā devatā abhikkantāya rattiyā abhikkantavaṇṇā kevalakappaṃ jetavanaṃ obhāsetvā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhāsi. Ekamantaṃ ṭhitā kho sā devatā bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::hangnum
261\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bahū devā manussā ca, maṅgalāni acintayuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ākaṅkhamānā sotthānaṃ, brūhi maṅgalamuttamaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
262\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Asevanā {pb:M:0.0319} ca bālānaṃ, paṇḍitānañca sevanā;
::

::gathalast
Pūjā ca pūjaneyyānaṃ {note:pūjanīyānaṃ (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)}, etaṃ maṅgalamuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
263\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Patirūpadesavāso ca, pubbe ca katapuññatā;
::

::gathalast
Attasammāpaṇidhi {note:attasammāpaṇīdhī (katthaci)} ca, etaṃ maṅgalamuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
264\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bāhusaccañca {pb:P:0.0047} sippañca, vinayo ca susikkhito;
::

::gathalast
Subhāsitā ca yā vācā, etaṃ maṅgalamuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
265\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mātāpitu upaṭṭhānaṃ, puttadārassa saṅgaho;
::

::gathalast
Anākulā {pb:T:0.0377} ca kammantā, etaṃ maṅgalamuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
266\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dānañca dhammacariyā ca, ñātakānañca saṅgaho;
::

::gathalast
Anavajjāni kammāni, etaṃ maṅgalamuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
267\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āratī viratī pāpā, majjapānā ca saṃyamo;
::

::gathalast
Appamādo ca dhammesu, etaṃ maṅgalamuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
268\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gāravo {pb:V:0.0124} ca nivāto ca, santuṭṭhi ca kataññutā;
::

::gathalast
Kālena dhammassavanaṃ {note:dhammasavaṇaṃ (katthaci), dhammasavanaṃ (sī. ka.)}, etaṃ maṅgalamuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
269\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Khantī ca sovacassatā, samaṇānañca dassanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kālena dhammasākacchā, etaṃ maṅgalamuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
270\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tapo ca brahmacariyañca, ariyasaccāna dassanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nibbānasacchikiriyā ca, etaṃ maṅgalamuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
271\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Phuṭṭhassa lokadhammehi, cittaṃ yassa na kampati;
::

::gathalast
Asokaṃ virajaṃ khemaṃ, etaṃ maṅgalamuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
272\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Etādisāni katvāna, sabbatthamaparājitā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbattha sotthiṃ gacchanti, taṃ tesaṃ maṅgalamuttama’’nti.
::

::centre
Maṅgalasuttaṃ catutthaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

#### 5. Sūcilomasuttaṃ

Evaṃ {pb:M:0.0320}{pb:T:0.0378} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā gayāyaṃ viharati ṭaṅkitamañce sūcilomassa yakkhassa bhavane. Tena kho pana samayena {pb:P:0.0048} kharo ca yakkho sūcilomo ca yakkho bhagavato avidūre atikkamanti. Atha kho kharo yakkho sūcilomaṃ yakkhaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘eso samaṇo’’ti. ‘‘Neso samaṇo, samaṇako eso. Yāvāhaṃ jānāmi {note:yāva jānāmi (sī. pī.)} yadi vā so samaṇo {note:yadi vā samaṇo (syā.)}, yadi vā so samaṇako’’ti {note:yadi vā samaṇakoti (sī. syā. pī.)}.

Atha kho sūcilomo yakkho yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavato kāyaṃ upanāmesi. Atha kho bhagavā kāyaṃ apanāmesi. Atha kho sūcilomo yakkho bhagavantaṃ etadavoca {pb:V:0.0125} – ‘‘bhāyasi maṃ, samaṇā’’ti? ‘‘Na khvāhaṃ taṃ, āvuso, bhāyāmi; api ca te sapphasso pāpako’’ti.

‘‘Pañhaṃ taṃ, samaṇa, pucchissāmi. Sace me na byākarissasi, cittaṃ vā te khipissāmi, hadayaṃ vā te phālessāmi, pādesu vā gahetvā pāragaṅgāya khipissāmī’’ti.

‘‘Na khvāhaṃ taṃ, āvuso, passāmi sadevake loke samārake sabrahmake sassamaṇabrāhmaṇiyā pajāya sadevamanussāya yo me cittaṃ vā khipeyya hadayaṃ vā phāleyya pādesu vā gahetvā pāragaṅgāya khipeyya. Api ca tvaṃ, āvuso, puccha yadākaṅkhasī’’ti. Atha kho sūcilomo yakkho bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::hangnum
273\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rāgo ca doso ca kutonidānā, aratī {pb:T:0.0379} ratī lomahaṃso kutojā;
::

::gathalast
Kuto samuṭṭhāya manovitakkā, kumārakā dhaṅkamivossajanti’’.
::

::hangnum
274\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rāgo ca doso ca itonidānā, aratī ratī lomahaṃso itojā;
::

::gathalast
Ito samuṭṭhāya manovitakkā, kumārakā dhaṅkamivossajanti.
::

::hangnum
274\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Snehajā {pb:M:0.0321}{pb:P:0.0049} attasambhūtā, nigrodhasseva khandhajā;
::

::gathalast
Puthū visattā kāmesu, māluvāva vitatāvane.
::

::hangnum
275\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye naṃ pajānanti yatonidānaṃ, te naṃ vinodenti suṇohi yakkha;
::

::gathalast
Te duttaraṃ oghamimaṃ taranti, atiṇṇapubbaṃ apunabbhavāyā’’ti.
::

::centre
Sūcilomasuttaṃ pañcamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

#### 6. Dhammacariyasuttaṃ

::hangnum
276\.
::

::gatha1
Dhammacariyaṃ {pb:V:0.0126} brahmacariyaṃ, etadāhu vasuttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pabbajitopi ce hoti, agārā anagāriyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
277\.
::

::gatha1
So ce mukharajātiko, vihesābhirato mago;
::

::gathalast
Jīvitaṃ {pb:T:0.0380} tassa pāpiyo, rajaṃ vaḍḍheti attano.
::

::hangnum
278\.
::

::gatha1
Kalahābhirato bhikkhu, mohadhammena āvuto;
::

::gathalast
Akkhātampi na jānāti, dhammaṃ buddhena desitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
279\.
::

::gatha1
Vihesaṃ bhāvitattānaṃ, avijjāya purakkhato;
::

::gathalast
Saṃkilesaṃ na jānāti, maggaṃ nirayagāminaṃ.
::

::hangnum
280\.
::

::gatha1
Vinipātaṃ samāpanno, gabbhā gabbhaṃ tamā tamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sa ve tādisako bhikkhu, pecca dukkhaṃ nigacchati.
::

::hangnum
281\.
::

::gatha1
Gūthakūpo yathā assa, sampuṇṇo gaṇavassiko;
::

::gathalast
Yo ca evarūpo assa, dubbisodho hi sāṅgaṇo.
::

::hangnum
282\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ evarūpaṃ jānātha, bhikkhavo gehanissitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pāpicchaṃ pāpasaṅkappaṃ, pāpaācāragocaraṃ.
::

::hangnum
283\.
::

::gatha1
Sabbe {pb:M:0.0322}{pb:P:0.0050} samaggā hutvāna, abhinibbajjiyātha {note:abhinibbajjayātha (sī. pī. a. ni. 8.10)} naṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kāraṇḍavaṃ {note:kāraṇḍaṃ va (syā. ka.) a. ni. 8.10} niddhamatha, kasambuṃ apakassatha {note:avakassatha (sī. syā. ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
284\.
::

::gatha1
Tato palāpe {note:palāse (ka.)} vāhetha, assamaṇe samaṇamānine;
::

::gathalast
Niddhamitvāna pāpicche, pāpaācāragocare.
::

::hangnum
285\.
::

::gatha1
Suddhā {pb:V:0.0127} suddhehi saṃvāsaṃ, kappayavho patissatā;
::

::gathalast
Tato samaggā nipakā, dukkhassantaṃ karissathāti.
::

::centre
Dhammacariyasuttaṃ {note:kapilasuttaṃ (aṭṭha.)} chaṭṭhaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

#### 7. Brāhmaṇadhammikasuttaṃ

Evaṃ {pb:T:0.0381} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. Atha kho sambahulā kosalakā brāhmaṇamahāsālā jiṇṇā vuḍḍhā mahallakā addhagatā vayoanuppattā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkamiṃsu; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavatā saddhiṃ sammodiṃsu. Sammodanīyaṃ kathaṃ sāraṇīyaṃ vītisāretvā ekamantaṃ nisīdiṃsu. Ekamantaṃ nisinnā kho te brāhmaṇamahāsālā bhagavantaṃ etadavocuṃ – ‘‘sandissanti nu kho, bho gotama, etarahi brāhmaṇā porāṇānaṃ brāhmaṇānaṃ brāhmaṇadhamme’’ti? ‘‘Na kho, brāhmaṇā, sandissanti etarahi brāhmaṇā porāṇānaṃ brāhmaṇānaṃ brāhmaṇadhamme’’ti. ‘‘Sādhu no bhavaṃ gotamo porāṇānaṃ brāhmaṇānaṃ brāhmaṇadhammaṃ bhāsatu, sace bhoto gotamassa agarū’’ti. ‘‘Tena hi, brāhmaṇā, suṇātha, sādhukaṃ manasi karotha, bhāsissāmī’’ti. ‘‘Evaṃ, bho’’ti kho te brāhmaṇamahāsālā bhagavato paccassosuṃ. Bhagavā etadavoca –

::hangnum
286\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Isayo pubbakā āsuṃ, saññatattā tapassino;
::

::gathalast
Pañca kāmaguṇe hitvā, attadatthamacārisuṃ.
::

::hangnum
287\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:P:0.0051} pasū brāhmaṇānāsuṃ, na hiraññaṃ na dhāniyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sajjhāyadhanadhaññāsuṃ, brahmaṃ nidhimapālayuṃ.
::

::hangnum
288\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ {pb:M:0.0323}{pb:T:0.0382} nesaṃ pakataṃ āsi, dvārabhattaṃ upaṭṭhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Saddhāpakatamesānaṃ, dātave tadamaññisuṃ.
::

::hangnum
289\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nānārattehi {pb:V:0.0128} vatthehi, sayanehāvasathehi ca;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
290\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

291\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
294\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Brahmacariyañca sīlañca, ajjavaṃ maddavaṃ tapaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Soraccaṃ avihiṃsañca, khantiñcāpi avaṇṇayuṃ.
::

::hangnum
295\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo {pb:P:0.0052} nesaṃ paramo āsi, brahmā daḷhaparakkamo;

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum

::gatha1

::

::gatha2

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
309\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yathā āpo ca pathavī ca, hiraññaṃ dhanadhāniyaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Evaṃ gāvo manussānaṃ, parikkhāro so hi pāṇinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yajassu bahu te vittaṃ, yajassu bahu te dhanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
310\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato ca rājā saññatto, brāhmaṇehi rathesabho;
::

::gathalast
Nekā satasahassiyo, gāvo yaññe aghātayi.
::

::hangnum
311\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:M:0.0325} pādā na visāṇena, nāssu hiṃsanti kenaci;
::

::gatha2
Gāvo eḷakasamānā, soratā kumbhadūhanā;
::

::gathalast
Tā visāṇe gahetvāna, rājā satthena ghātayi.
::

::hangnum
312\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato {pb:P:0.0054} devā pitaro ca {note:tato ca devā pitaro (sī. syā.)}, indo asurarakkhasā;
::

::gathalast
Adhammo iti pakkanduṃ, yaṃ satthaṃ nipatī gave.
::

::hangnum
313\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tayo rogā pure āsuṃ, icchā anasanaṃ jarā;
::

::gathalast
Pasūnañca samārambhā, aṭṭhānavutimāgamuṃ.
::

::hangnum
314\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Eso {pb:T:0.0385} adhammo daṇḍānaṃ, okkanto purāṇo ahu;
::

::gathalast
Adūsikāyo haññanti, dhammā dhaṃsanti {note:dhaṃsenti (sī. pī.)} yājakā.
::

::hangnum

::gatha1
‘‘Evameso aṇudhammo, porāṇo viññugarahito;
::

::gathalast
Yattha edisakaṃ passati, yājakaṃ garahatī {note:garahī (ka.)} jano.
::

::hangnum
316\.
::

::gatha1

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
317\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Khattiyā {pb:V:0.0131} brahmabandhū ca, ye caññe gottarakkhitā;
::

::gathalast
Jātivādaṃ niraṃkatvā {note:nirākatvā (?) yathā anirākatajjhānoti}, kāmānaṃ vasamanvagu’’nti.
::

Evaṃ vutte, te brāhmaṇamahāsālā bhagavantaṃ etadavocuṃ – ‘‘abhikkantaṃ, bho gotama…pe. {pb:P:0.0055}… upāsake no bhavaṃ gotamo dhāretu ajjatagge pāṇupete saraṇaṃ gate’’ti.

::centre
Brāhmaṇadhammikasuttaṃ sattamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

#### 8. Nāvāsuttaṃ

::hangnum
318\.
::

::gatha1
Yasmā {pb:T:0.0386} hi dhammaṃ puriso vijaññā, indaṃva naṃ devatā pūjayeyya;
::

::gathalast
So pūjito tasmi pasannacitto, bahussuto pātukaroti dhammaṃ.
::

::hangnum
319\.
::

::gatha1
Tadaṭṭhikatvāna {pb:M:0.0326} nisamma dhīro, dhammānudhammaṃ paṭipajjamāno;
::

::gathalast
Viññū vibhāvī nipuṇo ca hoti, yo tādisaṃ bhajati appamatto.
::

::hangnum
320\.
::

::gatha1
Khuddañca bālaṃ upasevamāno, anāgatatthañca usūyakañca;
::

::gathalast
Idheva dhammaṃ avibhāvayitvā, avitiṇṇakaṅkho maraṇaṃ upeti.
::

::hangnum
321\.
::

::gatha1
Yathā naro āpagamotaritvā, mahodakaṃ salilaṃ sīghasotaṃ;
::

::gathalast
So vuyhamāno anusotagāmī, kiṃ so pare sakkhati tārayetuṃ.
::

::hangnum
322\.
::

::gatha1
Tatheva dhammaṃ avibhāvayitvā, bahussutānaṃ anisāmayatthaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sayaṃ ajānaṃ avitiṇṇakaṅkho, kiṃ {pb:T:0.0387} so pare sakkhati nijjhapetuṃ.
::

::hangnum
323\.
::

::gatha1
Yathāpi {pb:P:0.0056} nāvaṃ daḷhamāruhitvā, phiyena {note:piyena (sī. syā.)} rittena samaṅgibhūto;
::

::gathalast
So tāraye tattha bahūpi aññe, tatrūpayaññū kusalo mutīmā {note:matīmā (syā. ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
324\.
::

::gatha1
Evampi {pb:V:0.0132} yo vedagu bhāvitatto, bahussuto hoti avedhadhammo;
::

::gathalast
So kho pare nijjhapaye pajānaṃ, sotāvadhānūpanisūpapanne.
::

::hangnum
325\.
::

::gatha1
Tasmā have sappurisaṃ bhajetha, medhāvinañceva bahussutañca;
::

::gathalast
Aññāya atthaṃ paṭipajjamāno, viññātadhammo sa sukhaṃ {note:so sukhaṃ (sī.)} labhethāti.
::

::centre
Nāvāsuttaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
327\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
328\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum

::

::gatha3

#### 10. Uṭṭhānasuttaṃ

::gatha1

::hangnum
334\.
::

::gatha1
Uṭṭhahatha {pb:P:0.0058} nisīdatha, daḷhaṃ sikkhatha santiyā;

::hangnum

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::gathalast

::

::gathalast

::hangnum

::

::gathalast

::

Itthaṃ sudaṃ bhagavā āyasmantaṃ rāhulaṃ imāhi gāthāhi abhiṇhaṃ ovadatīti.

::centre
Rāhulasuttaṃ ekādasamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

#### 12. Nigrodhakappasuttaṃ

Evaṃ {pb:V:0.0135}{pb:T:0.0391} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā āḷaviyaṃ viharati aggāḷave cetiye. Tena kho pana samayena āyasmato vaṅgīsassa upajjhāyo nigrodhakappo nāma thero aggāḷave cetiye aciraparinibbuto hoti. Atha kho āyasmato vaṅgīsassa rahogatassa paṭisallīnassa evaṃ cetaso parivitakko udapādi – ‘‘parinibbuto nu kho me upajjhāyo udāhu no parinibbuto’’ti? Atha kho āyasmā vaṅgīso sāyanhasamayaṃ paṭisallānā vuṭṭhito yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ {pb:P:0.0060} nisīdi. Ekamantaṃ nisinno kho āyasmā vaṅgīso bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘idha mayhaṃ, bhante, rahogatassa paṭisallīnassa evaṃ cetaso parivitakko udapādi – ‘parinibbuto {pb:M:0.0330} nu kho me upajjhāyo, udāhu no parinabbuto’’’ti. Atha kho āyasmā vaṅgīso uṭṭhāyāsanā ekaṃsaṃ cīvaraṃ katvā yena bhagavā tenañjaliṃ paṇāmetvā bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::hangnum
345\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pucchāma {note:pucchāmi (ka.)} satthāramanomapaññaṃ, diṭṭheva dhamme yo vicikicchānaṃ chettā;
::

::gathalast
Aggāḷave kālamakāsi bhikkhu, ñāto yasassī abhinibbutatto.
::

::hangnum
346\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nigrodhakappo {pb:T:0.0392} iti tassa nāmaṃ, tayā kataṃ bhagavā brāhmaṇassa;
::

::gathalast
So taṃ namassaṃ acari mutyapekkho, āraddhavīriyo daḷhadhammadassī.
::

::hangnum
347\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ sāvakaṃ sakya {note:sakka (sī. syā. pī.)} mayampi sabbe, aññātumicchāma samantacakkhu;
::

::gathalast
Samavaṭṭhitā no savanāya sotā, tuvaṃ no satthā tvamanuttarosi.
::

::hangnum
348\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Chindeva no vicikicchaṃ brūhi metaṃ, parinibbutaṃ vedaya bhūripañña;
::

::gathalast
Majjheva {note:majjhe ca (syā. ka.)} no bhāsa samantacakkhu, sakkova devāna sahassanetto.
::

::hangnum
349\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye keci ganthā idha mohamaggā, aññāṇapakkhā vicikicchaṭhānā;
::

::gathalast
Tathāgataṃ {pb:P:0.0061} patvā na te bhavanti, cakkhuñhi etaṃ paramaṃ narānaṃ.
::

::hangnum
350\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘No {pb:V:0.0136} ce hi jātu puriso kilese, vāto yathā abbhadhanaṃ vihāne;
::

::gathalast
Tamovassa nivuto sabbaloko, na {pb:T:0.0393} jotimantopi narā tapeyyuṃ.
::

::hangnum
351\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhīrā {pb:M:0.0331} ca pajjotakarā bhavanti, taṃ taṃ ahaṃ vīra {note:dhīra (sī. syā.)} tatheva maññe;
::

::gathalast
Vipassinaṃ jānamupāgamumhā {note:jānamupagamamhā (sī. syā.)}, parisāsu no āvikarohi kappaṃ.
::

::hangnum
352\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Khippaṃ giraṃ eraya vaggu vagguṃ, haṃsova paggayha saṇikaṃ {note:saṇiṃ (syā. pī.)} nikūja;
::

::gathalast
Bindussarena suvikappitena, sabbeva te ujjugatā suṇoma.
::

::hangnum
353\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pahīnajātimaraṇaṃ asesaṃ, niggayha dhonaṃ {note:dhotaṃ (sī.)} vadessāmi dhammaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na kāmakāro hi puthujjanānaṃ, saṅkheyyakāro ca {note:saṅkhayyakārova (ka.)} tathāgatānaṃ.
::

::hangnum
354\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sampannaveyyākaraṇaṃ tavedaṃ, samujjupaññassa {note:samujjapaññassa (syā. ka.)} samuggahītaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ayamañjalī pacchimo suppaṇāmito, mā mohayī jānamanomapañña.
::

::hangnum
355\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Vāriṃ yathā {pb:P:0.0062} ghammani ghammatatto, vācābhikaṅkhāmi {pb:T:0.0394} sutaṃ pavassa {note:sutassa vassa (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
356\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yadatthikaṃ {note:yadatthiyaṃ (pī.), yadatthitaṃ (ka.)} brahmacariyaṃ acarī, kappāyano kaccissa taṃ amoghaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nibbāyi so ādu saupādiseso, yathā vimutto ahu taṃ suṇoma’’.
::

::hangnum
357\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Acchecchi {pb:M:0.0332} {note:achejji (ka.)} taṇhaṃ idha nāmarūpe, (iti bhagavā)

::gatha2
Kaṇhassa {note:taṇhāya (ka.)} sotaṃ dīgharattānusayitaṃ;
::

::gatha3

#### 13. Sammāparibbājanīyasuttaṃ

::hangnum

::gatha1
‘‘Pucchāmi {pb:P:0.0063}{pb:T:0.0395} muniṃ pahūtapaññaṃ,
::

::gatha2

::

::gatha3
Nikkhamma gharā panujja kāme, kathaṃ bhikkhu
::

::gathalast
Sammā so loke paribbajeyya’’.
::

::hangnum
362\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yassa maṅgalā samūhatā, (iti bhagavā)
::

So maṅgaladosavippahīno,
::

::gathalast

::hangnum

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
364\.

::

::gathalast
Anurodhavirodhavippahīno, sammā so loke paribbajeyya.
::

::hangnum
365\.

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
366\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:V:0.0138} so upadhīsu sārameti, ādānesu vineyya chandarāgaṃ;
::

::gathalast
So anissito anaññaneyyo, sammā so loke paribbajeyya.
::

::hangnum
367\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vacasā {pb:P:0.0064} manasā ca kammunā ca, aviruddho sammā viditvā dhammaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nibbānapadābhipatthayāno, sammā so loke paribbajeyya.
::

::hangnum
368\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo vandati manti nuṇṇameyya {note:nunnameyya (?)}, akkuṭṭhopi na sandhiyetha bhikkhu;
::

::gathalast
Laddhā parabhojanaṃ na majje, sammā so loke paribbajeyya.
::

::hangnum
369\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Lobhañca bhavañca vippahāya, virato chedanabandhanā ca {note:chedanabandhanato (sī. syā.)} bhikkhu;
::

::gathalast
So tiṇṇakathaṃkatho visallo, sammā so loke paribbajeyya.
::

::hangnum
370\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sāruppaṃ {pb:T:0.0397} attano viditvā, no ca bhikkhu hiṃseyya kañci loke;
::

::gathalast
Yathā tathiyaṃ viditvā dhammaṃ, sammā so loke paribbajeyya.
::

::hangnum
371\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yassānusayā {pb:M:0.0334} na santi keci, mūlā ca {note:mūlā (sī. syā.)} akusalā samūhatāse;
::

::gathalast
So nirāso {note:nirāsayo (sī.), nirāsaso (syā.)} anāsisāno {note:anāsayāno (sī. pī.), anāsasāno (syā.)}, sammā so loke paribbajeyya.
::

::hangnum
372\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āsavakhīṇo {pb:P:0.0065} pahīnamāno, sabbaṃ rāgapathaṃ upātivatto;
::

::gathalast
Danto parinibbuto ṭhitatto, sammā so loke paribbajeyya.
::

::hangnum
373\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saddho sutavā niyāmadassī, vaggagatesu na vaggasāri dhīro;
::

::gathalast
Lobhaṃ dosaṃ vineyya paṭighaṃ, sammā so loke paribbajeyya.
::

::hangnum
374\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṃsuddhajino vivaṭṭacchado, dhammesu vasī pāragū anejo;
::

::gathalast
Saṅkhāranirodhañāṇakusalo{pb:T:0.0398}, sammā so loke paribbajeyya.
::

::hangnum
375\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atītesu anāgatesu cāpi, kappātīto aticcasuddhipañño;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāyatanehi vippamutto, sammā so loke paribbajeyya.
::

::hangnum
376\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aññāya {pb:V:0.0139} padaṃ samecca dhammaṃ, vivaṭaṃ disvāna pahānamāsavānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbupadhīnaṃ parikkhayāno {note:parikkhayā (pī.)}, sammā so loke paribbajeyya’’.
::

::hangnum
377\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Addhā {pb:M:0.0335} hi bhagavā tatheva etaṃ, yo so evaṃvihārī danto bhikkhu;
::

::gathalast
Sabbasaṃyojanayogavītivatto {pb:P:0.0066} {note:sabbasaṃyojaniye ca vītivatto (sī. syā. pī.)}, sammā so loke paribbajeyyā’’ti.
::

::centre
Sammāparibbājanīyasuttaṃ terasamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

#### 14. Dhammikasuttaṃ

Evaṃ me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. Atha kho dhammiko upāsako {pb:T:0.0399} pañcahi upāsakasatehi saddhiṃ yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ nisīdi. Ekamantaṃ nisinno kho dhammiko upāsako bhagavantaṃ gāthāhi ajjhabhāsi –

::hangnum
378\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pucchāmi taṃ gotama bhūripañña, kathaṃkaro sāvako sādhu hoti;
::

::gathalast
Yo vā agārā anagārameti, agārino vā panupāsakāse.
::

::hangnum
379\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tuvañhi lokassa sadevakassa, gatiṃ pajānāsi parāyaṇañca;
::

::gathalast
Na catthi tulyo nipuṇatthadassī, tuvañhi buddhaṃ pavaraṃ vadanti.
::

::hangnum
380\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbaṃ tuvaṃ ñāṇamavecca dhammaṃ, pakāsesi satte anukampamāno;
::

::gathalast
Vivaṭṭacchadosi samantacakkhu, virocasi vimalo sabbaloke.
::

::hangnum
381\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āgañchi {pb:P:0.0067} te santike nāgarājā, erāvaṇo nāma jinoti sutvā;
::

::gathalast
Sopi tayā mantayitvājjhagamā, sādhūti sutvāna patītarūpo.
::

::hangnum
382\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rājāpi {pb:M:0.0336}{pb:V:0.0140}{pb:T:0.0400} taṃ vessavaṇo kuvero, upeti dhammaṃ paripucchamāno;
::

::gathalast
Tassāpi tvaṃ pucchito brūsi dhīra, so cāpi sutvāna patītarūpo.
::

::hangnum
383\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye kecime titthiyā vādasīlā, ājīvakā vā yadi vā nigaṇṭhā;
::

::gathalast
Paññāya taṃ nātitaranti sabbe, ṭhito vajantaṃ viya sīghagāmiṃ.
::

::hangnum
384\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye kecime brāhmaṇā vādasīlā, vuddhā cāpi brāhmaṇā santi keci;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe tayi atthabaddhā bhavanti, ye cāpi aññe vādino maññamānā.
::

::hangnum
385\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ayañhi dhammo nipuṇo sukho ca, yoyaṃ tayā bhagavā suppavutto;
::

::gathalast
Tameva sabbepi {note:sabbe mayaṃ (syā.)} sussūsamānā, taṃ no vada pucchito buddhaseṭṭha.
::

::hangnum
386\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbepi me bhikkhavo sannisinnā, upāsakā cāpi tatheva sotuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Suṇantu dhammaṃ vimalenānubuddhaṃ, subhāsitaṃ {pb:T:0.0401} vāsavasseva devā’’.
::

::hangnum
387\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Suṇātha me bhikkhavo sāvayāmi vo, dhammaṃ dhutaṃ tañca carātha sabbe;
::

::gathalast
Iriyāpathaṃ {pb:P:0.0068} pabbajitānulomikaṃ, sevetha naṃ atthadaso mutīmā.
::

::hangnum
388\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘No ve vikāle vicareyya bhikkhu, gāme ca piṇḍāya careyya kāle;
::

::gathalast
Akālacāriñhi sajanti saṅgā, tasmā vikāle na caranti buddhā.
::

::hangnum
389\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rūpā {pb:M:0.0337} ca saddā ca rasā ca gandhā, phassā ca ye sammadayanti satte;
::

::gathalast
Etesu dhammesu vineyya chandaṃ, kālena so pavise pātarāsaṃ.
::

::hangnum
390\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Piṇḍañca bhikkhu samayena laddhā, eko paṭikkamma raho nisīde;
::

::gathalast
Ajjhattacintī na mano bahiddhā, nicchāraye saṅgahitattabhāvo.
::

::hangnum
391\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sacepi so sallape sāvakena, aññena vā kenaci bhikkhunā vā;
::

::gathalast
Dhammaṃ {pb:T:0.0402} paṇītaṃ tamudāhareyya, na pesuṇaṃ nopi parūpavādaṃ.
::

::hangnum
392\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vādañhi {pb:V:0.0141} eke paṭiseniyanti, na te pasaṃsāma parittapaññe;
::

::gathalast
Tato tato ne pasajanti saṅgā, cittañhi te tattha gamenti dūre.
::

::hangnum
393\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Piṇḍaṃ vihāraṃ sayanāsanañca, āpañca saṅghāṭirajūpavāhanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sutvāna dhammaṃ sugatena desitaṃ, saṅkhāya seve varapaññasāvako.
::

::hangnum
394\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tasmā hi piṇḍe sayanāsane ca, āpe ca saṅghāṭirajūpavāhane;
::

::gathalast
Etesu {pb:P:0.0069} dhammesu anūpalitto, bhikkhu yathā pokkhare vāribindu.
::

::hangnum
395\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gahaṭṭhavattaṃ pana vo vadāmi, yathākaro sāvako sādhu hoti;
::

::gathalast
Na hesa {note:na heso (sī.)} labbhā sapariggahena, phassetuṃ yo kevalo bhikkhudhammo.
::

::hangnum
396\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pāṇaṃ {pb:M:0.0338} na hane {note:na hāne (sī.)} na ca ghātayeyya, na cānujaññā hanataṃ paresaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbesu {pb:T:0.0403} bhūtesu nidhāya daṇḍaṃ, ye thāvarā ye ca tasā santi {note:tasanti (sī. pī.)} loke.
::

::hangnum
397\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato adinnaṃ parivajjayeyya, kiñci kvaci sāvako bujjhamāno;
::

::gathalast
Na hāraye harataṃ nānujaññā, sabbaṃ adinnaṃ parivajjayeyya.
::

::hangnum
398\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Abrahmacariyaṃ parivajjayeyya, aṅgārakāsuṃ jalitaṃva viññū;
::

::gathalast
Asambhuṇanto pana brahmacariyaṃ, parassa dāraṃ na atikkameyya.
::

::hangnum
399\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabhaggato vā parisaggato vā, ekassa veko {note:ceto (sī. syā.)} na musā bhaṇeyya;
::

::gathalast
Na bhāṇaye bhaṇataṃ nānujaññā, sabbaṃ abhūtaṃ parivajjayeyya.
::

::hangnum
400\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Majjañca pānaṃ na samācareyya, dhammaṃ imaṃ rocaye yo gahaṭṭho;
::

::gathalast
Na pāyaye pivataṃ nānujaññā, ummādanantaṃ iti naṃ viditvā.
::

::hangnum
401\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Madā hi pāpāni karonti bālā, kārenti caññepi jane pamatte;
::

::gathalast
Etaṃ {pb:P:0.0070}{pb:T:0.0404} apuññāyatanaṃ vivajjaye, ummādanaṃ mohanaṃ bālakantaṃ.
::

::hangnum
402\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pāṇaṃ {pb:V:0.0142} na hane na cādinnamādiye, musā na bhāse na ca majjapo siyā;
::

::gathalast
Abrahmacariyā virameyya methunā, rattiṃ na bhuñjeyya vikālabhojanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
403\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mālaṃ {pb:M:0.0339} na dhāre na ca gandhamācare, mañce chamāyaṃ va sayetha santhate;
::

::gathalast
Etañhi aṭṭhaṅgikamāhuposathaṃ, buddhena dukkhantagunā pakāsitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
404\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato ca pakkhassupavassuposathaṃ, cātuddasiṃ pañcadasiñca aṭṭhamiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pāṭihāriyapakkhañca pasannamānaso, aṭṭhaṅgupetaṃ susamattarūpaṃ.
::

::hangnum
405\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato ca pāto upavutthuposatho, annena pānena ca bhikkhusaṅghaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pasannacitto anumodamāno, yathārahaṃ saṃvibhajetha viññū.
::

::hangnum
406\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhammena mātāpitaro bhareyya, payojaye dhammikaṃ so vaṇijjaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Etaṃ {pb:T:0.0405} gihī vattayamappamatto, sayampabhe nāma upeti deve’’ti.
::

::centre
Dhammikasuttaṃ cuddasamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

::centre
Cūḷavaggo dutiyo niṭṭhito.
::

Tassuddānaṃ {pb:P:0.0071} –

::gatha1
Ratanāmagandho hiri ca, maṅgalaṃ sūcilomena;
::

::gathalast
Dhammacariyañca brāhmaṇo {note:kapilo brāhmaṇopi ca (syā. ka.)}, nāvā kiṃsīlamuṭṭhānaṃ.
::

::gatha1
Rāhulo puna kappo ca, paribbājaniyaṃ tathā;
::

::gathalast
Dhammikañca viduno āhu, cūḷavagganti cuddasāti.
::

### 3. Mahāvaggo

#### 1. Pabbajjāsuttaṃ

::hangnum
407\.
::

::gatha1
Pabbajjaṃ {pb:M:0.0340}{pb:V:0.0143}{pb:P:0.0072} kittayissāmi, yathā pabbaji cakkhumā;
::

::gathalast
Yathā vīmaṃsamāno so, pabbajjaṃ samarocayi.
::

::hangnum
408\.
::

::gatha1
Sambādhoyaṃ gharāvāso, rajassāyatanaṃ iti;
::

::gathalast
Abbhokāsova pabbajjā, iti disvāna pabbaji.
::

::hangnum
409\.
::

::gatha1
Pabbajitvāna kāyena, pāpakammaṃ vivajjayi;
::

::gathalast
Vacīduccaritaṃ {pb:T:0.0406} hitvā, ājīvaṃ parisodhayi.
::

::hangnum
410\.
::

::gatha1
Agamā rājagahaṃ buddho, magadhānaṃ giribbajaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Piṇḍāya abhihāresi, ākiṇṇavaralakkhaṇo.
::

::hangnum
411\.
::

::gatha1
Tamaddasā bimbisāro, pāsādasmiṃ patiṭṭhito;
::

::gathalast
Disvā lakkhaṇasampannaṃ, imamatthaṃ abhāsatha.
::

::hangnum
412\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Imaṃ bhonto nisāmetha, abhirūpo brahā suci;
::

::gathalast
Caraṇena ca sampanno, yugamattañca pekkhati.
::

::hangnum
413\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Okkhittacakkhu satimā, nāyaṃ nīcakulāmiva;
::

::gathalast
Rājadūtābhidhāvantu, kuhiṃ bhikkhu gamissati’’.
::

::hangnum
414\.
::

::gatha1
Te pesitā rājadūtā, piṭṭhito anubandhisuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kuhiṃ gamissati bhikkhu, kattha vāso bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
415\.
::

::gatha1
Sapadānaṃ {pb:V:0.0144} caramāno, guttadvāro susaṃvuto;
::

::gathalast
Khippaṃ pattaṃ apūresi, sampajāno paṭissato.
::

::hangnum
416\.
::

::gatha1
Piṇḍacāraṃ {pb:P:0.0073} caritvāna, nikkhamma nagarā muni;
::

::gathalast
Paṇḍavaṃ abhihāresi, ettha vāso bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
417\.
::

::gatha1
Disvāna vāsūpagataṃ, tayo {note:tato (sī. pī.)} dūtā upāvisuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tesu ekova {note:eko ca dūto (sī. syā. pī.)} āgantvā, rājino paṭivedayi.
::

::hangnum
418\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Esa {pb:M:0.0341} bhikkhu mahārāja, paṇḍavassa puratthato {note:purakkhato (syā. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Nisinno byagghusabhova, sīhova girigabbhare’’.
::

::hangnum
419\.
::

::gatha1
Sutvāna {pb:T:0.0407} dūtavacanaṃ, bhaddayānena khattiyo;
::

::gathalast
Taramānarūpo niyyāsi, yena paṇḍavapabbato.
::

::hangnum
420\.
::

::gatha1
Sa yānabhūmiṃ yāyitvā, yānā oruyha khattiyo;
::

::gathalast
Pattiko upasaṅkamma, āsajja naṃ upāvisi.
::

::hangnum
421\.
::

::gatha1
Nisajja rājā sammodi, kathaṃ sāraṇīyaṃ tato;
::

::gathalast
Kathaṃ so vītisāretvā, imamatthaṃ abhāsatha.
::

::hangnum
422\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yuvā ca daharo cāsi, paṭhamuppattiko {note:paṭhamuppattiyā (sī.), paṭhamuppattito (syā.)} susu;
::

::gathalast
Vaṇṇārohena sampanno, jātimā viya khattiyo.
::

::hangnum
423\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sobhayanto anīkaggaṃ, nāgasaṅghapurakkhato;
::

::gathalast
Dadāmi bhoge bhuñjassu, jātiṃ akkhāhi pucchito’’.
::

::hangnum
424\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ujuṃ janapado rāja, himavantassa passato;
::

::gathalast
Dhanavīriyena sampanno, kosalesu {note:kosalassa (syā. ka.)} niketino.
::

::hangnum
425\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ādiccā {pb:V:0.0145}{pb:P:0.0074} {note:ādicco (ka.)} nāma gottena, sākiyā {note:sākiyo (ka.)} nāma jātiyā;
::

::gathalast
Tamhā kulā pabbajitomhi, na kāme abhipatthayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
426\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kāmesvādīnavaṃ disvā, nekkhammaṃ daṭṭhu khemato;
::

::gathalast
Padhānāya gamissāmi, ettha me rañjatī mano’’ti.
::

::centre
Pabbajjāsuttaṃ paṭhamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

#### 2. Padhānasuttaṃ

::hangnum
427\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ {pb:T:0.0408} maṃ padhānapahitattaṃ, nadiṃ nerañjaraṃ pati;
::

::gathalast
Viparakkamma jhāyantaṃ, yogakkhemassa pattiyā.
::

::hangnum
428\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Namucī karuṇaṃ vācaṃ, bhāsamāno upāgami;
::

::gathalast
‘Kiso tvamasi dubbaṇṇo, santike maraṇaṃ tava.
::

::hangnum
429\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Sahassabhāgo {pb:M:0.0342} maraṇassa, ekaṃso tava jīvitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Jīva bho jīvitaṃ seyyo, jīvaṃ puññāni kāhasi.
::

::hangnum
430\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Carato {pb:P:0.0075} ca te brahmacariyaṃ, aggihuttañca jūhato;
::

::gathalast
Pahūtaṃ cīyate puññaṃ, kiṃ padhānena kāhasi.
::

::hangnum
431\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Duggo maggo padhānāya, dukkaro durabhisambhavo’’’;
::

::gathalast
Imā gāthā bhaṇaṃ māro, aṭṭhā buddhassa santike.
::

::hangnum
432\.
::

::gatha1
Taṃ tathāvādinaṃ māraṃ, bhagavā etadabravi;
::

::gathalast
‘‘Pamattabandhu pāpima, yenatthena {note:senatthena (?), attano atthena (aṭṭha. saṃvaṇṇanā)} idhāgato.
::

::hangnum
433\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aṇumattopi {pb:V:0.0146} {note:aṇumattenapi (sī. syā.)} puññena, attho mayhaṃ na vijjati;
::

::gathalast
Yesañca attho puññena, te māro vattumarahati.
::

::hangnum
434\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atthi saddhā tathā {note:tato (sī. pī.), tapo (syā. ka.)} vīriyaṃ, paññā ca mama vijjati;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ maṃ pahitattampi, kiṃ jīvamanupucchasi.
::

::hangnum
435\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nadīnamapi sotāni, ayaṃ vāto visosaye;
::

::gathalast
Kiñca {pb:T:0.0409} me pahitattassa, lohitaṃ nupasussaye.
::

::hangnum
436\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Lohite sussamānamhi, pittaṃ semhañca sussati;
::

::gatha2
Maṃsesu khīyamānesu, bhiyyo cittaṃ pasīdati;
::

::gathalast
Bhiyyo sati ca paññā ca, samādhi mama tiṭṭhati.
::

::hangnum
437\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassa mevaṃ viharato, pattassuttamavedanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kāmesu {note:kāme (sī. syā.)} nāpekkhate cittaṃ, passa sattassa suddhataṃ.
::

::hangnum
438\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kāmā {pb:P:0.0076} te paṭhamā senā, dutiyā arati vuccati;
::

::gathalast
Tatiyā khuppipāsā te, catutthī taṇhā pavuccati.
::

::hangnum
439\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pañcamaṃ {note:pañcamī (sī. pī.)} thinamiddhaṃ te, chaṭṭhā bhīrū pavuccati;
::

::gathalast
Sattamī vicikicchā te, makkho thambho te aṭṭhamo.
::

::hangnum
440\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Lābho siloko sakkāro, micchāladdho ca yo yaso;
::

::gathalast
Yo cattānaṃ samukkaṃse, pare ca avajānati.
::

::hangnum
441\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Esā {pb:M:0.0343} namuci te senā, kaṇhassābhippahārinī;
::

::gathalast
Na naṃ asūro jināti, jetvā ca labhate sukhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
442\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Esa muñjaṃ parihare, dhiratthu mama {note:ida (ka.)} jīvitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Saṅgāme me mataṃ seyyo, yaṃ ce jīve parājito.
::

::hangnum
443\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pagāḷhettha {pb:V:0.0147} na dissanti, eke samaṇabrāhmaṇā;
::

::gathalast
Tañca maggaṃ na jānanti, yena gacchanti subbatā.
::

::hangnum
444\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samantā dhajiniṃ disvā, yuttaṃ māraṃ savāhanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yuddhāya paccuggacchāmi, mā maṃ ṭhānā acāvayi.
::

::hangnum
445\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ {pb:T:0.0410} te taṃ nappasahati, senaṃ loko sadevako;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ {pb:P:0.0077} te paññāya bhecchāmi {note:gacchāmi (sī.), vecchāmi (syā.), vajjhāmi (ka.)}, āmaṃ pattaṃva asmanā {note:pakkaṃva amunā (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
446\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vasīkaritvā {note:vasiṃ karitvā (bahūsu)} saṅkappaṃ, satiñca sūpatiṭṭhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Raṭṭhā raṭṭhaṃ vicarissaṃ, sāvake vinayaṃ puthū.
::

::hangnum
447\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Te appamattā pahitattā, mama sāsanakārakā;
::

::gathalast
Akāmassa {note:akāmā (ka.)} te gamissanti, yattha gantvā na socare’’.
::

::hangnum
448\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satta vassāni bhagavantaṃ, anubandhiṃ padāpadaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Otāraṃ nādhigacchissaṃ, sambuddhassa satīmato.
::

::hangnum
449\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Medavaṇṇaṃva pāsāṇaṃ, vāyaso anupariyagā;
::

::gathalast
Apettha muduṃ {note:mudu (sī.)} vindema, api assādanā siyā.
::

::hangnum
450\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aladdhā tattha assādaṃ, vāyasetto apakkami;
::

::gathalast
Kākova selamāsajja, nibbijjāpema gotamaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
451\.
::

::gatha1
Tassa {pb:P:0.0078} sokaparetassa, vīṇā kacchā abhassatha;
::

::gathalast
Tato so dummano yakkho, tatthevantaradhāyathāti.
::

::centre
Padhānasuttaṃ dutiyaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

#### 3. Subhāsitasuttaṃ

Evaṃ {pb:M:0.0344}{pb:V:0.0148} me sutaṃ – eka samayaṃ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. Tatra kho bhagavā bhikkhū {pb:T:0.0411} āmantesi – ‘‘bhikkhavo’’ti. ‘‘Bhadante’’ti te bhikkhū bhagavato paccassosuṃ. Bhagavā etadavoca –

‘‘Catūhi, bhikkhave, aṅgehi samannāgatā vācā subhāsitā hoti, na dubbhāsitā, anavajjā ca ananuvajjā ca viññūnaṃ. Katamehi catūhi? Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu subhāsitaṃyeva bhāsati no dubbhāsitaṃ, dhammaṃyeva bhāsati no adhammaṃ, piyaṃyeva bhāsati no appiyaṃ, saccaṃyeva bhāsati no alikaṃ. Imehi kho, bhikkhave, catūhi aṅgehi samannāgatā vācā subhāsitā hoti, no dubbhāsitā, anavajjā ca ananuvajjā ca viññūna’’nti. Idamavoca bhagavā. Idaṃ vatvāna sugato athāparaṃ etadavoca satthā –

::hangnum
452\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Subhāsitaṃ uttamamāhu santo, dhammaṃ bhaṇe nādhammaṃ taṃ dutiyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Piyaṃ bhaṇe nāppiyaṃ taṃ tatiyaṃ, saccaṃ bhaṇe nālikaṃ taṃ catuttha’’nti.
::

Atha {pb:P:0.0079} kho āyasmā vaṅgīso uṭṭhāyāsanā ekaṃsaṃ cīvaraṃ katvā yena bhagavā tenañjaliṃ paṇāmetvā bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘paṭibhāti maṃ bhagavā, paṭibhāti maṃ sugatā’’ti. ‘‘Paṭibhātu taṃ vaṅgīsā’’ti bhagavā avoca. Atha kho āyasmā vaṅgīso bhagavantaṃ sammukhā sāruppāhi gāthāhi abhitthavi –

::hangnum
453\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tameva vācaṃ bhāseyya, yāyattānaṃ na tāpaye;
::

::gathalast
Pare {pb:T:0.0412} ca na vihiṃseyya, sā ve vācā subhāsitā.
::

::hangnum
454\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Piyavācameva bhāseyya, yā vācā paṭinanditā;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ anādāya pāpāni, paresaṃ bhāsate piyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
455\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saccaṃ ve amatā vācā, esa dhammo sanantano;
::

::gathalast
Sacce atthe ca dhamme ca, āhu santo patiṭṭhitā.
::

::hangnum
456\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ {pb:M:0.0345}{pb:V:0.0149} buddho bhāsati vācaṃ, khemaṃ nibbānapattiyā;
::

::gathalast
Dukkhassantakiriyāya, sā ve vācānamuttamā’’ti.
::

::centre
Subhāsitasuttaṃ tatiyaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

#### 4. Sundarikabhāradvājasuttaṃ

Evaṃ me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā kosalesu viharati sundarikāya nadiyā tīre. Tena kho pana samayena sundarikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo sundarikāya nadiyā tīre aggiṃ juhati, aggihuttaṃ paricarati. Atha kho sundarikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo aggiṃ juhitvā aggihuttaṃ paricaritvā uṭṭhāyāsanā samantā catuddisā anuvilokesi – ‘‘ko nu kho imaṃ habyasesaṃ bhuñjeyyā’’ti? Addasā kho sundarikabhāradvājo {pb:P:0.0080} brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ avidūre aññatarasmiṃ rukkhamūle sasīsaṃ pārutaṃ nisinnaṃ; disvāna vāmena hatthena habyasesaṃ gahetvā dakkhiṇena hatthena kamaṇḍaluṃ gahetvā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami.

Atha kho bhagavā sundarikabhāradvājassa brāhmaṇassa padasaddena sīsaṃ {pb:T:0.0413} vivari. Atha kho sundarikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo – ‘‘muṇḍo ayaṃ bhavaṃ, muṇḍako ayaṃ bhava’’nti tatova puna nivattitukāmo ahosi. Atha kho sundarikabhāradvājassa brāhmaṇassa etadahosi – ‘‘muṇḍāpi hi idhekacce brāhmaṇā bhavanti, yaṃnūnāhaṃ upasaṅkamitvā jātiṃ puccheyya’’nti. Atha kho sundarikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘kiṃjacco bhava’’nti?

Atha kho bhagavā sundarikabhāradvājaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ gāthāhi ajjhabhāsi –

::hangnum
457\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na brāhmaṇo nomhi na rājaputto, na vessāyano uda koci nomhi;
::

::gathalast
Gottaṃ pariññāya puthujjanānaṃ, akiñcano manta carāmi loke.
::

::hangnum
458\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṅghāṭivāsī {pb:M:0.0346}{pb:V:0.0150} agaho carāmi {note:agiho (ka. sī. pī.) ageho (katthaci)}, nivuttakeso abhinibbutatto;
::

::gathalast

::

::gathalast

Atha kho sundarikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘abhikkantaṃ, bho gotama, abhikkantaṃ, bho gotama! Seyyathāpi, bho gotama, nikkujjitaṃ vā ukkujjeyya, paṭicchannaṃ vā vivareyya, mūḷhassa vā maggaṃ ācikkheyya, andhakāre vā telapajjotaṃ dhāreyya – cakkhumanto rūpāni dakkhantīti; evamevaṃ bhotā gotamena anekapariyāyena dhammo pakāsito. Esāhaṃ bhavantaṃ gotamaṃ saraṇaṃ gacchāmi dhammañca bhikkhusaṅghañca. Labheyyāhaṃ bhoto gotamassa santike pabbajjaṃ, labheyyaṃ upasampada’’nti. Alattha kho {pb:T:0.0420} sundarikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo…pe… arahataṃ ahosīti.

::centre
Sundarikabhāradvājasuttaṃ catutthaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

#### 5. Māghasuttaṃ

Evaṃ me sutaṃ – eka samayaṃ bhagavā rājagahe viharati gijjhakūṭe pabbate. Atha kho māgho māṇavo yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā {pb:M:0.0351} bhagavatā saddhiṃ sammodi. Sammodanīyaṃ kathaṃ sāraṇīyaṃ vītisāretvā ekamantaṃ nisīdi. Ekamantaṃ nisinno kho māgho māṇavo bhagavantaṃ {pb:P:0.0087} etadavoca –

‘‘Ahañhi, bho gotama, dāyako dānapati vadaññū yācayogo; dhammena bhoge pariyesāmi; dhammena bhoge pariyesitvā dhammaladdhehi bhogehi dhammādhigatehi ekassapi dadāmi dvinnampi {pb:V:0.0154} tiṇṇampi catunnampi pañcannampi channampi sattannampi aṭṭhannampi navannampi dasannampi dadāmi, vīsāyapi tiṃsāyapi cattālīsāyapi paññāsāyapi dadāmi, satassapi dadāmi, bhiyyopi dadāmi. Kaccāhaṃ, bho gotama, evaṃ dadanto evaṃ yajanto bahuṃ puññaṃ pasavāmī’’ti{pb:T:0.0421}?

‘‘Taggha tvaṃ, māṇava, evaṃ dadanto evaṃ yajanto bahuṃ puññaṃ pasavasi. Yo kho, māṇava, dāyako dānapati vadaññū yācayogo; dhammena bhoge pariyesati; dhammena bhoge pariyesitvā dhammaladdhehi bhogehi dhammādhigatehi ekassapi dadāti…pe… satassapi dadāti, bhiyyopi dadāti, bahuṃ so puññaṃ pasavatī’’ti. Atha kho māgho māṇavo bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::hangnum
491\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pucchāmahaṃ gotamaṃ vadaññuṃ, (iti māgho māṇavo)
::

::gatha2
Kāsāyavāsiṃ agahaṃ {note:agihaṃ (sī.), agehaṃ (pī.)} carantaṃ;
::

::gatha3
Yo yācayogo dānapati {note:dānapatī (sī. syā. pī.)} gahaṭṭho, puññatthiko {note:puññapekho (sī. pī. ka.)} yajati puññapekkho;
::

::gathalast
Dadaṃ {pb:P:0.0088} paresaṃ idha annapānaṃ, kathaṃ hutaṃ yajamānassa sujjhe’’.
::

::hangnum
492\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo yācayogo dānapati gahaṭṭho, (māghāti bhagavā)
::

::gatha2
Puññatthiko yajati puññapekkho;
::

::gathalast
Dadaṃ paresaṃ idha annapānaṃ, ārādhaye dakkhiṇeyyebhi tādi’’.
::

::hangnum
493\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo {pb:M:0.0352} yācayogo dānapati gahaṭṭho, (iti māgho māṇavo)
::

::gatha2
Puññatthiko yajati puññapekkho;
::

::gathalast
Dadaṃ paresaṃ idha annapānaṃ, akkhāhi me bhagavā dakkhiṇeyye’’.
::

::hangnum
494\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye {pb:T:0.0422} ve asattā {note:alaggā (syā.)} vicaranti loke, akiñcanā kevalino yatattā;
::

::gathalast
Kālena tesu habyaṃ pavecche, yo brāhmaṇo puññapekkho yajetha.
::

::hangnum
495\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye sabbasaṃyojanabandhanacchidā, dantā vimuttā anīghā nirāsā;
::

::gathalast
Kālena tesu habyaṃ pavecche, yo brāhmaṇo puññapekkho yajetha.

496\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye {pb:V:0.0155} sabbasaṃyojanavippamuttā, dantā vimuttā anīghā nirāsā;
::

::gathalast
Kālena tesu habyaṃ pavecche, yo brāhmaṇo puññapekkho yajetha.

::hangnum
497\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rāgañca dosañca pahāya mohaṃ, khīṇāsavā vūsitabrahmacariyā;
::

::gathalast

::gatha2

::gatha3

::

::gathalast
