::

Evaṃ vutte, māgho māṇavo bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘abhikkantaṃ, bho gotama…pe… ajjatagge pāṇupetaṃ saraṇaṃ gata’’nti.

::centre
Māghasuttaṃ pañcamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

#### 6. Sabhiyasuttaṃ

Evaṃ {pb:T:0.0426} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā rājagahe viharati veḷuvane kalandakanivāpe. Tena kho pana samayena sabhiyassa paribbājakassa purāṇasālohitāya devatāya pañhā uddiṭṭhā honti – ‘‘yo te, sabhiya, samaṇo vā brāhmaṇo vā ime pañhe puṭṭho byākaroti tassa santike brahmacariyaṃ careyyāsī’’ti.

Atha kho sabhiyo paribbājako tassā devatāya santike te pañhe uggahetvā ye te samaṇabrāhmaṇā saṅghino gaṇino gaṇācariyā ñātā yasassino titthakarā sādhusammatā {pb:P:0.0092} bahujanassa, seyyathidaṃ – pūraṇo kassapo makkhaligosālo ajito kesakambalo pakudho {note:kakudho (sī.) pakuddho (syā. kaṃ.)} kaccāno sañcayo {note:sañjayo (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} belaṭṭhaputto {note:bellaṭṭhiputto (sī. pī.), veḷaṭṭhaputto (syā.)} nigaṇṭho nāṭaputto {note:nātaputto (sī. pī.)}, te upasaṅkamitvā te pañhe pucchati. Te sabhiyena {pb:M:0.0356} paribbājakena pañhe puṭṭhā na sampāyanti; asampāyantā kopañca dosañca appaccayañca pātukaronti. Api ca sabhiyaṃ yeva paribbājakaṃ paṭipucchanti.

Atha kho sabhiyassa paribbājakassa etadahosi – ‘‘ye kho te bhonto samaṇabrāhmaṇā saṅghino gaṇino gaṇācariyā ñātā yasassino titthakarā sādhusammatā bahujanassa, seyyathidaṃ – pūraṇo kassapo…pe… nigaṇṭho nāṭaputto, te mayā pañhe puṭṭhā na sampāyanti, asampāyantā kopañca dosañca appaccayañca pātukaronti; api {pb:T:0.0427} ca maññevettha paṭipucchanti. Yannūnnāhaṃ hīnāyāvattitvā kāme paribhuñjeyya’’nti.

Atha {pb:V:0.0158} kho sabhiyassa paribbājakassa etadahosi – ‘‘ayampi kho samaṇo gotamo saṅghī ceva gaṇī ca gaṇācariyo ca ñāto yasassī titthakaro sādhusammato bahujanassa; yaṃnūnāhaṃ samaṇaṃ gotamaṃ upasaṅkamitvā ime pañhe puccheyya’’nti.

Atha kho sabhiyassa paribbājakassa etadahosi – ‘‘yepi kho te {note:ye kho te (syā.), yaṃ kho te (ka.)} bhonto samaṇabrāhmaṇā jiṇṇā vuḍḍhā mahallakā addhagatā vayoanuppattā therā rattaññū cirapabbajitā saṅghino gaṇino gaṇācariyā ñātā yasassino titthakarā sādhusammatā bahujanassa, seyyathidaṃ – pūraṇo kassapo…pe. {pb:P:0.0093}… nigaṇṭho nāṭaputto, tepi mayā pañhe puṭṭhā na sampāyanti, asampāyantā kopañca dosañca appaccayañca pātukaronti, api ca maññevettha paṭipucchanti; kiṃ pana me samaṇo gotamo ime pañhe puṭṭho byākarissati! Samaṇo hi gotamo daharo ceva jātiyā, navo ca pabbajjāyā’’ti.

Atha kho sabhiyassa paribbājakassa etadahosi – ‘‘samaṇo kho {note:samaṇo kho gotamo (syā. ka.)} daharoti na uññātabbo na paribhotabbo. Daharopi cesa samaṇo gotamo mahiddhiko hoti mahānubhāvo, yaṃnūnāhaṃ samaṇaṃ gotamaṃ upasaṅkamitvā ime pañhe puccheyya’’nti.

Atha {pb:T:0.0428} kho sabhiyo paribbājako yena rājagahaṃ tena cārikaṃ pakkāmi. Anupubbena cārikaṃ caramāno yena rājagahaṃ veḷuvanaṃ kalandakanivāpo, yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavatā saddhiṃ {pb:M:0.0357} sammodi. Sammodanīyaṃ kathaṃ sāraṇīyaṃ vītisāretvā ekamantaṃ nisīdi. Ekamantaṃ nisinno kho sabhiyo paribbājako bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::hangnum
515\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kaṅkhī vecikicchī āgamaṃ, (iti sabhiyo)

::gatha2
Pañhe pucchituṃ abhikaṅkhamāno;

::gatha3

::

::gathalast
Anupubbaṃ anudhammaṃ byākarohi me’’.

::gathalast

::

::gathalast
Tassa tasseva pañhassa, ahaṃ antaṃ karomi te’’ti.
::

Atha kho sabhiyassa paribbājakassa etadahosi – ‘‘acchariyaṃ vata, bho, abbhutaṃ vata, bho! Yaṃ vatāhaṃ aññesu samaṇabrāhmaṇesu okāsakammamattampi {note:okāsamattampi (sī. pī.)} nālatthaṃ taṃ me idaṃ samaṇena gotamena okāsakammaṃ kata’’nti. Attamano pamudito udaggo pītisomanassajāto bhagavantaṃ {pb:T:0.0429} pañhaṃ apucchi –

::gatha1

Atha kho sabhiyo paribbājako bhagavato bhāsitaṃ abhinanditvā anumoditvā attamano pamudito udaggo pītisomanassajāto {pb:P:0.0100} uṭṭhāyāsanā ekaṃsaṃ uttarāsaṅgaṃ karitvā yena bhagavā tenañjaliṃ paṇāmetvā bhagavantaṃ sammukhā sāruppāhi gāthāhi abhitthavi –

543\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
544\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
545\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ me kaṅkhitamaññāsi, vicikicchā maṃ tārayi namo te;
::

::gathalast
Muni monapathesu pattipatta, akhila ādiccabandhu soratosi.
::

::hangnum
546\.

::gathalast
Addhā munīsi sambuddho, natthi nīvaraṇā tava.
::

551\.

::

::gathalast
Sīhosi anupādāno, pahīnabhayabheravo.
::

::hangnum
552\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Puṇḍarīkaṃ {pb:M:0.0363} yathā vaggu, toye na upalimpati {note:toyena na upalippati (sī.), toye na upalippati (pī.), toyena na upalimpati (ka.)};
::

::gatha2
Evaṃ puññe ca pāpe ca, ubhaye tvaṃ na limpasi;
::

::gathalast
Pāde vīra pasārehi, sabhiyo vandati satthuno’’ti.
::

Atha kho sabhiyo paribbājako bhagavato pādesu sirasā nipatitvā bhagavantaṃ etadavoca {pb:V:0.0164} – ‘‘abhikkantaṃ, bhante…pe… esāhaṃ bhagavantaṃ saraṇaṃ gacchāmi dhammañca bhikkhusaṅghañca; labheyyāhaṃ, bhante, bhagavato santike pabbajjaṃ, labheyyaṃ upasampada’’nti{pb:P:0.0102}.

‘‘Yo kho, sabhiya, aññatitthiyapubbo imasmiṃ dhammavinaye ākaṅkhati pabbajjaṃ, ākaṅkhati upasampadaṃ, so cattāro māse parivasati; catunnaṃ māsānaṃ accayena āraddhacittā bhikkhū pabbājenti, upasampādenti bhikkhubhāvāya. Api ca mettha puggalavemattatā viditā’’ti.

‘‘Sace, bhante, aññatitthiyapubbā imasmiṃ dhammavinaye ākaṅkhantā pabbajjaṃ, ākaṅkhantā {pb:T:0.0437} upasampadaṃ cattāro māse parivasanti, catunnaṃ māsānaṃ accayena āraddhacittā bhikkhū pabbājenti, upasampādenti bhikkhubhāvāya, ahaṃ cattāri vassāni parivasissāmi; catunnaṃ vassānaṃ accayena āraddhacittā bhikkhū pabbājentu upasampādentu bhikkhubhāvāyā’’ti. Alattha kho sabhiyo paribbājako bhagavato santike pabbajjaṃ alattha upasampadaṃ…pe… aññataro kho panāyasmā sabhiyo arahataṃ ahosīti.

::centre
Sabhiyasuttaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

#### 7. Selasuttaṃ

Evaṃ me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā aṅguttarāpesu cārikaṃ caramāno mahatā bhikkhusaṅghena saddhiṃ aḍḍhateḷasehi {pb:P:0.0103} bhikkhusatehi yena āpaṇaṃ nāma aṅguttarāpānaṃ nigamo tadavasari. Assosi {pb:T:0.0438} kho keṇiyo jaṭilo ‘‘samaṇo khalu, bho, gotamo sakyaputto sakyakulā pabbajito aṅguttarāpesu cārikaṃ caramāno mahatā bhikkhusaṅghena saddhiṃ aḍḍhateḷasehi bhikkhusatehi āpaṇaṃ anuppatto. Taṃ kho pana bhavantaṃ gotamaṃ {pb:M:0.0364} evaṃ kalyāṇo kittisaddo abbhuggato – ‘itipi so bhagavā arahaṃ sammāsambuddho vijjācaraṇasampanno sugato lokavidū anuttaro purisadammasārathi satthā devamanussānaṃ buddho bhagavā’ti {note:bhagavā (syā. pī.)}. So imaṃ lokaṃ sadevakaṃ samārakaṃ sabrahmakaṃ sassamaṇabrāhmaṇiṃ pajaṃ sadevamanussaṃ sayaṃ abhiññā sacchikatvā pavedeti. So dhammaṃ desati ādikalyāṇaṃ majjhekalyāṇaṃ pariyosānakalyāṇaṃ sātthaṃ sabyañjanaṃ, kevalaparipuṇṇaṃ {pb:V:0.0165} parisuddhaṃ brahmacariyaṃ pakāseti. Sādhu kho pana tathārūpānaṃ arahataṃ dassanaṃ hotī’’ti.

Atha kho keṇiyo jaṭilo yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavatā saddhiṃ sammodi. Sammodanīyaṃ kathaṃ sāraṇīyaṃ vītisāretvā ekamantaṃ nisīdi. Ekamantaṃ nisinnaṃ kho keṇiyaṃ jaṭilaṃ bhagavā dhammiyā kathāya sandassesi samādapesi samuttejesi sampahaṃsesi. Atha kho keṇiyo jaṭilo bhagavatā dhammiyā kathāya sandassito samādapito samuttejito sampahaṃsito bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘adhivāsetu me bhavaṃ gotamo svātanāya bhattaṃ saddhiṃ bhikkhusaṅghenā’’ti. Evaṃ vutte, bhagavā keṇiyaṃ jaṭilaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘mahā kho, keṇiya, bhikkhusaṅgho {pb:P:0.0104} aḍḍhateḷasāni bhikkhusatāni; tvañca brāhmaṇesu {pb:T:0.0439} abhippasanno’’ti.

Dutiyampi kho keṇiyo jaṭilo bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘kiñcāpi, bho gotama, mahā bhikkhusaṅgho aḍḍhateḷasāni bhikkhusatāni, ahañca brāhmaṇesu abhippasanno; adhivāsetu me bhavaṃ gotamo svātanāya bhattaṃ saddhiṃ bhikkhusaṅghenā’’ti. Dutiyampi kho bhagavā keṇiyaṃ jaṭilaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘mahā kho, keṇiya, bhikkhusaṅgho aḍḍhateḷasāni bhikkhusatāni; tvañca brāhmaṇesu abhippasanno’’ti.

Tatiyampi kho keṇiyo jaṭilo bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘kiñcāpi, bho gotama, mahā bhikkhusaṅgho aḍḍhateḷasāni bhikkhusatāni, ahañca brāhmaṇesu abhippasanno, adhivāsetu {note:adhivāsetveva (sī.)} me bhavaṃ gotamo svātanāya bhattaṃ saddhiṃ bhikkhusaṅghenā’’ti. Adhivāsesi bhagavā tuṇhībhāvena. Atha kho keṇiyo jaṭilo bhagavato adhivāsanaṃ viditvā {pb:M:0.0365} uṭṭhāyāsanā yena sako assamo tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā mittāmacce ñātisālohite āmantesi – ‘‘suṇantu me bhavanto mittāmaccā ñātisālohitā, samaṇo me gotamo nimantito svātanāya bhattaṃ saddhiṃ bhikkhusaṅghena, yena me kāyaveyyāvaṭikaṃ kareyyāthā’’ti. ‘‘Evaṃ, bho’’ti kho keṇiyassa jaṭilassa mittāmaccā ñātisālohitā keṇiyassa jaṭilassa paṭissutvā appekacce uddhanāni khaṇanti, appekacce kaṭṭhāni phālenti, appekacce bhājanāni dhovanti, appekacce udakamaṇikaṃ patiṭṭhāpenti, appekacce āsanāni paññāpenti. Keṇiyo pana jaṭilo sāmaṃyeva maṇḍalamāḷaṃ {pb:T:0.0440} paṭiyādeti.

Tena kho pana samayena selo brāhmaṇo āpaṇe paṭivasati, tiṇṇaṃ {pb:P:0.0105} vedānaṃ pāragū sanighaṇḍukeṭubhānaṃ {pb:V:0.0166} sākkharappabhedānaṃ itihāsapañcamānaṃ padako veyyākaraṇo lokāyatamahāpurisalakkhaṇesu anavayo, tīṇi ca māṇavakasatāni mante vāceti.

Tena kho pana samayena keṇiyo jaṭilo sele brāhmaṇe abhippasanno hoti. Atha kho selo brāhmaṇo tīhi māṇavakasatehi parivuto jaṅghāvihāraṃ anucaṅkamamāno anuvicaramāno yena keṇiyassa jaṭilassa assamo tenupasaṅkami. Addasā kho selo brāhmaṇo keṇiyassa jaṭilassa assame {note:keṇissamiye jaṭile (sī. pī.)} appekacce uddhanāni khaṇante…pe… appekacce āsanāni paññapente, keṇiyaṃ pana jaṭilaṃ sāmaṃyeva maṇḍalamāḷaṃ paṭiyādentaṃ. Disvāna keṇiyaṃ jaṭilaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘kiṃ nu kho bhoto keṇiyassa āvāho vā bhavissati, vivāho vā bhavissati, mahāyañño vā paccupaṭṭhito, rājā vā māgadho seniyo bimbisāro nimantito svātanāya saddhiṃ balakāyenā’’ti?

‘‘Na me, bho sela, āvāho vā bhavissati vivāho vā, nāpi rājā māgadho seniyo bimbisāro nimantito svātanāya saddhiṃ balakāyena; api ca kho me mahāyañño paccupaṭṭhito. Atthi samaṇo gotamo sakyaputto sakyakulā pabbajito aṅguttarāpesu cārikaṃ {pb:M:0.0366} caramāno mahatā bhikkhusaṅghena saddhiṃ aḍḍhateḷasehi {pb:T:0.0441} bhikkhusatehi āpaṇaṃ anuppatto. Taṃ kho pana {pb:P:0.0106} bhavantaṃ gotamaṃ…pe… buddho bhagavāti. So me nimantito svātanāya bhattaṃ saddhiṃ bhikkhusaṅghenā’’ti. ‘‘Buddhoti, bho keṇiya, vadesi’’? ‘‘Buddhoti, bho sela, vadāmi’’. ‘‘Buddhoti, bho keṇiya, vadesi’’? ‘‘Buddhoti, bho sela, vadāmī’’ti.

Atha kho selassa brāhmaṇassa etadahosi – ‘‘ghosopi kho eso dullabho lokasmiṃ yadidaṃ buddhoti. Āgatāni kho panamhākaṃ mantesu dvattiṃsamahāpurisalakkhaṇāni, yehi samannāgatassa mahāpurisassa dveva gatiyo bhavanti anaññā. Sace agāraṃ ajjhāvasati rājā hoti cakkavatti dhammiko dhammarājā cāturanto vijitāvī janapadatthāvariyappatto sattaratanasamannāgato. Tassimāni satta ratanāni bhavanti, seyyathidaṃ – cakkaratanaṃ, hatthiratanaṃ, assaratanaṃ, maṇiratanaṃ, itthiratanaṃ, gahapatiratanaṃ, pariṇāyakaratanameva sattamaṃ. Parosahassaṃ kho panassa puttā bhavanti sūrā vīraṅgarūpā parasenappamaddanā. So imaṃ pathaviṃ sāgarapariyantaṃ adaṇḍena asatthena dhammena abhivijiya ajjhāvasati. Sace kho pana agārasmā anagāriyaṃ pabbajati, arahaṃ hoti sammāsambuddho loke vivaṭṭacchado {note:vivattacchaddo (sī. pī.)}. Kahaṃ pana, bho keṇiya, etarahi so bhavaṃ gotamo viharati {pb:T:0.0442} arahaṃ sammāsambuddho’’ti?

Evaṃ {pb:V:0.0167} vutte, keṇiyo jaṭilo dakkhiṇaṃ bāhuṃ paggahetvā selaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘yenesā{pb:P:0.0107}, bho sela, nīlavanarājī’’ti. Atha kho selo brāhmaṇo tīhi māṇavakasatehi saddhiṃ yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami. Atha kho selo brāhmaṇo te māṇavake āmantesi – ‘‘appasaddā bhonto āgacchantu, pade padaṃ nikkhipantā. Durāsadā hi te bhagavanto {note:bhavanto (syā. ka.)} sīhāva ekacarā. Yadā cāhaṃ, bho, samaṇena gotamena saddhiṃ manteyyuṃ, mā me bhonto antarantarā kathaṃ opātetha; kathāpariyosānaṃ me bhavanto āgamentū’’ti.

Atha kho selo brāhmaṇo yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavatā saddhiṃ sammodi. Sammodanīyaṃ kathaṃ sāraṇīyaṃ vītisāretvā ekamantaṃ nisīdi. Ekamantaṃ nisinno kho selo brāhmaṇo bhagavato {pb:M:0.0367} kāye dvattiṃsamahāpurisalakkhaṇāni samannesi {note:sammannesi (sī. syā.)}. Addasā kho selo brāhmaṇo bhagavato kāye dvattiṃsamahāpurisalakkhaṇāni yebhuyyena ṭhapetvā dve. Dvīsu mahāpurisalakkhaṇesu kaṅkhati vicikicchati nādhimuccati na sampasīdati – kosohite ca vatthaguyhe, pahūtajivhatāya cāti.

Atha kho bhagavato etadahosi – ‘‘passati kho me ayaṃ selo brāhmaṇo dvattiṃsamahāpurisalakkhaṇāni yebhuyyena ṭhapetvā dve. Dvīsu mahāpurisalakkhaṇesu kaṅkhati vicikicchati nādhimuccati na sampasīdati – kosohite ca vatthaguyhe, pahūtajivhatāya {pb:T:0.0443} cā’’ti. Atha kho bhagavā tathārūpaṃ iddhābhisaṅkhāraṃ abhisaṅkhāsi {note:abhisaṅkhāresi (syā. ka.)}, yathā addasa selo brāhmaṇo bhagavato kosohitaṃ vatthaguyhaṃ{pb:P:0.0108}. Atha kho bhagavā jivhaṃ ninnāmetvā ubhopi kaṇṇasotāni anumasi paṭimasi, ubhopi nāsikasotāni anumasi paṭimasi, kevalampi nalāṭamaṇḍalaṃ jivhāya chādesi.

Atha kho selassa brāhmaṇassa etadahosi – ‘‘samannāgato kho samaṇo gotamo dvattiṃsamahāpurisalakkhaṇehi paripuṇṇehi, no apuripuṇṇehi. No ca kho naṃ jānāmi buddho vā no vā. Sutaṃ kho pana metaṃ brāhmaṇānaṃ vuḍḍhānaṃ mahallakānaṃ ācariyapācariyānaṃ bhāsamānānaṃ – ‘ye te bhavanti arahanto sammāsambuddhā, te sake vaṇṇe bhaññamāne attānaṃ pātukarontī’ti. Yaṃnūnāhaṃ samaṇaṃ gotamaṃ sammukhā sāruppāhi gāthāhi abhitthaveyya’’nti. Atha kho selo brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ sammukhā sāruppāhi gāthāhi abhitthavi –

::hangnum
553\.

571\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Brāhmaṇā tisatā ime, yācanti pañjalīkatā;
::

::gathalast
Brahmacariyaṃ carissāma, bhagavā tava santike’’.

::hangnum
572\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svākkhātaṃ brahmacariyaṃ, (selāti bhagavā) sandiṭṭhikamakālikaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yattha amoghā pabbajjā, appamattassa sikkhato’’ti.
::

Alattha kho selo brāhmaṇo sapariso bhagavato santike pabbajjaṃ, alattha upasampadaṃ. Atha kho keṇiyo jaṭilo tassā {pb:T:0.0446} rattiyā accayena sake assame paṇītaṃ khādanīyaṃ bhojanīyaṃ paṭiyādāpetvā bhagavato {pb:P:0.0111} kālaṃ ārocāpesi – ‘‘kālo, bho gotama, niṭṭhitaṃ bhatta’’nti{pb:V:0.0170}. Atha kho bhagavā pubbaṇhasamayaṃ nivāsetvā pattacīvaramādāya yena keṇiyassa jaṭilassa assamo tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā paññatte āsane nisīdi saddhiṃ bhikkhusaṅghena.

Atha {pb:M:0.0370} kho keṇiyo jaṭilo buddhappamukhaṃ bhikkhusaṅghaṃ paṇītena khādanīyena bhojanīyena sahatthā santappesi sampavāresi. Atha kho keṇiyo jaṭilo bhagavantaṃ bhuttāviṃ onītapattapāṇiṃ aññataraṃ nīcaṃ āsanaṃ gahetvā ekamantaṃ nisīdi. Ekamantaṃ nisinnaṃ kho keṇiyaṃ jaṭilaṃ bhagavā imāhi gāthāhi anumodi –

::hangnum
573\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aggihuttamukhā yaññā, sāvittī chandaso mukhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Rājā mukhaṃ manussānaṃ, nadīnaṃ sāgaro mukhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
574\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nakkhattānaṃ mukhaṃ cando, ādicco tapataṃ mukhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Puññaṃ ākaṅkhamānānaṃ, saṅgho ve yajataṃ mukha’’nti.
::

Atha kho bhagavā keṇiyaṃ jaṭilaṃ imāhi gāthāhi anumoditvā uṭṭhāyāsanā pakkāmi. Atha kho āyasmā selo sapariso eko vūpakaṭṭho appamatto ātāpī pahitatto viharanto nacirasse {pb:P:0.0112} …pe… {pb:T:0.0447} aññataro kho panāpasmā selo sapariso arahataṃ ahosi.

Atha kho āyasmā selo sapariso yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami, upasaṅkamitvā ekaṃsaṃ cīvaraṃ katvā yena bhagavā tenañjaliṃ paṇāmetvā bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::hangnum
575\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ taṃ saraṇamāgamha {note:māgamma (sī. syā. ka.)}, ito aṭṭhami cakkhuma;
::

::gathalast
Sattarattena bhagavā, dantamha tava sāsane.
::

::hangnum
576\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tuvaṃ buddho tuvaṃ satthā, tuvaṃ mārābhibhū muni;
::

::gathalast
Tuvaṃ anusaye chetvā, tiṇṇo tāresimaṃ pajaṃ.
::

::hangnum
577\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upadhī te samatikkantā, āsavā te padālitā;
::

::gathalast
Sīhosi {note:sīhova (ma. ni. 2.401)} anupādāno, pahīnabhayabheravo.
::

::hangnum
578\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhikkhavo {pb:V:0.0171} tisatā ime, tiṭṭhanti pañjalīkatā;
::

::gathalast
Pāde vīra pasārehi, nāgā vandantu satthuno’’ti.
::

::centre
Selasuttaṃ sattamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

#### 8. Sallasuttaṃ

::hangnum
579\.
::

::gatha1
Animittamanaññātaṃ{pb:M:0.0371}, maccānaṃ idha jīvitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kasirañca parittañca, tañca dukkhena saṃyutaṃ.
::

::hangnum
580\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:P:0.0113} hi so upakkamo atthi, yena jātā na miyyare;
::

::gathalast
Jarampi {pb:T:0.0448} patvā maraṇaṃ, evaṃdhammā hi pāṇino.
::

::hangnum
581\.
::

::gatha1
Phalānamiva pakkānaṃ, pāto patanato {note:papatato (sī. pī. aṭṭha.)} bhayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ jātāna maccānaṃ, niccaṃ maraṇato bhayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
582\.
::

::gatha1
Yathāpi kumbhakārassa, katā mattikabhājanā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe bhedanapariyantā {note:bhedapariyantā (syā.)}, evaṃ maccāna jīvitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
583\.
::

::gatha1
Daharā ca mahantā ca, ye bālā ye ca paṇḍitā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe maccuvasaṃ yanti, sabbe maccuparāyaṇā.
::

::hangnum
584\.
::

::gatha1
Tesaṃ maccuparetānaṃ, gacchataṃ paralokato;
::

::gathalast
Na pitā tāyate puttaṃ, ñātī vā pana ñātake.
::

::hangnum
585\.
::

::gatha1
Pekkhataṃ yeva ñātīnaṃ, passa lālapataṃ puthu;
::

::gathalast
Ekamekova maccānaṃ, govajjho viya nīyati {note:niyyati (bahūsu)}.
::

::hangnum
586\.
::

::gatha1
Evamabbhāhato {pb:V:0.0172} loko, maccunā ca jarāya ca;
::

::gathalast
Tasmā dhīrā na socanti, viditvā lokapariyāyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
587\.
::

::gatha1
Yassa maggaṃ na jānāsi, āgatassa gatassa vā;
::

::gathalast
Ubho ante asampassaṃ, niratthaṃ paridevasi.
::

::hangnum
588\.
::

::gatha1
Paridevayamāno ce, kiñcidatthaṃ udabbahe;
::

::gathalast
Sammūḷho hiṃsamattānaṃ, kayirā ce naṃ vicakkhaṇo.
::

::hangnum
589\.
::

::gatha1
Na hi ruṇṇena sokena, santiṃ pappoti cetaso;
::

::gathalast
Bhiyyassuppajjate dukkhaṃ, sarīraṃ cupahaññati.
::

::hangnum
590\.
::

::gatha1
Kiso {pb:P:0.0114} vivaṇṇo bhavati, hiṃsamattānamattanā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
591\.
::

::gatha1
Sokamappajahaṃ {pb:M:0.0372} jantu, bhiyyo dukkhaṃ nigacchati;
::

::gathalast
Anutthunanto kālaṅkataṃ {note:kālakataṃ (sī. syā.)}, sokassa vasamanvagū.

::hangnum
592\.
::

::gatha1
Aññepi passa gamine, yathākammūpage nare;

::gathalast
Maccuno vasamāgamma, phandantevidha pāṇino.
::

::hangnum
593\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
594\.

::gatha1

::

::hangnum

::hangnum

598\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::centre
Sallasuttaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

#### 9. Vāseṭṭhasuttaṃ

Evaṃ {pb:P:0.0115}{pb:T:0.0450} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā icchānaṅgale viharati icchānaṅgalavanasaṇḍe. Tena kho pana samayena sambahulā abhiññātā abhiññātā brāhmaṇamahāsālā icchānaṅgale paṭivasanti, seyyathidaṃ – caṅkī brāhmaṇo, tārukkho brāhmaṇo, pokkharasāti brāhmaṇo, jāṇussoṇi {note:jāṇusoṇi (ka.)} brāhmaṇo, todeyyo brāhmaṇo, aññe ca abhiññātā abhiññātā brāhmaṇamahāsālā. Atha kho vāseṭṭhabhāradvājānaṃ māṇavānaṃ {pb:M:0.0373} jaṅghāvihāraṃ anucaṅkamantānaṃ anuvicarantānaṃ {note:anucaṅkamamānānaṃ anuvicaramānānaṃ (sī. pī.)} ayamantarākathā udapādi – ‘‘kathaṃ, bho, brāhmaṇo hotī’’ti?

Bhāradvājo māṇavo evamāha – ‘‘yato kho, bho, ubhato sujāto hoti mātito ca pitito ca saṃsuddhagahaṇiko yāva sattamā pitāmahayugā akkhitto anupakkuṭṭho jātivādena, ettāvatā kho bho brāhmaṇo hotī’’ti.

Vāseṭṭho māṇavo evamāha – ‘‘yato kho, bho, sīlavā ca hoti vatasampanno {note:vattasampanno (sī. syā. ma. ni. 2.454)} ca, ettāvatā kho, bho, brāhmaṇo hotī’’ti. Neva kho asakkhi bhāradvājo māṇavo vāseṭṭhaṃ {pb:P:0.0116} māṇavaṃ saññāpetuṃ, na pana asakkhi vāseṭṭho māṇavo bhāradvājaṃ māṇavaṃ saññāpetuṃ.

Atha {pb:V:0.0174} kho vāseṭṭho māṇavo bhāradvājaṃ māṇavaṃ āmantesi – ‘‘ayaṃ kho, bho {note:ayaṃ bho (sī. syā. ka.), ayaṃ kho (pī.)} bhāradvāja, samaṇo gotamo sakyaputto sakyakulā {pb:T:0.0451} pabbajito icchānaṅgale viharati icchānaṅgalavanasaṇḍe; taṃ kho pana bhavantaṃ gotamaṃ evaṃ kalyāṇo kittisaddo abbhuggato – ‘itipi…pe… buddho bhagavā’ti. Āyāma, bho bhāradvāja, yena samaṇo gotamo tenupasaṅkamissāma; upasaṅkamitvā samaṇaṃ gotamaṃ etamatthaṃ pucchissāma. Yathā no samaṇo gotamo byākarissati tathā naṃ dhāressāmā’’ti. ‘‘Evaṃ, bho’’ti kho bhāradvājo māṇavo vāseṭṭhassa māṇavassa paccassosi.

Atha kho vāseṭṭhabhāradvājā māṇavā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkamiṃsu; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavatā saddhiṃ sammodiṃsu. Sammodanīyaṃ kathaṃ sāraṇīyaṃ vītisāretvā ekamantaṃ nisīdiṃsu. Ekamantaṃ nisinno kho vāseṭṭho māṇavo bhagavantaṃ gāthāhi ajjhabhāsi –

::hangnum
599\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anuññātapaṭiññātā, tevijjā mayamasmubho;
::

::gathalast
Ahaṃ pokkharasātissa, tārukkhassāyaṃ māṇavo.
::

::hangnum
600\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tevijjānaṃ yadakkhātaṃ, tatra kevalinosmase;
::

::gathalast
Padakasma veyyākaraṇā, jappe ācariyasādisā.
::

::hangnum
601\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tesaṃ {pb:M:0.0374}{pb:P:0.0117} no jātivādasmiṃ, vivādo atthi gotama;
::

::gatha2
Jātiyā brāhmaṇo hoti, bhāradvājo iti bhāsati;
::

::gathalast
Ahañca kammunā {note:kammanā (sī. pī.) evamuparipi} brūmi, evaṃ jānāhi cakkhuma.
::

::hangnum
602\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Te na sakkoma saññāpetuṃ, aññamaññaṃ mayaṃ ubho;
::

::gathalast

::gathalast

::gatha1
‘‘Candaṃva vimalaṃ suddhaṃ, vippasannamanāvilaṃ;
::

Atho jātikkhayaṃ patto, tamahaṃ brūmi brāhmaṇaṃ.

Evaṃ vutte, vāseṭṭhabhāradvājā māṇavā bhagavantaṃ etadavocuṃ – ‘‘abhikkantaṃ, bho gotama…pe… upāsake no bhavaṃ gotamo dhāretu ajjatagge pāṇupete {note:pāṇupetaṃ (ka.)} saraṇaṃ gate’’ti.

::centre
Vāseṭṭhasuttaṃ navamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

#### 10. Kokālikasuttaṃ

Evaṃ {pb:V:0.0181} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. Atha kho kokāliko bhikkhu yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ {pb:P:0.0124} abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ nisīdi. Ekamantaṃ nisinno kho kokāliko bhikkhu bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘pāpicchā, bhante, sāriputtamoggallānā, pāpikānaṃ icchānaṃ vasaṃ gatā’’ti.

Evaṃ vutte, bhagavā kokālikaṃ bhikkhuṃ etadavoca – ‘‘mā hevaṃ, kokālika, mā hevaṃ, kokālika! Pasādehi, kokālika, sāriputtamoggallānesu cittaṃ. Pesalā sāriputtamoggallānā’’ti.

Dutiyampi kho…pe… {pb:T:0.0459} tatiyampi kho kokāliko bhikkhu bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘kiñcāpi me, bhante, bhagavā saddhāyiko paccayiko, atha kho pāpicchāva sāriputtamoggallānā, pāpikānaṃ icchānaṃ vasaṃ gatā’’ti. Tatiyampi kho bhagavā kokālikaṃ bhikkhuṃ etadavoca – ‘‘mā hevaṃ, kokālika{pb:M:0.0380}, mā hevaṃ, kokālika! Pasādehi, kokālika, sāriputtamoggallānesu cittaṃ. Pesalā sāriputtamoggallānā’’ti.

Atha kho kokāliko bhikkhu uṭṭhāyāsanā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā padakkhiṇaṃ katvā pakkāmi. Acirappakkantassa ca kokālikassa bhikkhuno sāsapamattīhi piḷakāhi sabbo kāyo phuṭo {note:phuṭṭho (syā.)} ahosi; sāsapamattiyo hutvā muggamattiyo ahesuṃ; muggamattiyo hutvā kaḷāyamattiyo ahesuṃ; kaḷāyamattiyo hutvā kolaṭṭhimattiyo ahesuṃ; kolaṭṭhimattiyo {pb:P:0.0125} hutvā kolamattiyo ahesuṃ; kolamattiyo hutvā āmalakamattiyo ahesuṃ; āmalakamattiyo hutvā beḷuvasalāṭukamattiyo ahesuṃ; beḷuvasalāṭukamattiyo hutvā billamattiyo ahesuṃ; billamattiyo hutvā pabhijjiṃsu; pubbañca lohitañca pagghariṃsu. Atha kho kokāliko bhikkhu tenevābādhena kālamakāsi. Kālaṅkato ca kokāliko bhikkhu padumaṃ nirayaṃ upapajji sāriputtamoggallānesu cittaṃ āghātetvā{pb:T:0.0460}.

Atha kho brahmā sahampati abhikkantāya rattiyā abhikkantavaṇṇo kevalakappaṃ jetavanaṃ obhāsetvā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhāsi{pb:V:0.0182}. Ekamantaṃ, ṭhito kho brahmā sahampati bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘kokāliko, bhante, bhikkhu kālaṅkato; kālaṅkato ca, bhante, kokāliko bhikkhu padumaṃ nirayaṃ upapanno sāriputtamoggallānesu cittaṃ āghātetvā’’ti. Idamavoca brahmā sahampati; idaṃ vatvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā padakkhiṇaṃ katvā tatthevantaradhāyi.

Atha kho bhagavā tassā rattiyā accayena bhikkhū āmantesi – ‘‘imaṃ, bhikkhave, rattiṃ brahmā sahampati abhikkantāya rattiyā…pe… idamavoca, bhikkhave, brahmā sahampati, idaṃ vatvā maṃ padakkhiṇaṃ katvā tatthevantaradhāyī’’ti.

Evaṃ vutte, aññataro bhikkhu bhagavantaṃ {pb:P:0.0126} etadavoca – ‘‘kīvadīghaṃ nu kho, bhante, padume niraye āyuppamāṇa’’nti? ‘‘Dīghaṃ kho, bhikkhu, padume niraye āyuppamāṇaṃ; taṃ na sukaraṃ saṅkhātuṃ ettakāni vassāni iti vā ettakāni vassasatāni iti vā ettakāni vassasahassāni {pb:M:0.0381} iti vā ettakāni vassasatasahassāni iti vā’’ti. ‘‘Sakkā pana, bhante, upamā {note:upamaṃ (sī. syā. ka.)} kātu’’nti? ‘‘Sakkā, bhikkhū’’ti bhagavā avoca –

‘‘Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsatikhāriko kosalako tilavāho; tato puriso vassasatassa vassasatassa accayena ekamekaṃ tilaṃ uddhareyya. Khippataraṃ kho so bhikkhu vīsatikhāriko kosalako tilavāho {pb:T:0.0461} iminā upakkamena parikkhayaṃ pariyādānaṃ gaccheyya, natveva eko abbudo nirayo. Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsati abbudā nirayā evameko nirabbudo nirayo. Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsati nirabbudā nirayā evameko ababo nirayo. Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsati ababā nirayā evameko ahaho nirayo. Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsati ahahā nirayā evameko aṭaṭo nirayo. Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsati aṭaṭā nirayā evameko kumudo nirayo. Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsati kumudā nirayā evameko sogandhiko nirayo. Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsati sogandhikā nirayā evameko uppalako nirayo. Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsati uppalakā nirayā evameko puṇḍarīko nirayo. Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsati puṇḍarīkā nirayā evameko padumo nirayo. Padumaṃ kho pana bhikkhu nirayaṃ kokāliko bhikkhu upapanno sāriputtamoggallānesu cittaṃ āghātetvā’’ti. Idamavoca bhagavā, idaṃ vatvāna sugato athāparaṃ etadavoca satthā –

::hangnum

#### 11. Nālakasuttaṃ

::hangnum
684\.
::

::gatha1
Ānandajāte tidasagaṇe patīte, sakkañca indaṃ sucivasane ca deve;
::

::gathalast
Dussaṃ gahetvā atiriva thomayante, asito isi addasa divāvihāre.
::

::hangnum
685\.
::

::gatha1
Disvāna {pb:P:0.0132} deve muditamane udagge, cittiṃ karitvāna idamavoca {note:karitvā idamavocāsi (sī.)} tattha;
::

::gathalast
‘‘Kiṃ devasaṅgho atiriva kalyarūpo, dussaṃ gahetvā ramayatha {note:bhamayatha (sī.)} kiṃ paṭicca.
::

::hangnum
686\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yadāpi āsī asurehi saṅgamo, jayo surānaṃ asurā parājitā.
::

::gathalast
Tadāpi netādiso lomahaṃsano, kimabbhutaṃ daṭṭhu marū pamoditā.
::

::hangnum
687\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Seḷenti gāyanti ca vādayanti ca, bhujāni phoṭenti {note:poṭhenti (sī. pī.), pothenti (ka.)} ca naccayanti ca;
::

::gathalast
Pucchāmi {pb:T:0.0467} vohaṃ merumuddhavāsine, dhunātha me saṃsayaṃ khippa mārisā’’.
::

::hangnum
688\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So {pb:M:0.0386} bodhisatto ratanavaro atulyo, manussaloke hitasukhatthāya {note:hitasukhatāya (sī. syā. pī.)} jāto;
::

::gathalast
Sakyāna gāme janapade lumbineyye, tenamha tuṭṭhā atiriva kalyarūpā.
::

::hangnum
689\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So sabbasattuttamo aggapuggalo, narāsabho sabbapajānamuttamo;
::

::gathalast
Vattessati {pb:P:0.0133} cakkamisivhaye vane, nadaṃva sīho balavā migābhibhū’’.
::

::hangnum
690\.
::

::gatha1
Taṃ {pb:V:0.0186} saddaṃ sutvā turitamavasarī so, suddhodanassa tada bhavanaṃ upāvisi {note:upāgami (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Nisajja tattha idamavocāsi sakye, ‘‘kuhiṃ kumāro ahamapi daṭṭhukāmo’’.
::

::hangnum
691\.
::

::gatha1
Tato kumāraṃ jalitamiva suvaṇṇaṃ, ukkāmukheva sukusalasampahaṭṭhaṃ {note:sukusalena sampahaṭṭhaṃ (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Daddallamānaṃ {note:daddaḷhamānaṃ (ka.)} siriyā anomavaṇṇaṃ, dassesu puttaṃ asitavhayassa sakyā.
::

::hangnum
692\.
::

::gatha1
Disvā kumāraṃ sikhimiva pajjalantaṃ, tārāsabhaṃva {pb:T:0.0468} nabhasigamaṃ visuddhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sūriyaṃ tapantaṃ saradarivabbhamuttaṃ, ānandajāto vipulamalattha pītiṃ.
::

::hangnum
693\.
::

::gatha1
Anekasākhañca sahassamaṇḍalaṃ, chattaṃ marū dhārayumantalikkhe;
::

::gathalast
Suvaṇṇadaṇḍā vītipatanti cāmarā, na dissare cāmarachattagāhakā.
::

::hangnum
694\.
::

::gatha1
Disvā {pb:M:0.0387}{pb:P:0.0134} jaṭī kaṇhasirivhayo isi, suvaṇṇanikkhaṃ viya paṇḍukambale;
::

::gathalast
Setañca chattaṃ dhariyanta {note:dhāriyanta (syā.), dhārayantaṃ (sī. ka.)} muddhani, udaggacitto sumano paṭiggahe.
::

::hangnum
695\.
::

::gatha1
Paṭiggahetvā pana sakyapuṅgavaṃ, jigīsato {note:jigiṃsako (sī. syā. pī.)} lakkhaṇamantapāragū;
::

::gathalast
Pasannacitto giramabbhudīrayi, ‘‘anuttarāyaṃ dvipadānamuttamo’’ {note:dipadānamuttamo (sī. syā. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
696\.
::

::gatha1
Athattano gamanamanussaranto, akalyarūpo gaḷayati assukāni;
::

::gatha2
Disvāna sakyā isimavocuṃ rudantaṃ,
::

::gathalast
‘‘No ce kumāre bhavissati antarāyo’’.
::

::hangnum
697\.
::

::gatha1
Disvāna sakye isimavoca akalye, ‘‘nāhaṃ {pb:T:0.0469} kumāre ahitamanussarāmi;
::

::gathalast
Na cāpimassa bhavissati antarāyo, na orakāyaṃ adhimānasā {note:adhimanasā (sī. syā.)} bhavātha.
::

::hangnum
698\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sambodhiyaggaṃ phusissatāyaṃ kumāro, so dhammacakkaṃ paramavisuddhadassī;
::

::gathalast
Vattessatāyaṃ bahujanahitānukampī, vitthārikassa bhavissati brahmacariyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
699\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mamañca {pb:P:0.0135} āyu na ciramidhāvaseso, athantarā me bhavissati kālakiriyā;
::

::gathalast
Sohaṃ na sossaṃ {note:sussaṃ (sī. syā.)} asamadhurassa dhammaṃ, tenamhi aṭṭo byasanaṃgato aghāvī’’.
::

::hangnum
700\.
::

::gatha1
So {pb:M:0.0388}{pb:V:0.0187} sākiyānaṃ vipulaṃ janetvā pītiṃ, antepuramhā niggamā {note:niragamā (sī. syā.), nigamā (ka. sī.), niragama (pī.)} brahmacārī;
::

::gathalast
So bhāgineyyaṃ sayaṃ anukampamāno, samādapesi asamadhurassa dhamme.
::

::hangnum
701\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Buddhoti ghosaṃ yada {note:yadi (syā. ka.)} parato suṇāsi, sambodhipatto vivarati dhammamaggaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Gantvāna tattha samayaṃ paripucchamāno {note:sayaṃ paripucchiyāno (sī. syā.)}, carassu tasmiṃ bhagavati brahmacariyaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
702\.
::

::gatha1
Tenānusiṭṭho hitamanena tādinā, anāgate {pb:T:0.0470} paramavisuddhadassinā;
::

::gathalast
So nālako upacitapuññasañcayo, jinaṃ patikkhaṃ {note:pati + ikkhaṃ = patikkhaṃ} parivasi rakkhitindriyo.
::

::hangnum
703\.
::

::gatha1
Sutvāna ghosaṃ jinavaracakkavattane, gantvāna disvā isinisabhaṃ pasanno;
::

::gathalast
Moneyyaseṭṭhaṃ {pb:P:0.0136} munipavaraṃ apucchi, samāgate asitāvhayassa sāsaneti.
::

::centre
Vatthugāthā niṭṭhitā.
::

::hangnum
704\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aññātametaṃ vacanaṃ, asitassa yathātathaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ taṃ gotama pucchāmi, sabbadhammāna pāraguṃ.
::

::hangnum
705\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anagāriyupetassa, bhikkhācariyaṃ jigīsato;
::

::gathalast
Muni pabrūhi me puṭṭho, moneyyaṃ uttamaṃ padaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
706\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Moneyyaṃ te upaññissaṃ, (iti bhagavā) dukkaraṃ durabhisambhavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Handa te naṃ pavakkhāmi, santhambhassu daḷho bhava.
::

::hangnum
707\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samānabhāgaṃ {pb:M:0.0389} kubbetha, gāme akkuṭṭhavanditaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Manopadosaṃ rakkheyya, santo anuṇṇato care.
::

::hangnum
708\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
