::

::hangnum
709\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Virato methunā dhammā, hitvā kāme paropare {note:parovare (sī. pī.), varāvare (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Aviruddho {pb:T:0.0471} asāratto, pāṇesu tasathāvare.
::

::hangnum
710\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yathā ahaṃ tathā ete, yathā ete tathā ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Attānaṃ upamaṃ katvā, na haneyya na ghātaye.
::

::hangnum
711\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Hitvā icchañca lobhañca, yattha satto puthujjano;
::

::gathalast
Cakkhumā paṭipajjeyya, tareyya narakaṃ imaṃ.
::

::hangnum
712\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ūnūdaro mitāhāro, appicchassa alolupo;
::

::gathalast
Sadā {note:sa ve (pī.)} icchāya nicchāto, aniccho hoti nibbuto.
::

::hangnum
713\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sa piṇḍacāraṃ caritvā, vanantamabhihāraye;
::

::gathalast
Upaṭṭhito rukkhamūlasmiṃ, āsanūpagato muni.
::

::hangnum
714\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sa jhānapasuto dhīro, vanante ramito siyā;
::

::gathalast
Jhāyetha rukkhamūlasmiṃ, attānamabhitosayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
715\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato ratyā vivasāne {note:vivasane (sī. syā. pī.)}, gāmantamabhihāraye;
::

::gathalast
Avhānaṃ nābhinandeyya, abhihārañca gāmato.
::

::hangnum
716\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na munī gāmamāgamma, kulesu sahasā care;
::

::gathalast
Ghāsesanaṃ chinnakatho, na vācaṃ payutaṃ bhaṇe.
::

::hangnum
717\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Alatthaṃ yadidaṃ sādhu, nālatthaṃ kusalaṃ iti;
::

::gathalast
Ubhayeneva so tādī, rukkhaṃvupanivattati {note:rukkhaṃvu’pativattati (ka.), rukkhaṃva upātivattati (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
718\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sa {pb:V:0.0189}{pb:P:0.0138} pattapāṇi vicaranto, amūgo mūgasammato;
::

::gathalast
Appaṃ dānaṃ na hīḷeyya, dātāraṃ nāvajāniyā.
::

::hangnum
719\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uccāvacā {pb:M:0.0390} hi paṭipadā, samaṇena pakāsitā;
::

::gathalast
Na pāraṃ {pb:T:0.0472} diguṇaṃ yanti, nayidaṃ ekaguṇaṃ mutaṃ.
::

::hangnum
720\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yassa ca visatā natthi, chinnasotassa bhikkhuno;
::

::gathalast
Kiccākiccappahīnassa, pariḷāho na vijjati.
::

::hangnum
721\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Moneyyaṃ te upaññissaṃ, khuradhārūpamo bhave;
::

::gathalast
Jivhāya tālumāhacca, udare saññato siyā.
::

::hangnum
722\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Alīnacitto ca siyā, na cāpi bahu cintaye;
::

::gathalast
Nirāmagandho asito, brahmacariyaparāyaṇo.
::

::hangnum
723\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekāsanassa sikkhetha, samaṇūpāsanassa ca;
::

::gatha2
Ekattaṃ monamakkhātaṃ, eko ce abhiramissasi;
::

::gathalast
Atha bhāhisi {note:bhāsihi (sī. syā. pī.)} dasadisā.
::

::hangnum
724\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sutvā dhīrānaṃ nigghosaṃ, jhāyīnaṃ kāmacāginaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tato hiriñca saddhañca, bhiyyo kubbetha māmako.
::

::hangnum
725\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ {pb:P:0.0139} nadīhi vijānātha, sobbhesu padaresu ca;
::

::gathalast
Saṇantā yanti kusobbhā {note:kussubbhā (sī.)}, tuṇhīyanti mahodadhī.
::

::hangnum
726\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yadūnakaṃ taṃ saṇati, yaṃ pūraṃ santameva taṃ;
::

::gathalast
Aḍḍhakumbhūpamo bālo, rahado pūrova paṇḍito.
::

::hangnum
727\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ samaṇo bahuṃ bhāsati, upetaṃ atthasañhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Jānaṃ so dhammaṃ deseti, jānaṃ so bahu bhāsati.
::

::hangnum
728\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo {pb:V:0.0190} ca jānaṃ saṃyatatto, jānaṃ na bahu bhāsati;
::

::gathalast
Sa {pb:T:0.0473} munī monamarahati, sa munī monamajjhagā’’ti.
::

::centre
Nālakasuttaṃ ekādasamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

#### 12. Dvayatānupassanāsuttaṃ

Evaṃ me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati pubbārāme migāramātupāsāde. Tena kho pana samayena bhagavā tadahuposathe pannarase {pb:M:0.0391} puṇṇāya puṇṇamāya rattiyā bhikkhusaṅghaparivuto abbhokāse nisinno hoti{pb:P:0.0140}. Atha kho bhagavā tuṇhībhūtaṃ tuṇhībhūtaṃ bhikkhusaṅghaṃ anuviloketvā bhikkhū āmantesi –

‘‘‘Ye te, bhikkhave, kusalā dhammā ariyā niyyānikā sambodhagāmino, tesaṃ vo, bhikkhave, kusalānaṃ dhammānaṃ ariyānaṃ niyyānikānaṃ sambodhagāmīnaṃ kā upanisā savanāyā’ti iti ce, bhikkhave, pucchitāro assu, te evamassu vacanīyā – ‘yāvadeva dvayatānaṃ dhammānaṃ yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇāyā’ti. Kiñca dvayataṃ vadetha?

(1) ‘‘Idaṃ dukkhaṃ, ayaṃ dukkhasamudayoti ayamekānupassanā. Ayaṃ dukkhanirodho, ayaṃ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadāti, ayaṃ dutiyānupassanā. Evaṃ sammā dvayatānupassino kho, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno appamattassa ātāpino pahitattassa viharato dvinnaṃ phalānaṃ aññataraṃ phalaṃ pāṭikaṅkhaṃ – diṭṭheva dhamme aññā, sati vā {pb:T:0.0474} upādisese anāgāmitā’’ti.

Idamavoca bhagavā. Idaṃ vatvāna sugato athāparaṃ etadavoca satthā –

::hangnum
729\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye dukkhaṃ nappajānanti, atho dukkhassa sambhavaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Yattha ca sabbaso dukkhaṃ, asesaṃ uparujjhati;
::

::gathalast
Tañca maggaṃ na jānanti, dukkhūpasamagāminaṃ.
::

::hangnum
730\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cetovimuttihīnā te, atho paññāvimuttiyā;
::

::gathalast
Abhabbā te antakiriyāya, te ve jātijarūpagā.
::

::hangnum
731\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye {pb:V:0.0191} ca dukkhaṃ pajānanti, atho dukkhassa sambhavaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Yattha ca sabbaso dukkhaṃ, asesaṃ uparujjhati;
::

::gathalast
Tañca {pb:P:0.0141} maggaṃ pajānanti, dukkhūpasamagāminaṃ.
::

::hangnum
732\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cetovimuttisampannā, atho paññāvimuttiyā;
::

::gathalast
Bhabbā te antakiriyāya, na te jātijarūpagā’’ti.
::

(2) ‘‘‘Siyā aññenapi pariyāyena sammā dvayatānupassanā’ti, iti ce, bhikkhave, pucchitāro assu; ‘siyā’tissu vacanīyā. Kathañca siyā? Yaṃ kiñci dukkhaṃ sambhoti sabbaṃ upadhipaccayāti, ayamekānupassanā. Upadhīnaṃ {pb:M:0.0392} tveva asesavirāganirodhā natthi dukkhassa sambhavoti, ayaṃ dutiyānupassanā. Evaṃ sammā…pe… athāparaṃ etadavoca satthā –

::hangnum
733\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upadhinidānā pabhavanti dukkhā, ye {pb:T:0.0475} keci lokasmimanekarūpā;
::

::gatha2
Yo ve avidvā upadhiṃ karoti, punappunaṃ dukkhamupeti mando;
::

::gathalast
Tasmā pajānaṃ upadhiṃ na kayirā, dukkhassa jātippabhavānupassī’’ti.
::

(3) ‘‘‘Siyā aññenapi pariyāyena sammā dvayatānupassanā’ti, iti ce, bhikkhave, pucchitāro assu; ‘siyā’tissu vacanīyā. Kathañca siyā? Yaṃ kiñci dukkhaṃ sambhoti sabbaṃ avijjāpaccayāti, ayamekānupassanā. Avijjāya tveva asesavirāganirodhā natthi dukkhassa sambhavoti, ayaṃ dutiyānupassanā. Evaṃ sammā…pe… athāparaṃ etadavoca satthā –

::hangnum
734\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jātimaraṇasaṃsāraṃ{pb:P:0.0142}, ye vajanti punappunaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Itthabhāvaññathābhāvaṃ, avijjāyeva sā gati.
::

::hangnum
735\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Avijjā hāyaṃ mahāmoho, yenidaṃ saṃsitaṃ ciraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vijjāgatā ca ye sattā, na te gacchanti {note:nāgacchanti (sī. pī.)} punabbhava’’nti.
::

(4) ‘‘Siyā aññenapi…pe… kathañca siyā? Yaṃ kiñci dukkhaṃ sambhoti sabbaṃ saṅkhārapaccayāti, ayamekānupassanā. Saṅkhārānaṃ tveva asesavirāganirodhā natthi dukkhassa sambhavoti, ayaṃ dutiyānupassanā. Evaṃ sammā…pe… athāparaṃ etadavoca satthā –

::hangnum
736\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ {pb:V:0.0192}{pb:T:0.0476} kiñci dukkhaṃ sambhoti, sabbaṃ saṅkhārapaccayā;
::

::gathalast
Saṅkhārānaṃ nirodhena, natthi dukkhassa sambhavo.
::

::hangnum
737\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Etamādīnavaṃ ñatvā, dukkhaṃ saṅkhārapaccayā;
::

::gatha2
Sabbasaṅkhārasamathā, saññānaṃ uparodhanā;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ dukkhakkhayo hoti, etaṃ ñatvā yathātathaṃ.
::

::hangnum
738\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sammaddasā vedaguno, sammadaññāya paṇḍitā;
::

::gathalast
Abhibhuyya mārasaṃyogaṃ, na gacchanti {note:nāgacchanti (sī. pī.)} punabbhava’’nti.
::

(5) ‘‘Siyā {pb:M:0.0393}{pb:P:0.0143} aññenapi…pe… kathañca siyā? Yaṃ kiñci dukkhaṃ sambhoti sabbaṃ viññāṇapaccayāti, ayamekānupassanā. Viññāṇassa tveva asesavirāganirodhā natthi dukkhassa sambhavoti, ayaṃ dutiyānupassanā. Evaṃ sammā…pe… athāparaṃ etadavoca satthā –

::hangnum
739\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ kiñci dukkhaṃ sambhoti, sabbaṃ viññāṇapaccayā;
::

::gathalast
Viññāṇassa nirodhena, natthi dukkhassa sambhavo.
::

::hangnum
740\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Etamādīnavaṃ ñatvā, dukkhaṃ viññāṇapaccayā;
::

::gathalast
Viññāṇūpasamā bhikkhu, nicchāto parinibbuto’’ti.
::

(6) ‘‘Siyā aññenapi…pe… kathañca siyā? Yaṃ kiñci dukkhaṃ sambhoti sabbaṃ phassapaccayāti, ayamekānupassanā. Phassassa tveva asesavirāganirodhā natthi dukkhassa sambhavoti, ayaṃ dutiyānupassanā. Evaṃ sammā…pe… athāparaṃ etadavoca {pb:T:0.0477} satthā –

::hangnum
741\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tesaṃ phassaparetānaṃ, bhavasotānusārinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kummaggapaṭipannānaṃ, ārā saṃyojanakkhayo.
::

::hangnum
742\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye ca phassaṃ pariññāya, aññāyupasame {note:paññāya upasame (syā.)} ratā;
::

::gathalast
Te ve phassābhisamayā, nicchātā parinibbutā’’ti.
::

(7) ‘‘Siyā {pb:V:0.0193} aññenapi…pe… kathañca siyā? Yaṃ kiñci dukkhaṃ sambhoti sabbaṃ vedanāpaccayāti, ayamekānupassanā. Vedanānaṃ tveva asesavirāganirodhā natthi dukkhassa sambhavoti, ayaṃ dutiyānupassanā. Evaṃ sammā…pe… athāparaṃ etadavoca satthā –

::hangnum
743\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sukhaṃ {pb:P:0.0144} vā yadi vā dukkhaṃ, adukkhamasukhaṃ saha;
::

::gathalast
Ajjhattañca bahiddhā ca, yaṃ kiñci atthi veditaṃ.
::

::hangnum
744\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Etaṃ dukkhanti ñatvāna, mosadhammaṃ palokinaṃ {note:palokitaṃ (sī.)};
::

::gatha2
Phussa phussa vayaṃ passaṃ, evaṃ tattha vijānati {note:virajjati (ka. sī.)};
::

::gathalast
Vedanānaṃ khayā bhikkhu, nicchāto parinibbuto’’ti.
::

(8) ‘‘Siyā {pb:M:0.0394} aññenapi…pe… kathañca siyā? Yaṃ kiñci dukkhaṃ sambhoti sabbaṃ taṇhāpaccayāti, ayamekānupassanā. Taṇhāya tveva asesavirāganirodhā natthi dukkhassa sambhavoti, ayaṃ dutiyānupassanā. Evaṃ sammā…pe… athāparaṃ etadavoca satthā –

::hangnum
745\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṇhādutiyo {pb:T:0.0478} puriso, dīghamaddhāna saṃsaraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Itthabhāvaññathābhāvaṃ, saṃsāraṃ nātivattati.
::

::hangnum
746\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Etamādīnavaṃ ñatvā, taṇhaṃ {note:taṇhā (bahūsu) itivuttake 15 passitabbaṃ} dukkhassa sambhavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vītataṇho anādāno, sato bhikkhu paribbaje’’ti.
::

(9) ‘‘Siyā aññenapi…pe… kathañca siyā? Yaṃ kiñci dukkhaṃ sambhoti sabbaṃ upādānapaccayāti, ayamekānupassanā. Upādānānaṃ {note:upādānassa (syā. ka.)} tveva asesavirāganirodhā natthi dukkhassa sambhavoti, ayaṃ dutiyānupassanā. Evaṃ sammā…pe… athāparaṃ etadavoca satthā –

::hangnum
747\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upādānapaccayā bhavo, bhūto dukkhaṃ nigacchati;
::

::gathalast
Jātassa maraṇaṃ hoti, eso dukkhassa sambhavo.
::

::hangnum
748\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tasmā upādānakkhayā, sammadaññāya paṇḍitā;
::

::gathalast
Jātikkhayaṃ abhiññāya, na gacchanti punabbhava’’nti.
::

(10) ‘‘Siyā {pb:V:0.0194}{pb:P:0.0145} aññenapi…pe… kathañca siyā? Yaṃ kiñci dukkhaṃ sambhoti sabbaṃ ārambhapaccayāti, ayamekānupassanā. Ārambhānaṃ tveva asesavirāganirodhā natthi dukkhassa sambhavoti, ayaṃ dutiyānupassanā. Evaṃ sammā…pe… athāparaṃ etadavoca satthā –

::hangnum
749\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ kiñci dukkhaṃ sambhoti, sabbaṃ ārambhapaccayā;
::

::gathalast
Ārambhānaṃ nirodhena, natthi dukkhassa sambhavo.
::

::hangnum
750\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Etamādīnavaṃ {pb:T:0.0479} ñatvā, dukkhaṃ ārambhapaccayā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbārambhaṃ paṭinissajja, anārambhe vimuttino.
::

::hangnum
751\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ucchinnabhavataṇhassa, santacittassa bhikkhuno;
::

::gathalast
Vikkhīṇo {note:vitiṇṇo (sī.)} jātisaṃsāro, natthi tassa punabbhavo’’ti.
::

(11) ‘‘Siyā {pb:M:0.0395} aññenapi…pe… kathañca siyā? Yaṃ kiñci dukkhaṃ sambhoti sabbaṃ āhārapaccayāti, ayamekānupassanā. Āhārānaṃ tveva asesavirāganirodhā natthi dukkhassa sambhavoti, ayaṃ dutiyānupassanā. Evaṃ sammā…pe… athāparaṃ etadavoca satthā –

::hangnum
752\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ kiñci dukkhaṃ sambhoti, sabbaṃ āhārapaccayā;
::

::gathalast
Āhārānaṃ nirodhena, natthi dukkhassa sambhavo.
::

::hangnum
753\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Etamādīnavaṃ ñatvā, dukkhaṃ āhārapaccayā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāhāraṃ pariññāya, sabbāhāramanissito.
::

::hangnum
754\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ārogyaṃ {pb:P:0.0146} sammadaññāya, āsavānaṃ parikkhayā;
::

::gathalast
Saṅkhāya sevī dhammaṭṭho, saṅkhyaṃ {note:saṅkhaṃ (sī. pī.)} nopeti vedagū’’ti.
::

(12) ‘‘Siyā aññenapi…pe… kathañca siyā? Yaṃ kiñci dukkhaṃ sambhoti sabbaṃ iñjitapaccayāti, ayamekānupassanā. Iñjitānaṃ tveva asesavirāganirodhā natthi dukkhassa sambhavoti, ayaṃ dutiyānupassanā. Evaṃ sammā…pe… athāparaṃ etadavoca satthā –

::hangnum
755\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ {pb:V:0.0195}{pb:T:0.0480} kiñci dukkhaṃ sambhoti, sabbaṃ iñjitapaccayā;
::

::gathalast
Iñjitānaṃ nirodhena, natthi dukkhassa sambhavo.
::

::hangnum
756\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Etamādīnavaṃ ñatvā, dukkhaṃ iñjitapaccayā;
::

::gatha2
Tasmā hi ejaṃ vossajja, saṅkhāre uparundhiya;
::

::gathalast
Anejo anupādāno, sato bhikkhu paribbaje’’ti.
::

(13) ‘‘Siyā aññenapi…pe… kathañca siyā? Nissitassa calitaṃ hotīti, ayamekānupassanā. Anissito na calatīti, ayaṃ dutiyānupassanā. Evaṃ sammā…pe… athāparaṃ etadavoca satthā –

::hangnum
757\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anissito na calati, nissito ca upādiyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Itthabhāvaññathābhāvaṃ, saṃsāraṃ nātivattati.
::

::hangnum
758\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Etamādīnavaṃ ñatvā, nissayesu mahabbhayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anissito anupādāno, sato bhikkhu paribbaje’’ti.
::

(14) ‘‘Siyā {pb:M:0.0396} aññenapi…pe… kathañca siyā? Rūpehi, bhikkhave, arūpā {note:āruppā (sī. pī.)} santatarāti, ayamekānupassanā. Arūpehi {pb:P:0.0147} nirodho santataroti, ayaṃ dutiyānupassanā. Evaṃ sammā…pe… athāparaṃ etadavoca satthā –

::hangnum
759\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye ca rūpūpagā sattā, ye ca arūpaṭṭhāyino {note:āruppavāsino (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Nirodhaṃ appajānantā, āgantāro punabbhavaṃ.
::

::hangnum
760\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye ca rūpe pariññāya, arūpesu asaṇṭhitā {note:susaṇṭhitā (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Nirodhe {pb:T:0.0481} ye vimuccanti, te janā maccuhāyino’’ti.
::

(15) ‘‘Siyā aññenapi…pe… kathañca siyā? Yaṃ, bhikkhave, sadevakassa lokassa samārakassa sabrahmakassa sassamaṇabrāhmaṇiyā pajāya sadevamanussāya idaṃ saccanti upanijjhāyitaṃ tadamariyānaṃ etaṃ musāti yathābhūtaṃ sammappaññāya sudiṭṭhaṃ, ayamekānupassanā. Yaṃ{pb:V:0.0196}, bhikkhave, sadevakassa…pe… sadevamanussāya idaṃ musāti upanijjhāyitaṃ, tadamariyānaṃ etaṃ saccanti yathābhūtaṃ sammappaññāya sudiṭṭhaṃ, ayaṃ dutiyānupassanā. Evaṃ sammā…pe… athāparaṃ etadavoca satthā –

::hangnum
761\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anattani attamāniṃ {note:attamānī (syā.), attamānaṃ (pī. ka.)}, passa lokaṃ sadevakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Niviṭṭhaṃ nāmarūpasmiṃ, idaṃ saccanti maññati.
::

::hangnum
762\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yena yena hi maññanti, tato taṃ hoti aññathā;
::

::gathalast
Tañhi tassa musā hoti, mosadhammañhi ittaraṃ.
::

::hangnum
763\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Amosadhammaṃ {pb:P:0.0148} nibbānaṃ, tadariyā saccato vidū;
::

::gathalast
Te ve saccābhisamayā, nicchātā parinibbutā’’ti.
::

(16) ‘‘‘Siyā aññenapi pariyāyena sammā dvayatānupassanā’ti, iti ce, bhikkhave, pucchitāro assu; ‘siyā’tissu vacanīyā. Kathañca siyā? Yaṃ, bhikkhave, sadevakassa lokassa samārakassa sabrahmakassa sassamaṇabrāhmaṇiyā pajāya sadevamanussāya idaṃ sukhanti upanijjhāyitaṃ, tadamariyānaṃ etaṃ dukkhanti yathābhūtaṃ sammappaññāya sudiṭṭhaṃ, ayamekānupassanā{pb:T:0.0482}. Yaṃ, bhikkhave, sadevakassa…pe… sadevamanussāya idaṃ dukkhanti upanijjhāyitaṃ tadamariyānaṃ etaṃ sukhanti yathābhūtaṃ sammappaññāya sudiṭṭhaṃ, ayaṃ {pb:M:0.0397} dutiyānupassanā. Evaṃ sammā dvayatānupassino kho, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno appamattassa ātāpino pahitattassa viharato dvinnaṃ phalānaṃ aññataraṃ phalaṃ pāṭikaṅkhaṃ – diṭṭheva dhamme aññā, sati vā upādisese anāgāmitāti. Idamavoca bhagavā. Idaṃ vatvāna sugato athāparaṃ etadavoca satthā –

::hangnum
764\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rūpā saddā rasā gandhā, phassā dhammā ca kevalā;
::

::gathalast
Iṭṭhā kantā manāpā ca, yāvatatthīti vuccati.
::

::hangnum
765\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sadevakassa lokassa, ete vo sukhasammatā;
::

::gathalast
Yattha cete nirujjhanti, taṃ nesaṃ dukkhasammataṃ.
::

::hangnum
766\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sukhanti {pb:V:0.0197} diṭṭhamariyehi, sakkāyassuparodhanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Paccanīkamidaṃ hoti, sabbalokena passataṃ.
::

::hangnum
767\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ {pb:P:0.0149} pare sukhato āhu, tadariyā āhu dukkhato;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ pare dukkhato āhu, tadariyā sukhato vidū.
::

::hangnum
768\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Passa dhammaṃ durājānaṃ, sampamūḷhetthaviddasu {note:sampamūḷhettha aviddasu (sī. pī.), sammūḷhettha aviddasu (?)};
::

::gathalast
Nivutānaṃ tamo hoti, andhakāro apassataṃ.
::

::hangnum
769\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satañca vivaṭaṃ hoti, āloko passatāmiva;
::

::gathalast
Santike na vijānanti, maggā dhammassa kovidā.
::

::hangnum
770\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhavarāgaparetehi{pb:T:0.0483}, bhavasotānusāribhi;
::

::gathalast
Māradheyyānupannehi, nāyaṃ dhammo susambudho.
::

::hangnum
771\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ko nu aññatramariyehi, padaṃ sambuddhumarahati;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ padaṃ sammadaññāya, parinibbanti anāsavā’’ti.
::

Idamavoca bhagavā. Attamanā te bhikkhū bhagavato bhāsitaṃ abhinandunti. Imasmiṃ ca {note:imasmiṃ kho (sī.)} pana veyyākaraṇasmiṃ bhaññamāne saṭṭhimattānaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ anupādāya āsavehi cittāni vimucciṃsūti.

::centre
Dvayatānupassanāsuttaṃ dvādasamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

Tassuddānaṃ {pb:P:0.0150} –

::gatha1
Saccaṃ {pb:M:0.0398} upadhi avijjā ca, saṅkhāre viññāṇapañcamaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Phassavedaniyā taṇhā, upādānārambhaāhārā;
::

::gathalast
Iñjitaṃ calitaṃ rūpaṃ, saccaṃ dukkhena soḷasāti.
::

::centre
Mahāvaggo tatiyo niṭṭhito.
::

Tassuddānaṃ {pb:V:0.0198} –

::gatha1
Pabbajjā ca padhānañca, subhāsitañca sundari;
::

::gathalast
Māghasuttaṃ sabhiyo ca, selo sallañca vuccati.
::

::gatha1
Vāseṭṭho cāpi kokāli, nālako dvayatānupassanā;
::

::gathalast
Dvādasetāni suttāni, mahāvaggoti vuccatīti.
::

### 4. Aṭṭhakavaggo

#### 1. Kāmasuttaṃ

::hangnum
772\.
::

::gatha1
Kāmaṃ {pb:M:0.0399}{pb:V:0.0199}{pb:P:0.0151}{pb:T:0.0484} kāmayamānassa, tassa ce taṃ samijjhati;
::

::gathalast
Addhā pītimano hoti, laddhā macco yadicchati.
::

::hangnum
773\.
::

::gatha1
Tassa ce kāmayānassa {note:kāmayamānassa (ka.)}, chandajātassa jantuno;
::

::gathalast
Te kāmā parihāyanti, sallaviddhova ruppati.
::

::hangnum
774\.
::

::gatha1
Yo kāme parivajjeti, sappasseva padā siro;
::

::gathalast
Somaṃ {note:so imaṃ (sī. pī.)} visattikaṃ loke, sato samativattati.
::

::hangnum
775\.
::

::gatha1
Khettaṃ vatthuṃ hiraññaṃ vā, gavassaṃ {note:gavāssaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} dāsaporisaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Thiyo bandhū puthu kāme, yo naro anugijjhati.
::

::hangnum
776\.
::

::gatha1
Abalā naṃ balīyanti, maddantenaṃ parissayā;
::

::gathalast
Tato naṃ dukkhamanveti, nāvaṃ bhinnamivodakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
777\.
::

::gatha1
Tasmā jantu sadā sato, kāmāni parivajjaye;
::

::gathalast
Te pahāya tare oghaṃ, nāvaṃ sitvāva {note:siñcitvā (sī.)} pāragūti.
::

::centre
Kāmasuttaṃ paṭhamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

#### 2. Guhaṭṭhakasuttaṃ

::hangnum
778\.
::

::gatha1
Satto {pb:V:0.0200}{pb:T:0.0485} guhāyaṃ bahunābhichanno, tiṭṭhaṃ naro mohanasmiṃ pagāḷho;
::

::gathalast
Dūre {pb:P:0.0152} vivekā hi tathāvidho so, kāmā hi loke na hi suppahāyā.
::

::hangnum
779\.
::

::gatha1
Icchānidānā {pb:M:0.0400} bhavasātabaddhā, te duppamuñcā na hi aññamokkhā;
::

::gathalast
Pacchā pure vāpi apekkhamānā, imeva kāme purimeva jappaṃ.
::

::hangnum
780\.
::

::gatha1
Kāmesu giddhā pasutā pamūḷhā, avadāniyā te visame niviṭṭhā;
::

::gathalast
Dukkhūpanītā paridevayanti, kiṃsū bhavissāma ito cutāse.
::

::hangnum
781\.
::

::gatha1
Tasmā hi sikkhetha idheva jantu, yaṃ kiñci jaññā visamanti loke;
::

::gathalast
Na tassa hetū visamaṃ careyya, appañhidaṃ jīvitamāhu dhīrā.
::

::hangnum
782\.
::

::gatha1
Passāmi loke pariphandamānaṃ, pajaṃ imaṃ taṇhagataṃ bhavesu;
::

::gathalast
Hīnā {pb:T:0.0486} narā maccumukhe lapanti, avītataṇhāse bhavābhavesu.
::

::hangnum
783\.
::

::gatha1
Mamāyite passatha phandamāne, maccheva appodake khīṇasote;
::

::gathalast
Etampi disvā amamo careyya, bhavesu āsattimakubbamāno.
::

::hangnum
784\.
::

::gatha1
Ubhosu antesu vineyya chandaṃ, phassaṃ pariññāya anānugiddho;
::

::gathalast
Yadattagarahī tadakubbamāno, na lippatī {note:na limpatī (syā. ka.)} diṭṭhasutesu dhīro.
::

::hangnum
785\.
::

::gatha1
Saññaṃ {pb:P:0.0153} pariññā vitareyya oghaṃ, pariggahesu muni nopalitto;
::

::gathalast
Abbūḷhasallo caramappamatto, nāsīsatī {note:nāsiṃsatī (sī. syā. pī.)} lokamimaṃ parañcāti.
::

::centre
Guhaṭṭhakasuttaṃ dutiyaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

#### 3. Duṭṭhaṭṭhakasuttaṃ

::hangnum
786\.
::

::gatha1
Vadanti {pb:M:0.0401}{pb:V:0.0201}{pb:T:0.0487} ve duṭṭhamanāpi eke, athopi ve saccamanā vadanti;
::

::gathalast
Vādañca jātaṃ muni no upeti, tasmā munī natthi khilo kuhiñci.
::

::hangnum
787\.
::

::gatha1
Sakañhi diṭṭhiṃ kathamaccayeyya, chandānunīto ruciyā niviṭṭho;
::

::gathalast
Sayaṃ samattāni pakubbamāno, yathā hi jāneyya tathā vadeyya.
::

::hangnum
788\.
::

::gatha1
Yo attano sīlavatāni jantu, anānupuṭṭhova paresa {note:parassa (ka.)} pāva {note:pāvā (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Anariyadhammaṃ kusalā tamāhu, yo ātumānaṃ sayameva pāva.
::

::hangnum
789\.
::

::gatha1
Santo ca bhikkhu abhinibbutatto, itihanti sīlesu akatthamāno;
::

::gathalast
Tamariyadhammaṃ kusalā vadanti, yassussadā natthi kuhiñci loke.
::

::hangnum
790\.
::

::gatha1
Pakappitā {pb:P:0.0154} saṅkhatā yassa dhammā, purakkhatā {note:purekkhatā (sī.)} santi avīvadātā;
::

::gathalast
Yadattani {pb:T:0.0488} passati ānisaṃsaṃ, taṃ nissito kuppapaṭicca santiṃ.
::

::hangnum
791\.
::

::gatha1
Diṭṭhīnivesā na hi svātivattā, dhammesu niccheyya samuggahītaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tasmā naro tesu nivesanesu, nirassatī ādiyatī ca dhammaṃ.
::

::hangnum
792\.
::

::gatha1
Dhonassa {pb:M:0.0402} hi natthi kuhiñci loke, pakappitā diṭṭhi bhavābhavesu;
::

::gathalast
Māyañca mānañca pahāya dhono, sa kena gaccheyya anūpayo so.
::

::hangnum
793\.
::

::gatha1
Upayo hi dhammesu upeti vādaṃ, anūpayaṃ kena kathaṃ vadeyya;
::

::gathalast
Attā nirattā {note:attaṃ nirattaṃ (bahūsu)} na hi tassa atthi, adhosi so diṭṭhimidheva sabbanti.
::

::centre
Duṭṭhaṭṭhakasuttaṃ tatiyaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

#### 4. Suddhaṭṭhakasuttaṃ

::hangnum
794\.
::

::gatha1
Passāmi {pb:V:0.0202} suddhaṃ paramaṃ arogaṃ, diṭṭhena saṃsuddhi narassa hoti;
::

::gathalast
Evābhijānaṃ {pb:T:0.0489} {note:etābhijānaṃ (sī. pī.)} paramanti ñatvā, suddhānupassīti pacceti ñāṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
795\.
::

::gatha1
Diṭṭhena {pb:P:0.0155} ce suddhi narassa hoti, ñāṇena vā so pajahāti dukkhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Aññena so sujjhati sopadhīko, diṭṭhī hi naṃ pāva tathā vadānaṃ.
::

::hangnum
796\.
::

::gatha1
Na brāhmaṇo aññato suddhimāha, diṭṭhe sute sīlavate mute vā;
::

::gathalast
Puññe ca pāpe ca anūpalitto, attañjaho nayidha pakubbamāno.
::

::hangnum
797\.
::

::gatha1
Purimaṃ pahāya aparaṃ sitāse, ejānugā te na taranti saṅgaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Te uggahāyanti nirassajanti, kapīva sākhaṃ pamuñcaṃ gahāyaṃ {note:pamukhaṃ gahāya (syā.), pamuñca gahāya (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
798\.
::

::gatha1
Sayaṃ {pb:M:0.0403} samādāya vatāni jantu, uccāvacaṃ gacchati saññasatto;
::

::gathalast
Vidvā ca vedehi samecca dhammaṃ, na uccāvacaṃ gacchati bhūripañño.
::

::hangnum
799\.
::

::gatha1
Sa sabbadhammesu visenibhūto, yaṃ kiñci diṭṭhaṃ va sutaṃ mutaṃ vā;
::

::gathalast
Tameva {pb:T:0.0490} dassiṃ vivaṭaṃ carantaṃ, kenīdha lokasmi vikappayeyya.
::

::hangnum
800\.
::

::gatha1
Na kappayanti na purekkharonti, accantasuddhīti na te vadanti;
::

::gathalast
Ādānaganthaṃ {pb:P:0.0156} gathitaṃ visajja, āsaṃ na kubbanti kuhiñci loke.
::

::hangnum
801\.
::

::gatha1
Sīmātigo brāhmaṇo tassa natthi, ñatvā va disvā va {note:ñatvā ca disvā ca (ka. sī. ka.)} samuggahītaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na rāgarāgī na virāgaratto, tassīdha natthī paramuggahītanti.
::

::centre
Suddhaṭṭhakasuttaṃ catutthaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

#### 5. Paramaṭṭhakasuttaṃ

::hangnum
802\.
::

::gatha1
Paramanti {pb:V:0.0203} diṭṭhīsu paribbasāno, yaduttari kurute jantu loke;
::

::gathalast
Hīnāti aññe tato sabbamāha, tasmā vivādāni avītivatto.
::

::hangnum
803\.
::

::gatha1
Yadattanī passati ānisaṃsaṃ, diṭṭhe {pb:T:0.0491} sute sīlavate {note:sīlabbate (syā.)} mute vā;
::

::gathalast
Tadeva so tattha samuggahāya, nihīnato passati sabbamaññaṃ.
::

::hangnum
804\.
::

::gatha1
Taṃ {pb:M:0.0404} vāpi ganthaṃ kusalā vadanti, yaṃ nissito passati hīnamaññaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tasmā hi diṭṭhaṃ va sutaṃ mutaṃ vā, sīlabbataṃ bhikkhu na nissayeyya.
::

::hangnum
805\.
::

::gatha1
Diṭṭhimpi {pb:P:0.0157} lokasmiṃ na kappayeyya, ñāṇena vā sīlavatena vāpi;
::

::gathalast
Samoti attānamanūpaneyya, hīno na maññetha visesi vāpi.
::

::hangnum
806\.
::

::gatha1
Attaṃ pahāya anupādiyāno, ñāṇepi so nissayaṃ no karoti;
::

::gathalast
Sa ve viyattesu {note:viyuttesu (sī. aṭṭha.), dviyattesu (ka.)} na vaggasārī, diṭṭhimpi {note:diṭṭhimapi (ka.)} so na pacceti kiñci.
::

::hangnum
807\.
::

::gatha1
Yassūbhayante paṇidhīdha natthi, bhavābhavāya idha vā huraṃ vā;
::

::gathalast
Nivesanā tassa na santi keci, dhammesu niccheyya samuggahītaṃ.
::

::hangnum
808\.
::

::gatha1
Tassīdha diṭṭhe va sute mute vā, pakappitā {pb:T:0.0492} natthi aṇūpi saññā;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ brāhmaṇaṃ diṭṭhimanādiyānaṃ, kenīdha lokasmiṃ vikappayeyya.
::

::hangnum
809\.
::

::gatha1
Na kappayanti na purekkharonti, dhammāpi tesaṃ na paṭicchitāse;
::

::gathalast
Na {pb:P:0.0158} brāhmaṇo sīlavatena neyyo, pāraṅgato na pacceti tādīti.
::

::centre
Paramaṭṭhakasuttaṃ pañcamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

#### 6. Jarāsuttaṃ

::hangnum
810\.
::

::gatha1
Appaṃ {pb:M:0.0405}{pb:V:0.0204} vata jīvitaṃ idaṃ, oraṃ vassasatāpi miyyati {note:mīyati (sī. aṭṭha.)};
::

::gathalast
Yo cepi aticca jīvati, atha kho so jarasāpi miyyati.
::

::hangnum
811\.
::

::gatha1
Socanti janā mamāyite, na hi santi {note:na hi santā (sī.), na hī santi (katthaci)} niccā pariggahā;
::

::gathalast
Vinābhāvasantamevidaṃ, iti disvā nāgāramāvase.
::

::hangnum
812\.
::

::gatha1
Maraṇenapi taṃ pahīyati {note:pahiyyati (sī. syā. ka.)}, yaṃ puriso mamidanti {note:mamayidanti (sī. syā. ka.), mamāyanti (ka.)} maññati;
::

::gathalast
Etampi viditvā {note:etaṃ disvāna (niddese), etampi viditva (?)} paṇḍito, na mamattāya nametha māmako.
::

::hangnum
813\.
::

::gatha1
Supinena yathāpi saṅgataṃ, paṭibuddho puriso na passati;
::

::gathalast
Evampi {pb:P:0.0159} piyāyitaṃ janaṃ, petaṃ kālakataṃ na passati.
::

::hangnum
814\.
::

::gatha1
Diṭṭhāpi {pb:T:0.0493} sutāpi te janā, yesaṃ nāmamidaṃ pavuccati {note:nāmamevā vasissati (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Nāmaṃyevāvasissati, akkheyyaṃ petassa jantuno.
::

::hangnum
815\.
::

::gatha1
Sokapparidevamaccharaṃ {note:sokaparidevamaccharaṃ (sī. syā. pī.), sokaṃ paridevamaccharaṃ (?)}, na jahanti giddhā mamāyite;
::

::gathalast
Tasmā munayo pariggahaṃ, hitvā acariṃsu khemadassino.
::

::hangnum
816\.
::

::gatha1
Patilīnacarassa {pb:M:0.0406} bhikkhuno, bhajamānassa vivittamāsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sāmaggiyamāhu tassa taṃ, yo attānaṃ bhavane na dassaye.
::

::hangnum
817\.
::

::gatha1
Sabbattha munī anissito, na piyaṃ kubbati nopi appiyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tasmiṃ paridevamaccharaṃ, paṇṇe vāri yathā na limpati {note:lippati (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
818\.
::

::gatha1
Udabindu yathāpi pokkhare, padume vāri yathā na limpati;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ muni nopalimpati, yadidaṃ diṭṭhasutaṃ mutesu vā.
::

::hangnum
819\.
::

::gatha1
Dhono {pb:V:0.0205}{pb:P:0.0160} na hi tena maññati, yadidaṃ diṭṭhasutaṃ mutesu vā;
::

::gathalast
Nāññena visuddhimicchati, na hi so rajjati no virajjatīti.
::

::centre
Jarāsuttaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

#### 7. Tissametteyyasuttaṃ

::hangnum
820\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Methunamanuyuttassa, (iccāyasmā tisso metteyyo) vighātaṃ brūhi mārisa;
::

::gathalast
Sutvāna tava sāsanaṃ, viveke sikkhissāmase.
::

::hangnum
821\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Methunamanuyuttassa, (metteyyāti bhagavā) mussate vāpi sāsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Micchā {pb:T:0.0494} ca paṭipajjati, etaṃ tasmiṃ anāriyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
822\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Eko {pb:M:0.0407} pubbe caritvāna, methunaṃ yo nisevati;
::

::gathalast
Yānaṃ bhantaṃ va taṃ loke, hīnamāhu puthujjanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
823\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaso kitti ca yā pubbe, hāyate vāpi tassa sā;
::

::gathalast
Etampi disvā sikkhetha, methunaṃ vippahātave.
::

::hangnum
824\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṅkappehi pareto so, kapaṇo viya jhāyati;
::

::gathalast
Sutvā paresaṃ nigghosaṃ, maṅku hoti tathāvidho.
::

::hangnum
825\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atha satthāni kurute, paravādehi codito;
::

::gathalast
Esa khvassa mahāgedho, mosavajjaṃ pagāhati.
::

::hangnum
826\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṇḍitoti samaññāto, ekacariyaṃ adhiṭṭhito;
::

::gathalast
Athāpi {note:sa cāpi (niddese)} methune yutto, mandova parikissati {note:parikilissati (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
827\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Etamādīnavaṃ {pb:V:0.0206}{pb:P:0.0161} ñatvā, muni pubbāpare idha;
::

::gathalast
Ekacariyaṃ daḷhaṃ kayirā, na nisevetha methunaṃ.
::

::hangnum
828\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vivekaññeva sikkhetha, etadariyānamuttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na tena seṭṭho maññetha, sa ve nibbānasantike.
::

::hangnum
829\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rittassa munino carato, kāmesu anapekkhino;
::

::gathalast
Oghatiṇṇassa pihayanti, kāmesu gadhitā {note:gathitā (sī.)} pajā’’ti.
::

::centre
Tissametteyyasuttaṃ sattamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

#### 8. Pasūrasuttaṃ

::hangnum
830\.
::

::gatha1
Idheva {pb:T:0.0495} suddhi iti vādayanti {note:vidiyanti (sī. pī.)}, nāññesu dhammesu visuddhimāhu;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ nissitā tattha subhaṃ vadānā, paccekasaccesu puthū niviṭṭhā.
::

::hangnum
831\.
::

::gatha1
Te {pb:M:0.0408} vādakāmā parisaṃ vigayha, bālaṃ dahantī mithu aññamaññaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vadanti te aññasitā kathojjaṃ, pasaṃsakāmā kusalā vadānā.
::

::hangnum
832\.
::

::gatha1
Yutto kathāyaṃ parisāya majjhe, pasaṃsamicchaṃ vinighāti hoti;
::

::gathalast
Apāhatasmiṃ pana maṅku hoti, nindāya so kuppati randhamesī.
::

::hangnum
833\.
::

::gatha1
Yamassa {pb:P:0.0162} vādaṃ parihīnamāhu, apāhataṃ pañhavimaṃsakāse;
::

::gathalast
Paridevati socati hīnavādo, upaccagā manti anutthunāti.
::

::hangnum
834\.
::

::gatha1
Ete vivādā samaṇesu jātā, etesu ugghāti nighāti hoti;
::

::gathalast
Etampi {pb:T:0.0496} disvā virame kathojjaṃ, na haññadatthatthipasaṃsalābhā.
::

::hangnum
835\.
::

::gatha1
Pasaṃsito {pb:V:0.0207} vā pana tattha hoti, akkhāya vādaṃ parisāya majjhe;
::

::gathalast
So hassatī uṇṇamatī {note:unnamatī (?)} ca tena, pappuyya tamatthaṃ yathā mano ahu.
::

::hangnum
836\.
::

::gatha1
Yā uṇṇatī {note:unnatī (?)} sāssa vighātabhūmi, mānātimānaṃ vadate paneso;
::

::gathalast
Etampi disvā na vivādayetha, na hi tena suddhiṃ kusalā vadanti.
::

::hangnum
837\.
::

::gatha1
Sūro yathā rājakhādāya puṭṭho, abhigajjameti paṭisūramicchaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yeneva so tena palehi sūra, pubbeva natthi yadidaṃ yudhāya.
::

::hangnum
838\.
::

::gatha1
Ye {pb:M:0.0409} diṭṭhimuggayha vivādayanti {note:vivādiyanti (sī. pī.)}, idameva saccanti ca vādayanti;
::

::gathalast
Te {pb:P:0.0163} tvaṃ vadassū na hi tedha atthi, vādamhi jāte paṭisenikattā.
::

::hangnum
839\.
::

::gatha1
Visenikatvā pana ye caranti, diṭṭhīhi diṭṭhiṃ avirujjhamānā;
::

::gathalast
Tesu {pb:T:0.0497} tvaṃ kiṃ labhetho pasūra, yesīdha natthī paramuggahītaṃ.
::

::hangnum
840\.
::

::gatha1
Atha tvaṃ pavitakkamāgamā, manasā diṭṭhigatāni cintayanto;
::

::gathalast
Dhonena yugaṃ samāgamā, na hi tvaṃ sakkhasi sampayātaveti.
::

::centre
Pasūrasuttaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

#### 9. Māgaṇḍiyasuttaṃ

::hangnum
841\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Disvāna taṇhaṃ aratiṃ ragañca {note:aratiñca rāgaṃ (syā. ka.)}, nāhosi chando api methunasmiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kimevidaṃ muttakarīsapuṇṇaṃ, pādāpi naṃ samphusituṃ na icche’’.
::

::hangnum
842\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Etādisaṃ {pb:P:0.0164} ce ratanaṃ na icchasi, nāriṃ narindehi bahūhi patthitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Diṭṭhigataṃ sīlavataṃ nu jīvitaṃ {note:sīlavatānujīvitaṃ (sī. pī. ka.)}, bhavūpapattiñca vadesi kīdisaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
843\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idaṃ {pb:V:0.0208} vadāmīti na tassa hoti, (māgaṇḍiyāti {note:māgandiyāti (sī. syā. pī.)} bhagavā)
::

::gatha2
Dhammesu niccheyya samuggahītaṃ;
::

::gatha3
Passañca {pb:T:0.0498} diṭṭhīsu anuggahāya,
::

::gathalast
Ajjhattasantiṃ pacinaṃ adassaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
844\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vinicchayā {pb:M:0.0410} yāni pakappitāni, (iti māgaṇḍiyo {note:māgandiyo (sī. syā. pī.)} )
::

::gatha2
Te ve munī brūsi anuggahāya;
::

::gatha3
Ajjhattasantīti yametamatthaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Kathaṃ nu dhīrehi paveditaṃ taṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
845\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na diṭṭhiyā na sutiyā na ñāṇena, (māgaṇḍiyāti bhagavā)
::

::gatha2
Sīlabbatenāpi na suddhimāha;
::

::gatha3
Adiṭṭhiyā assutiyā añāṇā,
::

::gatha2
Asīlatā abbatā nopi tena;
::

::gatha3
Ete ca nissajja anuggahāya,
::

::gathalast
Santo anissāya bhavaṃ na jappe’’.
::

::hangnum
846\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘No ce kira diṭṭhiyā na sutiyā na ñāṇena, (iti māgaṇḍiyo)
::

::gatha2
Sīlabbatenāpi na suddhimāha;
::

::gatha3
Adiṭṭhiyā {pb:P:0.0165} assutiyā añāṇā,
::

::gatha2
Asīlatā abbatā nopi tena;
::

::gatha3
Maññāmahaṃ momuhameva dhammaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Diṭṭhiyā eke paccenti suddhiṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
847\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Diṭṭhañca nissāya anupucchamāno, (māgaṇḍiyāti bhagavā)
::

::gatha2
Samuggahītesu pamohamāgā {note:samohamāgā (syā. ka.)};
::

::gatha3
Ito {pb:T:0.0499} ca nāddakkhi aṇumpi saññaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Tasmā tuvaṃ momuhato dahāsi.
::

::hangnum
848\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samo {pb:V:0.0209} visesī uda vā nihīno, yo maññatī so vivadetha tena;
::

::gathalast
Tīsu vidhāsu avikampamāno, samo visesīti na tassa hoti.
::

::hangnum
849\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saccanti so brāhmaṇo kiṃ vadeyya, musāti vā so vivadetha kena;
::

::gathalast
Yasmiṃ samaṃ visamaṃ vāpi natthi, sa kena vādaṃ paṭisaṃyujeyya.
::

::hangnum
850\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Okaṃ {pb:M:0.0411} pahāya aniketasārī, gāme akubbaṃ muni santhavāni {note:sandhavāni (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Kāmehi ritto apurekkharāno, kathaṃ na viggayha janena kayirā.
::

::hangnum
851\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yehi vivitto vicareyya loke, na tāni uggayha vadeyya nāgo;
::

::gatha2
Jalambujaṃ {pb:P:0.0166} {note:elambujaṃ (sī. syā.)} kaṇḍakaṃ vārijaṃ yathā, jalena paṅkena canūpalittaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ munī santivādo agiddho, kāme ca loke ca anūpalitto.
::

::hangnum
852\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:T:0.0500} vedagū diṭṭhiyāyako {note:na vedagū diṭṭhiyā (ka. sī. syā. pī.)} na mutiyā, sa mānameti na hi tammayo so;
::

::gathalast
Na kammunā nopi sutena neyyo, anūpanīto sa nivesanesu.
::

::hangnum
853\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saññāvirattassa na santi ganthā, paññāvimuttassa na santi mohā;
::

::gathalast
Saññañca diṭṭhiñca ye aggahesuṃ, te ghaṭṭayantā {note:ghaṭṭamānā (syā. ka.)} vicaranti loke’’ti.
::

::centre
Māgaṇḍiyasuttaṃ navamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

#### 10. Purābhedasuttaṃ

::hangnum
854\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kathaṃdassī kathaṃsīlo, upasantoti vuccati;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ me gotama pabrūhi, pucchito uttamaṃ naraṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
855\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vītataṇho purā bhedā, (iti bhagavā) pubbamantamanissito;
::

::gathalast
Vemajjhe nupasaṅkheyyo, tassa natthi purakkhataṃ.
::

::hangnum
856\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Akkodhano {pb:M:0.0412}{pb:V:0.0210}{pb:P:0.0167} asantāsī, avikatthī akukkuco;
::

::gathalast
Mantabhāṇī {note:mantābhāṇī (syā. pī.)} anuddhato, sa ve vācāyato muni.
::

::hangnum
857\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nirāsatti anāgate, atītaṃ nānusocati;
::

::gathalast
Vivekadassī phassesu, diṭṭhīsu ca na nīyati {note:niyyati (bahūsu)}.
::

::hangnum
858\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Patilīno akuhako, apihālu amaccharī;
::

::gathalast
Appagabbho {pb:T:0.0501} ajeguccho, pesuṇeyye ca no yuto.
::

::hangnum
859\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sātiyesu anassāvī, atimāne ca no yuto;
::

::gathalast
Saṇho ca paṭibhānavā {note:paṭibhāṇavā (syā. pī.)}, na saddho na virajjati.
::

::hangnum
860\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Lābhakamyā na sikkhati, alābhe ca na kuppati;
::

::gathalast
Aviruddho ca taṇhāya, rasesu nānugijjhati.
::

::hangnum
861\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upekkhako sadā sato, na loke maññate samaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na visesī na nīceyyo, tassa no santi ussadā.
::

::hangnum
862\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yassa nissayanā {note:nissayatā (sī. syā. pī.)} natthi, ñatvā dhammaṃ anissito;
::

::gathalast
Bhavāya vibhavāya vā, taṇhā yassa na vijjati.
::

::hangnum
863\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ brūmi upasantoti, kāmesu anapekkhinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ganthā tassa na vijjanti, atarī so visattikaṃ.
::

::hangnum
864\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na tassa puttā pasavo, khettaṃ vatthuñca vijjati;
::

::gathalast
Attā {pb:P:0.0168} vāpi nirattā vā {note:attaṃ vāpi nirattaṃ vā (bahūsu)}, na tasmiṃ upalabbhati.
::

::hangnum
865\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yena naṃ vajjuṃ puthujjanā, atho samaṇabrāhmaṇā;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ tassa apurakkhataṃ, tasmā vādesu nejati.
::

::hangnum
866\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vītagedho {pb:V:0.0211} amaccharī, na ussesu vadate muni;
::

::gathalast
Na samesu na omesu, kappaṃ neti akappiyo.
::

::hangnum
867\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yassa loke sakaṃ natthi, asatā ca na socati;
::

::gathalast
Dhammesu ca na gacchati, sa ve santoti vuccatī’’ti.
::

::centre
Purābhedasuttaṃ dasamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

#### 11. Kalahavivādasuttaṃ

::hangnum
868\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kutopahūtā {pb:M:0.0413}{pb:T:0.0502} kalahā vivādā, paridevasokā sahamaccharā ca;
::

::gathalast
Mānātimānā sahapesuṇā ca, kutopahūtā te tadiṅgha brūhi’’.
::

::hangnum
869\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Piyappahūtā kalahā vivādā,
::

::gatha2
Paridevasokā sahamaccharā ca;
::

::gatha3
Mānātimānā sahapesuṇā ca,
::

::gatha2
Maccherayuttā kalahā vivādā;
::

::gathalast
Vivādajātesu ca pesuṇāni’’.
::

::hangnum
870\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Piyā {pb:P:0.0169} su {note:piyānu (syā.), piyassu (ka.)} lokasmiṃ kutonidānā, ye cāpi {note:ye vāpi (sī. syā. pī.)} lobhā vicaranti loke;
::

::gathalast
Āsā ca niṭṭhā ca kutonidānā, ye samparāyāya narassa honti’’.
::

::hangnum
871\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Chandānidānāni piyāni loke, ye cāpi lobhā vicaranti loke;
::

::gathalast
Āsā ca niṭṭhā ca itonidānā, ye samparāyāya narassa honti’’.
::

::hangnum
872\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Chando {pb:T:0.0503} nu lokasmiṃ kutonidāno, vinicchayā cāpi {note:vāpi (sī. syā. pī.)} kutopahūtā;
::

::gathalast
Kodho mosavajjañca kathaṃkathā ca, ye vāpi dhammā samaṇena vuttā’’.
::

::hangnum
873\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sātaṃ {pb:V:0.0212} asātanti yamāhu loke, tamūpanissāya pahoti chando;
::

::gathalast
Rūpesu disvā vibhavaṃ bhavañca, vinicchayaṃ kubbati {note:kurute (bahūsu)} jantu loke.
::

::hangnum
874\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kodho {pb:M:0.0414} mosavajjañca kathaṃkathā ca, etepi dhammā dvayameva sante;
::

::gathalast
Kathaṃkathī ñāṇapathāya sikkhe, ñatvā pavuttā samaṇena dhammā’’.
::

::hangnum
875\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sātaṃ asātañca kutonidānā, kismiṃ asante na bhavanti hete;
::

::gathalast
Vibhavaṃ bhavañcāpi yametamatthaṃ, etaṃ me pabrūhi yatonidānaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
876\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Phassanidānaṃ sātaṃ asātaṃ, phasse asante na bhavanti hete;
::

::gathalast
Vibhavaṃ {pb:P:0.0170} bhavañcāpi yametamatthaṃ, etaṃ te pabrūmi itonidānaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
877\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Phasso {pb:T:0.0504} nu lokasmi kutonidāno, pariggahā cāpi kutopahūtā;
::

::gathalast
Kismiṃ asante na mamattamatthi, kismiṃ vibhūte na phusanti phassā’’.
::

::hangnum
878\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nāmañca rūpañca paṭicca phasso, icchānidānāni pariggahāni;
::

::gathalast
Icchāyasantyā na mamattamatthi, rūpe vibhūte na phusanti phassā’’.
::

::hangnum
879\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kathaṃsametassa vibhoti rūpaṃ, sukhaṃ dukhañcāpi {note:dukhaṃ vāpi (sī. syā.)} kathaṃ vibhoti;
::

::gathalast
Etaṃ me pabrūhi yathā vibhoti, taṃ jāniyāmāti {note:jānissāmāti (sī. ka.)} me mano ahu’’.
::

::hangnum
880\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na saññasaññī na visaññasaññī, nopi asaññī na vibhūtasaññī;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃsametassa vibhoti rūpaṃ, saññānidānā hi papañcasaṅkhā’’.
::

::hangnum
881\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ {pb:M:0.0415} taṃ apucchimha akittayī no,
::

::gatha2
Aññaṃ taṃ pucchāma tadiṅgha brūhi;
::

::gatha3
Ettāvataggaṃ {pb:P:0.0171} nu {note:no (sī. syā.)} vadanti heke,
::

::gatha2
Yakkhassa suddhiṃ idha paṇḍitāse;
::

::gathalast
Udāhu {pb:T:0.0505} aññampi vadanti etto.
::

::hangnum
882\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ettāvataggampi {pb:V:0.0213} vadanti heke, yakkhassa suddhiṃ idha paṇḍitāse;
::

::gathalast
Tesaṃ paneke samayaṃ vadanti, anupādisese kusalā vadānā.
::

::hangnum
883\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ete ca ñatvā upanissitāti, ñatvā munī nissaye so vimaṃsī;
::

::gathalast
Ñatvā vimutto na vivādameti, bhavābhavāya na sameti dhīro’’ti.
::

::centre
Kalahavivādasuttaṃ ekādasamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

#### 12. Cūḷabyūhasuttaṃ {note:cūḷaviyūhasuttaṃ (sī. syā. niddesa)}

::hangnum
884\.
::

::gatha1
Sakaṃsakaṃdiṭṭhiparibbasānā, viggayha nānā kusalā vadanti;
::

::gathalast
Yo evaṃ jānāti sa vedi dhammaṃ, idaṃ paṭikkosamakevalī so.
::

::hangnum
885\.
::

::gatha1
Evampi viggayha vivādayanti, bālo paro akkusaloti {note:akusaloti (sī. syā. pī.)} cāhu;
::

::gathalast
Sacco nu vādo katamo imesaṃ, sabbeva {pb:T:0.0506} hīme kusalā vadānā.
::

::hangnum
886\.
::

::gatha1
Parassa {pb:M:0.0416}{pb:P:0.0172} ce dhammamanānujānaṃ, bālomako {note:bālo mago (sī. syā. ka.)} hoti nihīnapañño;
::

::gathalast
Sabbeva bālā sunihīnapaññā, sabbevime diṭṭhiparibbasānā.
::

::hangnum
887\.
::

::gatha1
Sandiṭṭhiyā ceva na vīvadātā, saṃsuddhapaññā kusalā mutīmā;
::

::gathalast
Na tesaṃ koci parihīnapañño {note:kocipi nihīnapañño (sī. syā. ka.)}, diṭṭhī hi tesampi tathā samattā.
::

::hangnum
888\.
::

::gatha1
Na vāhametaṃ tathiyanti {note:tathivanti (syā. ka.)} brūmi, yamāhu bālā mithu aññamaññaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sakaṃsakaṃdiṭṭhimakaṃsu saccaṃ, tasmā hi bāloti paraṃ dahanti.
::

::hangnum
889\.
::

::gatha1
Yamāhu saccaṃ tathiyanti eke, tamāhu aññe {note:aññepi (syā.), aññe ca (?)} tucchaṃ musāti;
::

::gathalast
Evampi vigayha vivādayanti, kasmā na ekaṃ samaṇā vadanti.
::

::hangnum
890\.
::

::gatha1
Ekañhi {pb:V:0.0214} saccaṃ na dutīyamatthi, yasmiṃ pajā no vivade pajānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nānā te {note:nānāto (ka.)} saccāni sayaṃ thunanti, tasmā {pb:T:0.0507} na ekaṃ samaṇā vadanti.
::

::hangnum
891\.
::

::gatha1
Kasmā {pb:P:0.0173} nu saccāni vadanti nānā, pavādiyāse kusalā vadānā;
::

::gathalast
Saccāni sutāni bahūni nānā, udāhu te takkamanussaranti.
::

::hangnum
892\.
::

::gatha1
Na heva saccāni bahūni nānā, aññatra saññāya niccāni loke;
::

::gathalast
Takkañca diṭṭhīsu pakappayitvā, saccaṃ musāti dvayadhammamāhu.
::

::hangnum
893\.
::

::gatha1
Diṭṭhe {pb:M:0.0417} sute sīlavate mute vā, ete ca nissāya vimānadassī;
::

::gathalast
Vinicchaye ṭhatvā pahassamāno, bālo paro akkusaloti cāha.
::

::hangnum
894\.
::

::gatha1
Yeneva bāloti paraṃ dahāti, tenātumānaṃ kusaloti cāha;
::

::gathalast
Sayamattanā so kusalo vadāno, aññaṃ vimāneti tadeva pāva.
::

::hangnum
895\.
::

::gatha1
Atisāradiṭṭhiyāva so samatto, mānena matto paripuṇṇamānī;
::

::gathalast
Sayameva sāmaṃ manasābhisitto, diṭṭhī {pb:T:0.0508} hi sā tassa tathā samattā.
::

::hangnum
896\.
::

::gatha1
Parassa ce hi vacasā nihīno, tumo sahā hoti nihīnapañño;
::

::gathalast
Atha ce sayaṃ vedagū hoti dhīro, na koci bālo samaṇesu atthi.
::

::hangnum
897\.
::

::gatha1
Aññaṃ {pb:P:0.0174} ito yābhivadanti dhammaṃ, aparaddhā suddhimakevalī te {note:suddhimakevalīno (sī.)};
::

::gathalast
Evampi titthyā puthuso vadanti, sandiṭṭhirāgena hi tebhirattā {note:tyābhirattā (syā. ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
898\.
::

::gatha1
Idheva suddhi iti vādayanti, nāññesu dhammesu visuddhimāhu;
::

::gathalast
Evampi titthyā puthuso niviṭṭhā, sakāyane tattha daḷhaṃ vadānā.
::

::hangnum
899\.
::

::gatha1
Sakāyane vāpi daḷhaṃ vadāno, kamettha bāloti paraṃ daheyya;
::

::gathalast
Sayameva so medhagamāvaheyya {note:medhakaṃ āvaheyya (sī. pī.)}, paraṃ vadaṃ bālamasuddhidhammaṃ.
::

::hangnum
900\.
::

::gatha1
Vinicchaye {pb:M:0.0418}{pb:V:0.0215} ṭhatvā sayaṃ pamāya, uddhaṃ sa {note:uddaṃ so (sī. syā. pī.)} lokasmiṃ vivādameti;
::

::gathalast
Hitvāna sabbāni vinicchayāni, na {pb:T:0.0509} medhagaṃ kubbati jantu loketi.
::

::centre
Cūḷabyūhasuttaṃ dvādasamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

#### 13. Mahābyūhasuttaṃ

::hangnum
901\.
::

::gatha1
Ye kecime diṭṭhiparibbasānā, idameva saccanti vivādayanti {note:vivādiyanti (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Sabbeva te nindamanvānayanti, atho pasaṃsampi labhanti tattha.
::

::hangnum
902\.
::

::gatha1
Appañhi {pb:P:0.0175} etaṃ na alaṃ samāya, duve vivādassa phalāni brūmi;
::

::gathalast
Etampi disvā na vivādayetha, khemābhipassaṃ avivādabhūmiṃ.
::

::hangnum
903\.
::

::gatha1
Yā kācimā sammutiyo puthujjā, sabbāva etā na upeti vidvā;
::

::gathalast
Anūpayo so upayaṃ kimeyya, diṭṭhe sute khantimakubbamāno.
::

::hangnum
904\.
::

::gatha1
Sīluttamā saññamenāhu suddhiṃ, vataṃ samādāya upaṭṭhitāse;
::

::gathalast
Idheva sikkhema athassa suddhiṃ, bhavūpanītā {pb:T:0.0510} kusalā vadānā.
::

::hangnum
905\.
::

::gatha1
Sace cuto sīlavatato hoti, pavedhatī {note:sa vedhati (sī. pī.)} kamma virādhayitvā;
::

::gathalast
Pajappatī patthayatī ca suddhiṃ, satthāva hīno pavasaṃ gharamhā.
::

::hangnum
906\.
::

::gatha1
Sīlabbataṃ {pb:M:0.0419} vāpi pahāya sabbaṃ, kammañca sāvajjanavajjametaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Suddhiṃ {pb:P:0.0176} asuddhinti apatthayāno, virato care santimanuggahāya.
::

::hangnum
907\.
::

::gatha1
Tamūpanissāya jigucchitaṃ vā, athavāpi diṭṭhaṃ va sutaṃ mutaṃ vā;
::

::gathalast
Uddhaṃsarā suddhimanutthunanti, avītataṇhāse bhavābhavesu.
::

::hangnum
908\.
::

::gatha1
Patthayamānassa {pb:V:0.0216} hi jappitāni, pavedhitaṃ vāpi pakappitesu;
::

::gathalast
Cutūpapāto idha yassa natthi, sa kena vedheyya kuhiṃva jappe {note:kuhiñci jappe (sī. syā. ka.), kuhiṃ pajappe (pī.) niddeso passitabbo}.
::

::hangnum
909\.
::

::gatha1
Yamāhu dhammaṃ paramanti eke, tameva hīnanti panāhu aññe;
::

Sacco nu vādo katamo imesaṃ, sabbeva {pb:T:0.0511} hīme kusalā vadānā.

::hangnum
910\.
::

::gatha1
Sakañhi dhammaṃ paripuṇṇamāhu, aññassa dhammaṃ pana hīnamāhu;
::

::gathalast
Evampi viggayha vivādayanti, sakaṃ sakaṃ sammutimāhu saccaṃ.
::

::hangnum
911\.
::

::gatha1
Parassa ce vambhayitena hīno, na koci dhammesu visesi assa;
::

::gathalast
Puthū hi aññassa vadanti dhammaṃ, nihīnato samhi daḷhaṃ vadānā.
::

::hangnum
912\.
::

::gatha1
Saddhammapūjāpi {pb:P:0.0177} nesaṃ tatheva, yathā pasaṃsanti sakāyanāni;
::

::gathalast
Sabbeva vādā {note:sabbe pavādā (syā.)} tathiyā {note:tathivā (sabbattha)} bhaveyyuṃ, suddhī hi nesaṃ paccattameva.
::

::hangnum
913\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:M:0.0420} brāhmaṇassa paraneyyamatthi, dhammesu niccheyya samuggahītaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tasmā vivādāni upātivatto, na hi seṭṭhato passati dhammamaññaṃ.
::

::hangnum
914\.
::

::gatha1
Jānāmi passāmi tatheva etaṃ, diṭṭhiyā eke paccenti suddhiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Addakkhi ce kiñhi tumassa tena, atisitvā {pb:T:0.0512} aññena vadanti suddhiṃ.
::

::hangnum
915\.
::

::gatha1
Passaṃ naro dakkhati {note:dakkhiti (sī.)} nāmarūpaṃ, disvāna vā ñassati tānimeva;
::

::gathalast
Kāmaṃ bahuṃ passatu appakaṃ vā, na hi tena suddhiṃ kusalā vadanti.
::

::hangnum
916\.
::

::gatha1
Nivissavādī na hi subbināyo, pakappitaṃ diṭṭhi purekkharāno;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ nissito tattha subhaṃ vadāno, suddhiṃvado tattha tathaddasā so.
::

::hangnum
917\.
::

::gatha1
Na brāhmaṇo kappamupeti saṅkhā {note:saṅkhaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)}, na diṭṭhisārī napi ñāṇabandhu;
::

::gathalast
Ñatvā {pb:P:0.0178} ca so sammutiyo {note:sammatiyo (syā.)} puthujjā, upekkhatī uggahaṇanti maññe.
::

::hangnum
918\.
::

::gatha1
Vissajja {pb:V:0.0217} ganthāni munīdha loke, vivādajātesu na vaggasārī;
::

::gathalast
Santo asantesu upekkhako so, anuggaho uggahaṇanti maññe.
::

::hangnum
919\.
::

::gatha1
Pubbāsave hitvā nave akubbaṃ, na chandagū nopi nivissavādī;
::

::gathalast
Sa vippamutto diṭṭhigatehi dhīro, na {pb:T:0.0513} limpati {note:na lippati (sī. pī.)} loke anattagarahī.
::

::hangnum
920\.
::

::gatha1
Sa {pb:M:0.0421} sabbadhammesu visenibhūto, yaṃ kiñci diṭṭhaṃ va sutaṃ mutaṃ vā;
::

::gathalast
Sa pannabhāro muni vippamutto, na kappiyo nūparato na patthiyoti.
::

::centre
Mahābyūhasuttaṃ terasamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

#### 14. Tuvaṭakasuttaṃ

::hangnum
921\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pucchāmi {pb:P:0.0179} taṃ ādiccabandhu {note:ādiccabandhuṃ (sī. syā.)}, vivekaṃ santipadañca mahesi;
::

::gathalast
Kathaṃ disvā nibbāti bhikkhu, anupādiyāno lokasmiṃ kiñci’’.
::

::hangnum
922\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mūlaṃ papañcasaṅkhāya, (iti bhagavā)
::

::gatha2
Mantā asmīti sabbamuparundhe {note:sabbamuparuddhe (syā. pī. ka.)};
::

::gatha3
Yā kāci taṇhā ajjhattaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Tāsaṃ vinayā {note:vinayāya (?)} sadā sato sikkhe.
::

::hangnum
923\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ kiñci dhammamabhijaññā, ajjhattaṃ athavāpi bahiddhā;
::

::gathalast
Na tena thāmaṃ {note:mānaṃ (sī. ka.)} kubbetha, na {pb:T:0.0514} hi sā nibbuti sataṃ vuttā.
::

::hangnum
924\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Seyyo na tena maññeyya, nīceyyo athavāpi sarikkho;
::

::gathalast
Phuṭṭho {note:puṭṭho (sī. syā. ka.)} anekarūpehi, nātumānaṃ vikappayaṃ tiṭṭhe.
::

::hangnum
925\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ajjhattamevupasame{pb:V:0.0218}, na aññato bhikkhu santimeseyya;
::

::gathalast
Ajjhattaṃ upasantassa, natthi attā kuto nirattā vā.
::

::hangnum
926\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Majjhe {pb:M:0.0422}{pb:P:0.0180} yathā samuddassa, ūmi no jāyatī ṭhito hoti;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ ṭhito anejassa, ussadaṃ bhikkhu na kareyya kuhiñci’’.
::

::hangnum
927\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Akittayī vivaṭacakkhu, sakkhidhammaṃ parissayavinayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Paṭipadaṃ vadehi bhaddante, pātimokkhaṃ athavāpi samādhiṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
928\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cakkhūhi neva lolassa, gāmakathāya āvaraye sotaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Rase ca nānugijjheyya, na {pb:T:0.0515} ca mamāyetha kiñci lokasmiṃ.
::

::hangnum
929\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Phassena yadā phuṭṭhassa, paridevaṃ bhikkhu na kareyya kuhiñci;
::

::gathalast
Bhavañca nābhijappeyya, bheravesu ca na sampavedheyya.
::

::hangnum
930\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Annānamatho pānānaṃ, khādanīyānaṃ athopi vatthānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Laddhā na sannidhiṃ kayirā, na ca parittase tāni alabhamāno.
::

::hangnum
931\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jhāyī na pādalolassa, virame kukkuccā nappamajjeyya;
::

::gathalast
Athāsanesu sayanesu, appasaddesu bhikkhu vihareyya.
::

::hangnum
932\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Niddaṃ {pb:P:0.0181} na bahulīkareyya, jāgariyaṃ bhajeyya ātāpī;
::

::gathalast
Tandiṃ māyaṃ hassaṃ khiḍḍaṃ, methunaṃ vippajahe savibhūsaṃ.
::

::hangnum
933\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āthabbaṇaṃ {pb:M:0.0423} supinaṃ lakkhaṇaṃ, no vidahe athopi nakkhattaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Virutañca gabbhakaraṇaṃ, tikicchaṃ {pb:T:0.0516} māmako na seveyya.
::

::hangnum
934\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nindāya nappavedheyya, na uṇṇameyya pasaṃsito bhikkhu;
::

::gathalast
Lobhaṃ saha macchariyena, kodhaṃ pesuṇiyañca panudeyya.
::

::hangnum
935\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kayavikkaye {pb:V:0.0219} na tiṭṭheyya, upavādaṃ bhikkhu na kareyya kuhiñci;
::

::gathalast
Gāme ca nābhisajjeyya, lābhakamyā janaṃ na lapayeyya.
::

::hangnum
936\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na ca katthitā siyā bhikkhu, na ca vācaṃ payuttaṃ bhāseyya;
::

::gathalast
Pāgabbhiyaṃ na sikkheyya, kathaṃ viggāhikaṃ na kathayeyya.
::

::hangnum
937\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mosavajje na nīyetha, sampajāno saṭhāni na kayirā;
::

::gathalast
Atha {pb:P:0.0182} jīvitena paññāya, sīlabbatena nāññamatimaññe.
::

::hangnum
938\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sutvā rusito bahuṃ vācaṃ, samaṇānaṃ vā puthujanānaṃ {note:puthuvacanānaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Pharusena ne na paṭivajjā, na {pb:T:0.0517} hi santo paṭisenikaronti.
::

::hangnum
939\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Etañca dhammamaññāya, vicinaṃ bhikkhu sadā sato sikkhe;
::

::gathalast
Santīti nibbutiṃ ñatvā, sāsane gotamassa na pamajjeyya.
::

::hangnum
940\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Abhibhū {pb:M:0.0424} hi so anabhibhūto, sakkhidhammamanītihamadassī;
::

::gathalast
Tasmā hi tassa bhagavato sāsane, appamatto sadā namassamanusikkhe’’ti.
::

::centre
Tuvaṭakasuttaṃ cuddasamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

#### 15. Attadaṇḍasuttaṃ

::hangnum
941\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Attadaṇḍā bhayaṃ jātaṃ, janaṃ passatha medhagaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Saṃvegaṃ kittayissāmi, yathā saṃvijitaṃ mayā.
::

::hangnum
942\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Phandamānaṃ {pb:P:0.0183} pajaṃ disvā, macche appodake yathā;
::

::gathalast
Aññamaññehi byāruddhe, disvā maṃ bhayamāvisi.
::

::hangnum
943\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samantamasāro {pb:V:0.0220} loko, disā sabbā sameritā;
::

::gathalast
Icchaṃ bhavanamattano, nāddasāsiṃ anositaṃ.
::

::hangnum
944\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Osānetveva {pb:T:0.0518} byāruddhe, disvā me aratī ahu;
::

::gathalast
Athettha sallamaddakkhiṃ, duddasaṃ hadayanissitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
945\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yena sallena otiṇṇo, disā sabbā vidhāvati;
::

::gathalast
Tameva sallamabbuyha, na dhāvati na sīdati.
::

::hangnum
946\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tattha sikkhānugīyanti {note:sikkhānukiriyanti (ka.)}, yāni loke gadhitāni;
::

::gatha2
Na tesu pasuto siyā, nibbijjha sabbaso kāme;
::

::gathalast
Sikkhe nibbānamattano.
::

::hangnum
947\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sacco siyā appagabbho, amāyo rittapesuṇo;
::

::gathalast
Akkodhano lobhapāpaṃ, vevicchaṃ vitare muni.
::

::hangnum
948\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Niddaṃ tandiṃ sahe thīnaṃ, pamādena na saṃvase;
::

::gathalast
Atimāne na tiṭṭheyya, nibbānamanaso naro.
::

::hangnum
949\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mosavajje {pb:M:0.0425}{pb:P:0.0184} na nīyetha, rūpe snehaṃ na kubbaye;
::

::gathalast
Mānañca parijāneyya, sāhasā virato care.
::

::hangnum
950\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Purāṇaṃ nābhinandeyya, nave khantiṃ na kubbaye;
::

::gathalast
Hiyyamāne na soceyya, ākāsaṃ na sito siyā.
::

::hangnum
951\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gedhaṃ brūmi mahoghoti, ājavaṃ brūmi jappanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ārammaṇaṃ pakappanaṃ, kāmapaṅko duraccayo.
::

::hangnum
952\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saccā avokkamma {note:avokkamaṃ (niddesa)} muni, thale tiṭṭhati brāhmaṇo;
::

::gathalast
Sabbaṃ so {note:sabbaso (syā. ka.)} paṭinissajja, sa ve santoti vuccati.
::

::hangnum
953\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sa {pb:V:0.0221} ve vidvā sa vedagū, ñatvā dhammaṃ anissito;
::

::gathalast
Sammā {pb:T:0.0519} so loke iriyāno, na pihetīdha kassaci.
::

::hangnum
954\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yodha kāme accatari, saṅgaṃ loke duraccayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na so socati nājjheti, chinnasoto abandhano.
::

::hangnum
955\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ pubbe taṃ visosehi, pacchā te māhu kiñcanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Majjhe ce no gahessasi, upasanto carissasi.
::

::hangnum
956\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbaso nāmarūpasmiṃ, yassa natthi mamāyitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Asatā ca na socati, sa ve loke na jīyati.
::

::hangnum
957\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yassa natthi idaṃ meti, paresaṃ vāpi kiñcanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mamattaṃ so asaṃvindaṃ, natthi meti na socati.
::

::hangnum
958\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aniṭṭhurī {pb:P:0.0185} ananugiddho, anejo sabbadhī samo;
::

::gathalast
Tamānisaṃsaṃ pabrūmi, pucchito avikampinaṃ.
::

::hangnum
959\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anejassa vijānato, natthi kāci nisaṅkhati {note:nisaṅkhiti (sī. pī.)}.
::

::gathalast
Virato so viyārabbhā, khemaṃ passati sabbadhi.
::

::hangnum
960\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na samesu na omesu, na ussesu vadate muni;
::

::gathalast
Santo so vītamaccharo, nādeti na nirassatī’’ti.
::

::centre
Attadaṇḍasuttaṃ pannarasamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

#### 16. Sāriputtasuttaṃ

::hangnum
961\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:M:0.0426}{pb:V:0.0222}{pb:T:0.0520} me diṭṭho ito pubbe, (iccāyasmā sāriputto)
::

::gatha2
Na suto uda kassaci;
::

::gatha3
Evaṃ vagguvado satthā,
::

::gathalast
Tusitā gaṇimāgato.
::

::hangnum
962\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sadevakassa lokassa, yathā dissati cakkhumā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbaṃ tamaṃ vinodetvā, ekova ratimajjhagā.
::

::hangnum
963\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ {pb:P:0.0186} buddhaṃ asitaṃ tādiṃ, akuhaṃ gaṇimāgataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bahūnamidha baddhānaṃ, atthi pañhena āgamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
964\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhikkhuno vijigucchato, bhajato rittamāsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Rukkhamūlaṃ susānaṃ vā, pabbatānaṃ guhāsu vā.
::

::hangnum
965\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uccāvacesu sayanesu, kīvanto tattha bheravā;
::

::gathalast
Yehi bhikkhu na vedheyya, nigghose sayanāsane.
::

::hangnum
966\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Katī parissayā loke, gacchato agataṃ disaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ye bhikkhu abhisambhave, pantamhi sayanāsane.
::

::hangnum
967\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kyāssa byappathayo assu, kyāssassu idha gocarā;
::

::gathalast
Kāni sīlabbatānāssu, pahitattassa bhikkhuno.
::

::hangnum
968\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kaṃ so sikkhaṃ samādāya, ekodi nipako sato;
::

::gathalast
Kammāro rajatasseva, niddhame malamattano’’.
::

::hangnum
969\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vijigucchamānassa {pb:V:0.0223}{pb:T:0.0521} yadidaṃ phāsu, (sāriputtāti bhagavā)
::

::gatha2
Rittāsanaṃ sayanaṃ sevato ce;
::

::gatha2
Sambodhikāmassa yathānudhammaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Taṃ te pavakkhāmi yathā pajānaṃ.
::

::hangnum
970\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pañcannaṃ dhīro bhayānaṃ na bhāye, bhikkhu sato sapariyantacārī;
::

::gathalast
Ḍaṃsādhipātānaṃ sarīsapānaṃ, manussaphassānaṃ catuppadānaṃ.
::

::hangnum
971\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paradhammikānampi {pb:M:0.0427}{pb:P:0.0187} na santaseyya, disvāpi tesaṃ bahubheravāni;
::

::gathalast
Athāparāni abhisambhaveyya, parissayāni kusalānuesī.
::

::hangnum
972\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ātaṅkaphassena khudāya phuṭṭho, sītaṃ atuṇhaṃ {note:accuṇhaṃ (sī. syā.)} adhivāsayeyya;
::

::gathalast
So tehi phuṭṭho bahudhā anoko, vīriyaṃ parakkammadaḷhaṃ kareyya.
::

::hangnum
973\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Theyyaṃ na kāre {note:na kareyya (sī. syā. ka.)} na musā bhaṇeyya, mettāya phasse tasathāvarāni;
::

::gathalast
Yadāvilattaṃ manaso vijaññā, kaṇhassa pakkhoti vinodayeyya.
::

::hangnum
974\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kodhātimānassa {pb:T:0.0522} vasaṃ na gacche, mūlampi tesaṃ palikhañña tiṭṭhe;
::

::gathalast
Athappiyaṃ vā pana appiyaṃ vā, addhā bhavanto abhisambhaveyya.
::

::hangnum
975\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paññaṃ purakkhatvā kalyāṇapīti, vikkhambhaye tāni parissayāni;
::

::gathalast
Aratiṃ sahetha sayanamhi pante, caturo sahetha paridevadhamme.
::

::hangnum
976\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃsū asissāmi kuvaṃ vā {note:kudha vā (ka.), kutha vā (niddesa)} asissaṃ, dukkhaṃ vata settha kvajja sessaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ete vitakke paridevaneyye, vinayetha sekho aniketacārī.
::

::hangnum
977\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Annañca {pb:P:0.0188} laddhā vasanañca kāle, mattaṃ so jaññā idha tosanatthaṃ;
::

::gathalast
So tesu gutto yatacāri gāme, rusitopi vācaṃ pharusaṃ na vajjā.
::

::hangnum
978\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Okkhittacakkhu {pb:M:0.0428}{pb:V:0.0224} na ca pādalolo, jhānānuyutto bahujāgarassa;
::

::gathalast
Upekkhamārabbha samāhitatto, takkāsayaṃ kukkucciyūpachinde.
::

::hangnum
979\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cudito {pb:T:0.0523} vacībhi satimābhinande, sabrahmacārīsu khilaṃ pabhinde;
::

::gathalast
Vācaṃ pamuñce kusalaṃ nātivelaṃ, janavādadhammāya na cetayeyya.
::

::hangnum
980\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Athāparaṃ pañca rajāni loke, yesaṃ satīmā vinayāya sikkhe;
::

::gathalast
Rūpesu saddesu atho rasesu, gandhesu phassesu sahetha rāgaṃ.
::

::hangnum
981\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Etesu dhammesu vineyya chandaṃ, bhikkhu satimā suvimuttacitto;
::

::gatha2
Kālena {pb:P:0.0189} so sammā dhammaṃ parivīmaṃsamāno,
::

::gathalast
Ekodibhūto vihane tamaṃ so’’ti.
::

::centre
Sāriputtasuttaṃ soḷasamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

::centre
Aṭṭhakavaggo catuttho
::

Niṭṭhito.

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Kāmaṃ guhañca duṭṭhā ca, suddhañca paramā jarā;
::

::gathalast
Metteyyo ca pasūro ca, māgaṇḍi purābhedanaṃ.
::

::gatha1
Kalahaṃ dve ca byūhāni {note:byūhāni (sī.)}, punadeva tuvaṭṭakaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Attadaṇḍavaraṃ suttaṃ, therapuṭṭhena {note:therapañhena (sī.), sāriputtena (syā.)} soḷasa;
::

::gathalast
Iti etāni suttāni, sabbānaṭṭhakavaggikāti.
::

### 5. Pārāyanavaggo

#### Vatthugāthā

::hangnum
982\.
::

::gatha1
Kosalānaṃ {pb:M:0.0429}{pb:V:0.0225}{pb:P:0.0190}{pb:T:0.0524} purā rammā, agamā dakkhiṇāpathaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ākiñcaññaṃ patthayāno, brāhmaṇo mantapāragū.
::

::hangnum
983\.
::

::gatha1
So assakassa visaye, aḷakassa {note:muḷakassa (syā.), mūḷhakassa (ka.), maḷakassa (niddesa)} samāsane;
::

::gathalast
Vasi godhāvarīkūle, uñchena ca phalena ca.
::

::hangnum
984\.
::

::gatha1
Tasseva upanissāya, gāmo ca vipulo ahu;
::

::gathalast
Tato jātena āyena, mahāyaññamakappayi.
::

::hangnum
985\.
::

::gatha1
Mahāyaññaṃ yajitvāna, puna pāvisi assamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tasmiṃ paṭipaviṭṭhamhi, añño āgañchi brāhmaṇo.
::

::hangnum
986\.
::

::gatha1
Ugghaṭṭapādo tasito {note:tassito (ka.)}, paṅkadanto rajassiro;
::

::gathalast
So ca naṃ upasaṅkamma, satāni pañca yācati.
::

::hangnum
987\.
::

::gatha1
Tamenaṃ bāvarī disvā, āsanena nimantayi;
::

::gathalast
Sukhañca kusalaṃ pucchi, idaṃ vacanamabravi.
::

::hangnum
988\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ kho mama deyyadhammaṃ, sabbaṃ visajjitaṃ mayā;
::

::gathalast
Anujānāhi me brahme, natthi pañcasatāni me’’.
::

::hangnum
989\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sace {pb:P:0.0191} me yācamānassa, bhavaṃ nānupadassati;
::

::gathalast
Sattame divase tuyhaṃ, muddhā phalatu sattadhā’’.
::

::hangnum
990\.
::

::gatha1
Abhisaṅkharitvā {pb:V:0.0226}{pb:T:0.0525} kuhako, bheravaṃ so akittayi;
::

::gathalast
Tassa taṃ vacanaṃ sutvā, bāvarī dukkhito ahu.
::

::hangnum
991\.
::

::gatha1
Ussussati anāhāro, sokasallasamappito;
::

::gathalast
Athopi evaṃ cittassa, jhāne na ramatī mano.
::

::hangnum
992\.
::

::gatha1
Utrastaṃ dukkhitaṃ disvā, devatā atthakāminī;
::

::gathalast
Bāvariṃ upasaṅkamma, idaṃ vacanamabravi.
::

::hangnum
993\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:M:0.0430} so muddhaṃ pajānāti, kuhako so dhanatthiko;
::

::gathalast
Muddhani muddhapāte vā, ñāṇaṃ tassa na vijjati’’.
::

::hangnum
994\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhotī carahi jānāsi, taṃ me akkhāhi pucchitā;
::

::gathalast
Muddhaṃ muddhādhipātañca, taṃ suṇoma vaco tava’’.
::

::hangnum
995\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahampetaṃ na jānāmi, ñāṇamettha na vijjati;
::

::gathalast
Muddhani muddhādhipāte ca, jinānaṃ hettha {note:muddhaṃ muddhādhipāto ca, jinānaṃ heta (sī. syā. pī.)} dassanaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
996\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atha ko carahi jānāti, asmiṃ pathavimaṇḍale {note:puthavimaṇḍale (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Muddhaṃ muddhādhipātañca, taṃ me akkhāhi devate’’.
::

::hangnum
997\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Purā {pb:P:0.0192} kapilavatthumhā, nikkhanto lokanāyako;
::

::gathalast
Apacco okkākarājassa, sakyaputto pabhaṅkaro.
::

::hangnum
998\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So hi brāhmaṇa sambuddho, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
::

::gatha2
Sabbābhiññābalappatto, sabbadhammesu cakkhumā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbakammakkhayaṃ patto, vimutto upadhikkhaye.
::

::hangnum
999\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Buddho so bhagavā loke, dhammaṃ deseti cakkhumā;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ {pb:T:0.0526} tvaṃ gantvāna pucchassu, so te taṃ byākarissati’’.
::

::hangnum
1000\.
::

::gatha1
Sambuddhoti {pb:V:0.0227} vaco sutvā, udaggo bāvarī ahu;
::

::gathalast
Sokassa tanuko āsi, pītiñca vipulaṃ labhi.
::

::hangnum
1001\.
::

::gatha1
So bāvarī attamano udaggo, taṃ devataṃ pucchati vedajāto;
::

::gatha2
‘‘Katamamhi gāme nigamamhi vā pana, katamamhi vā janapade lokanātho;
::

::gathalast
Yattha gantvāna passemu {note:gantvā namassemu (sī. syā. pī.)}, sambuddhaṃ dvipaduttamaṃ’’ {note:dvipaduttamaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)},.
::

::hangnum
1002\.

::gatha1
‘‘Sāvatthiyaṃ kosalamandire jino, pahūtapañño varabhūrimedhaso;
::

::gathalast
So sakyaputto vidhuro anāsavo, muddhādhipātassa vidū narāsabho’’.
::

::hangnum
1003\.

::gatha1
Tato {pb:M:0.0431} āmantayī sisse, brāhmaṇe mantapārage;

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
1004\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
1005\.

::hangnum
1007\.

::gatha1

::hangnum
1008\.

::gatha1

1009\.

1010\.

::gatha1

::hangnum
1011\.

1012\.

::gatha1

1017\.

::hangnum
1022\.

::hangnum
1024\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
1026\.

::gathalast

::hangnum
1027\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Lakkhaṇānaṃ {pb:P:0.0196} pavicayaṃ, bāvarissa naruttama;
::

::gathalast
Kaṅkhacchida {note:taṇhacchida (bahūsu)} pakāsehi, mā no kaṅkhāyitaṃ ahu’’.
::

::hangnum
1028\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mukhaṃ jivhāya chādeti, uṇṇassa bhamukantare;
::

::gathalast
Kosohitaṃ vatthaguyhaṃ, evaṃ jānāhi māṇava’’.
::

::hangnum
1029\.
::

::gatha1
Pucchañhi {pb:V:0.0230} kiñci asuṇanto, sutvā pañhe viyākate;
::

::gathalast
Vicinteti jano sabbo, vedajāto katañjalī.
::

::hangnum
1030\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ko nu devo vā brahmā vā, indo vāpi sujampati;
::

::gathalast
Manasā pucchite pañhe, kametaṃ paṭibhāsati.
::

::hangnum
1031\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Muddhaṃ muddhādhipātañca, bāvarī paripucchati;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ byākarohi bhagavā, kaṅkhaṃ vinaya no ise’’.
::

::hangnum
1032\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Avijjā muddhāti jānāhi, vijjā muddhādhipātinī;
::

::gathalast
Saddhāsatisamādhīhi, chandavīriyena saṃyutā’’.
::

::hangnum
1033\.
::

::gatha1
Tato vedena mahatā, santhambhitvāna māṇavo;
::

::gathalast
Ekaṃsaṃ ajinaṃ katvā, pādesu sirasā pati.
::

::hangnum
1034\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bāvarī brāhmaṇo bhoto, saha sissehi mārisa;
::

::gathalast
Udaggacitto sumano, pāde vandati cakkhuma’’.
::

::hangnum
1035\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sukhito {pb:P:0.0197} bāvarī hotu, saha sissehi brāhmaṇo;
::

::gathalast
Tvañcāpi sukhito hohi, ciraṃ jīvāhi māṇava.
::

::hangnum
1036\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bāvarissa {pb:T:0.0530} ca tuyhaṃ vā, sabbesaṃ sabbasaṃsayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Katāvakāsā pucchavho, yaṃ kiñci manasicchatha’’.
::

::hangnum
1037\.
::

::gatha1
Sambuddhena katokāso, nisīditvāna pañjalī;
::

::gathalast
Ajito paṭhamaṃ pañhaṃ, tattha pucchi tathāgataṃ.
::

::centre
Vatthugāthā niṭṭhitā.
::

#### 1. Ajitamāṇavapucchā

::hangnum
1038\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kenassu {pb:M:0.0434}{pb:V:0.0231} nivuto loko, (iccāyasmā ajito)
::

::gatha2
Kenassu nappakāsati;
::

::gathalast
Kissābhilepanaṃ brūsi, kiṃsu tassa mahabbhayaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1039\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Avijjāya nivuto loko, (ajitāti bhagavā)
::

::gatha2
Vevicchā pamādā nappakāsati;
::

::gathalast
Jappābhilepanaṃ brūmi, dukkhamassa mahabbhayaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1040\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Savanti {pb:P:0.0198} sabbadhi sotā, (iccāyasmā ajito)
::

::gatha2
Sotānaṃ kiṃ nivāraṇaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sotānaṃ saṃvaraṃ brūhi, kena sotā pidhiyyare’’ {note:pithiyyare (sī. syā. pī.), pithīyare (sī. aṭṭha.), pidhīyare (?)}.
::

::hangnum
1041\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yāni sotāni lokasmiṃ, (ajitāti bhagavā)
::

::gatha2
Sati tesaṃ nivāraṇaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sotānaṃ saṃvaraṃ brūmi, paññāyete pidhiyyare’’.
::

::hangnum
1042\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paññā ceva sati yañca {note:satī ceva (sī.), satī ca (syā.), satī cāpi (pī. niddesa), sati cāpi (niddesa)}, (iccāyasmā ajito)
::

::gatha2
Nāmarūpañca mārisa;
::

::gathalast
Etaṃ {pb:T:0.0531} me puṭṭho pabrūhi, katthetaṃ uparujjhati’’.
::

::hangnum
1043\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yametaṃ pañhaṃ apucchi, ajita taṃ vadāmi te;
::

::gatha2
Yattha nāmañca rūpañca, asesaṃ uparujjhati;
::

::gathalast
Viññāṇassa nirodhena, etthetaṃ uparujjhati’’.
::

::hangnum
1044\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye ca saṅkhātadhammāse, ye ca sekhā puthū idha;
::

::gathalast
Tesaṃ me nipako iriyaṃ, puṭṭho pabrūhi mārisa’’.
::

::hangnum
1045\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kāmesu {pb:V:0.0232} nābhigijjheyya, manasānāvilo siyā;
::

::gathalast
Kusalo sabbadhammānaṃ, sato bhikkhu paribbaje’’ti.
::

::centre
Ajitamāṇavapucchā paṭhamā niṭṭhitā.
::

#### 2. Tissametteyyamāṇavapucchā

::hangnum
1046\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kodha {pb:M:0.0435}{pb:P:0.0199} santusito loke, (iccāyasmā tissametteyyo)
::

::gatha2
Kassa no santi iñjitā;
::

::gatha3
Ko ubhantamabhiññāya, majjhe mantā na lippati {note:limpati (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Kaṃ brūsi mahāpurisoti, ko idha sibbinimaccagā’’.
::

::hangnum
1047\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kāmesu brahmacariyavā, (metteyyāti bhagavā)
::

::gatha2
Vītataṇho sadā sato;
::

::gathalast
Saṅkhāya {pb:T:0.0532} nibbuto bhikkhu, tassa no santi iñjitā.
::

::hangnum
1048\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So ubhantamabhiññāya, majjhe mantā na lippati;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ brūmi mahāpurisoti, so idha sibbinimaccagā’’ti.
::

::centre
Tissametteyyamāṇavapucchā dutiyā niṭṭhitā.
::

#### 3. Puṇṇakamāṇavapucchā

::hangnum
1049\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anejaṃ mūladassāviṃ, (iccāyasmā puṇṇako)
::

::gatha2
Atthi {note:atthī (syā.)} pañhena āgamaṃ;
::

::gatha3
Kiṃ {pb:V:0.0233} nissitā {pb:P:0.0200} isayo manujā, khattiyā brāhmaṇā devatānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yaññamakappayiṃsu puthūdha loke, pucchāmi taṃ bhagavā brūhi me taṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1050\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye kecime isayo manujā, (puṇṇakāti bhagavā)
::

::gatha2
Khattiyā brāhmaṇā devatānaṃ;
::

::gatha3
Yaññamakappayiṃsu puthūdha loke, āsīsamānā puṇṇaka itthattaṃ {note:itthabhāvaṃ (sī. syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Jaraṃ sitā yaññamakappayiṃsu’’.
::

::hangnum
1051\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye {pb:M:0.0436} kecime isayo manujā, (iccāyasmā puṇṇako)
::

::gatha2
Khattiyā brāhmaṇā devatānaṃ;
::

::gatha3
Yaññamakappayiṃsu {pb:T:0.0533} puthūdha loke, kaccissu te bhagavā yaññapathe appamattā;
::

::gathalast
Atāruṃ jātiñca jarañca mārisa, pucchāmi taṃ bhagavā brūhi me taṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1052\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āsīsanti thomayanti, abhijappanti juhanti; (Puṇṇakāti bhagavā)
::

::gatha2
Kāmābhijappanti paṭicca lābhaṃ, te yājayogā bhavarāgarattā;
::

::gathalast
Nātariṃsu jātijaranti brūmi’’.
::

::hangnum
1053\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Te {pb:P:0.0201} ce nātariṃsu yājayogā, (iccāyasmā puṇṇako)
::

::gatha2
Yaññehi jātiñca jarañca mārisa;
::

::gatha3
Atha ko carahi devamanussaloke, atāri jātiñca jarañca mārisa;
::

::gathalast
Pucchāmi taṃ bhagavā brūhi me taṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1054\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṅkhāya lokasmi paroparāni {note:parovarāni (sī. syā.)}, (puṇṇakāti bhagavā)
::

::gatha2
Yassiñjitaṃ natthi kuhiñci loke;
::

::gathalast
Santo vidhūmo anīgho nirāso, atāri so jātijaranti brūmī’’ti.
::

::centre
Puṇṇakamāṇavapucchā tatiyā niṭṭhitā.
::

#### 4. Mettagūmāṇavapucchā

::hangnum
1055\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pucchāmi {pb:V:0.0234}{pb:T:0.0534} taṃ bhagavā brūhi me taṃ, (iccāyasmā mettagū)
::

::gatha2
Maññāmi taṃ vedaguṃ bhāvitattaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kuto nu dukkhā samudāgatā ime, ye keci lokasmimanekarūpā’’.
::

::hangnum
1056\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dukkhassa {pb:M:0.0437}{pb:P:0.0202} ve maṃ pabhavaṃ apucchasi, (mettagūti bhagavā)
::

::gatha2
Taṃ te pavakkhāmi yathā pajānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Upadhinidānā pabhavanti dukkhā, ye keci lokasmimanekarūpā.
::

::hangnum
1057\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo ve avidvā upadhiṃ karoti, punappunaṃ dukkhamupeti mando;
::

::gathalast
Tasmā pajānaṃ upadhiṃ na kayirā, dukkhassa jātippabhavānupassī’’.
::

::hangnum
1058\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ taṃ apucchimha akittayī no, aññaṃ taṃ pucchāma {note:pucchāmi (sī. pī.)} tadiṅgha brūhi;
::

::gatha2
Kathaṃ nu dhīrā vitaranti oghaṃ, jātiṃ jaraṃ sokapariddavañca;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ me muni sādhu viyākarohi, tathā hi te vidito esa dhammo’’.
::

::hangnum
1059\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kittayissāmi {pb:T:0.0535} te dhammaṃ, (mettagūti bhagavā)
::

::gatha2
Diṭṭhe dhamme anītihaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ viditvā sato caraṃ, tare loke visattikaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1060\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tañcāhaṃ abhinandāmi, mahesi dhammamuttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ viditvā sato caraṃ, tare loke visattikaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1061\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ kiñci sampajānāsi, (mettagūti bhagavā)
::

::gatha2
Uddhaṃ adho tiriyañcāpi majjhe;
::

::gathalast
Etesu {pb:P:0.0203} nandiñca nivesanañca, panujja viññāṇaṃ bhave na tiṭṭhe.
::

::hangnum
1062\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evaṃvihārī {pb:V:0.0235} sato appamatto, bhikkhu caraṃ hitvā mamāyitāni;
::

::gathalast
Jātiṃ jaraṃ sokapariddavañca, idheva vidvā pajaheyya dukkhaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1063\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Etābhinandāmi {pb:M:0.0438} vaco mahesino, sukittitaṃ gotamanūpadhīkaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Addhā hi bhagavā pahāsi dukkhaṃ, tathā hi te vidito esa dhammo.
::

::hangnum
1064\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Te cāpi nūnappajaheyyu dukkhaṃ, ye tvaṃ muni aṭṭhitaṃ ovadeyya;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ taṃ namassāmi samecca nāga, appeva maṃ bhagavā aṭṭhitaṃ ovadeyya’’.
::

::hangnum
1065\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ {pb:T:0.0536} brāhmaṇaṃ vedagumābhijaññā, akiñcanaṃ kāmabhave asattaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Addhā hi so oghamimaṃ atāri, tiṇṇo ca pāraṃ akhilo akaṅkho.
::

::hangnum
1066\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vidvā ca yo {note:so (sī. syā. pī.)} vedagū naro idha, bhavābhave saṅgamimaṃ visajja;
::

::gathalast
So {pb:P:0.0204} vītataṇho anīgho nirāso, atāri so jātijaranti brūmī’’ti.
::

::centre
Mettagūmāṇavapucchā catutthī niṭṭhitā.
::

#### 5. Dhotakamāṇavapucchā

::hangnum
1067\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pucchāmi taṃ bhagavā brūhi me taṃ, (iccāyasmā dhotako)
::

::gatha2
Vācābhikaṅkhāmi mahesi tuyhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tava sutvāna nigghosaṃ, sikkhe nibbānamattano’’.
::

::hangnum
1068\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tenahātappaṃ karohi, (dhotakāti bhagavā) idheva nipako sato;
::

::gathalast
Ito sutvāna nigghosaṃ, sikkhe nibbānamattano’’.
::

::hangnum
1069\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Passāmahaṃ {pb:M:0.0439} devamanussaloke, akiñcanaṃ brāhmaṇamiriyamānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ taṃ namassāmi samantacakkhu, pamuñca {pb:T:0.0537} maṃ sakka kathaṃkathāhi’’.
::

::hangnum
1070\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nāhaṃ {pb:V:0.0236} sahissāmi {note:samissāmi (syā.), gamissāmi (sī.), samīhāmi (pī.)} pamocanāya, kathaṃkathiṃ dhotaka kañci loke;
::

::gathalast
Dhammañca seṭṭhaṃ abhijānamāno {note:ājānamāno (sī. syā. pī.)}, evaṃ tuvaṃ oghamimaṃ taresi’’.
::

::hangnum
1071\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anusāsa brahme karuṇāyamāno, vivekadhammaṃ yamahaṃ vijaññaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yathāhaṃ {pb:P:0.0205} ākāsova abyāpajjamāno, idheva santo asito careyyaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1072\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kittayissāmi te santiṃ, (dhotakāti bhagavā) diṭṭhe dhamme anītihaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ viditvā sato caraṃ, tare loke visattikaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1073\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tañcāhaṃ abhinandāmi, mahesi santimuttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ viditvā sato caraṃ, tare loke visattikaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1074\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ kiñci sampajānāsi, (dhotakāti bhagavā)
::

::gatha2
Uddhaṃ adho tiriyañcāpi majjhe;
::

::gathalast
Etaṃ viditvā saṅgoti loke, bhavābhavāya mākāsi taṇha’’nti.
::

::centre
Dhotakamāṇavapucchā pañcamī niṭṭhitā.

#### 6. Upasīvamāṇavapucchā

::hangnum
1075\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Eko {pb:T:0.0538} ahaṃ sakka mahantamoghaṃ, (iccāyasmā upasīvo)
::

::gatha2
Anissito no visahāmi tārituṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ārammaṇaṃ brūhi samantacakkhu, yaṃ nissito oghamimaṃ tareyyaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1076\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ākiñcaññaṃ {pb:M:0.0440} pekkhamāno satimā, (upasīvāti bhagavā)
::

::gatha2
Natthīti nissāya tarassu oghaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kāme {pb:P:0.0206} pahāya virato kathāhi, taṇhakkhayaṃ nattamahābhipassa’’ {note:rattamahābhipassa (syā.), rattamahaṃ vipassa (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
1077\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbesu {pb:V:0.0237} kāmesu yo vītarāgo, (iccāyasmā upasīvo)
::

::gatha2
Ākiñcaññaṃ nissito hitvā maññaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Saññāvimokkhe parame vimutto {note:dhimutto (ka.)}, tiṭṭhe nu so tattha anānuyāyī’’ {note:anānuvāyī (syā. ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
1078\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbesu kāmesu yo vītarāgo, (upasīvāti bhagavā)
::

::gatha2
Ākiñcaññaṃ nissito hitvā maññaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Saññāvimokkhe parame vimutto, tiṭṭheyya so tattha anānuyāyī’’.
::

::hangnum
1079\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tiṭṭhe ce so tattha anānuyāyī, pūgampi {pb:T:0.0539} vassānaṃ samantacakkhu;
::

::gathalast
Tattheva so sītisiyā vimutto, cavetha viññāṇaṃ tathāvidhassa’’.
::

::hangnum
1080\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Accī yathā vātavegena khittā {note:khittaṃ (syā.), khitto (pī.)}, (upasīvāti bhagavā)
::

::gatha2
Atthaṃ paleti na upeti saṅkhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ {pb:P:0.0207} munī nāmakāyā vimutto, atthaṃ paleti na upeti saṅkhaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1081\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atthaṅgato so uda vā so natthi, udāhu ve sassatiyā arogo;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ me munī sādhu viyākarohi, tathā hi te vidito esa dhammo’’.
::

::hangnum
1082\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atthaṅgatassa {pb:M:0.0441} na pamāṇamatthi, (upasīvāti bhagavā)
::

::gatha2
Yena naṃ vajjuṃ taṃ tassa natthi;
::

::gathalast
Sabbesu dhammesu samūhatesu, samūhatā vādapathāpi sabbe’’ti.
::

::centre
Upasīvamāṇavapucchā chaṭṭhī niṭṭhitā.
::

#### 7. Nandamāṇavapucchā

::hangnum
1083\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Santi {pb:V:0.0238} loke munayo, (iccāyasmā nando)
::

::gatha2
Janā vadanti tayidaṃ kathaṃsu;
::

::gathalast
Ñāṇūpapannaṃ {pb:T:0.0540} no muniṃ {note:muni no (syā. ka.)} vadanti, udāhu ve jīvitenūpapannaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1084\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na diṭṭhiyā na sutiyā na ñāṇena, (na sīlabbatena) {note:( ) natthi sī.-pī potthakesu}
::

::gatha2
Munīdha nanda kusalā vadanti;
::

::gathalast
Visenikatvā {pb:P:0.0208} anīghā nirāsā, caranti ye te munayoti brūmi’’.
::

::hangnum
1085\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye kecime samaṇabrāhmaṇāse, (iccāyasmā nando)
::

::gatha2
Diṭṭhassutenāpi {note:diṭṭhena sutenāpi (sī.), diṭṭhe sutenāpi (syā. pī. ka.)} vadanti suddhiṃ;
::

::gatha3
Sīlabbatenāpi vadanti suddhiṃ, anekarūpena vadanti suddhiṃ;
::

::gatha2
Kaccissu te bhagavā tattha yatā carantā, atāru jātiñca jarañca mārisa;
::

::gathalast
Pucchāmi taṃ bhagavā brūhi me taṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1086\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye {pb:M:0.0442} kecime samaṇabrāhmaṇāse, (nandāti bhagavā)
::

::gatha2
Diṭṭhassutenāpi vadanti suddhiṃ;
::

::gatha3
Sīlabbatenāpi vadanti suddhiṃ, anekarūpena vadanti suddhiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kiñcāpi te tattha yatā caranti, nāriṃsu jātijaranti brūmi’’.
::

::hangnum
1087\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye {pb:T:0.0541} kecime samaṇabrāhmaṇāse, (iccāyasmā nando)
::

::gatha2
Diṭṭhassutenāpi vadanti suddhiṃ;
::

::gatha3
Sīlabbatenāpi vadanti suddhiṃ, anekarūpena vadanti suddhiṃ;
::

::gatha2
Te ce muni {note:sace muni (sī.)} brūsi anoghatiṇṇe, atha {pb:P:0.0209} ko carahi devamanussaloke;
::

::gathalast
Atāri jātiñca jarañca mārisa, pucchāmi taṃ bhagavā brūhi me taṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1088\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nāhaṃ sabbe samaṇabrāhmaṇāse, (nandāti bhagavā)
::

::gatha2
Jātijarāya nivutāti brūmi;
::

::gatha3
Ye {pb:V:0.0239} sīdha diṭṭhaṃva sutaṃ mutaṃ vā, sīlabbataṃ vāpi pahāya sabbaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Anekarūpampi pahāya sabbaṃ, taṇhaṃ pariññāya anāsavāse;
::

::gathalast
Te ve narā oghatiṇṇāti brūmi’’.
::

::hangnum
1089\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Etābhinandāmi vaco mahesino, sukittitaṃ gotamanūpadhīkaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Ye sīdha diṭṭhaṃ va sutaṃ mutaṃ vā, sīlabbataṃ vāpi pahāya sabbaṃ;
::

::gatha3
Anekarūpampi {pb:T:0.0542} pahāya sabbaṃ, taṇhaṃ pariññāya anāsavāse;
::

::gathalast
Ahampi te oghatiṇṇāti brūmī’’ti.
::

::centre
Nandamāṇavapucchā sattamā niṭṭhitā.
::

::

::gatha2

#### Pārāyanatthutigāthā

Idamavoca {pb:M:0.0449} bhagavā magadhesu viharanto pāsāṇake cetiye, paricārakasoḷasānaṃ {note:paricārakasoḷasannaṃ (syā. ka.)} brāhmaṇānaṃ ajjhiṭṭho puṭṭho puṭṭho pañhaṃ {note:pañhe (sī. pī.)} byākāsi. Ekamekassa cepi pañhassa atthamaññāya dhammamaññāya dhammānudhammaṃ paṭipajjeyya, gaccheyyeva jarāmaraṇassa pāraṃ. Pāraṅgamanīyā ime dhammāti, tasmā imassa dhammapariyāyassa pārāyananteva {note:pārāyaṇaṃtveva (sī. aṭṭha.)} adhivacanaṃ.

::hangnum
1130\.
::

::gatha1
Ajito tissametteyyo, puṇṇako atha mettagū;
::

::gathalast
Dhotako upasīvo ca, nando ca atha hemako.
::

::hangnum
1131\.
::

::gatha1
Todeyya-kappā {pb:P:0.0219} dubhayo, jatukaṇṇī ca paṇḍito;
::

::gatha2
Bhadrāvudho udayo ca, posālo cāpi brāhmaṇo;
::

::gathalast
Mogharājā {pb:T:0.0551} ca medhāvī, piṅgiyo ca mahāisi.
::

::hangnum
1132\.
::

::gatha1
Ete buddhaṃ upāgacchuṃ, sampannacaraṇaṃ isiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pucchantā nipuṇe pañhe, buddhaseṭṭhaṃ upāgamuṃ.
::

::hangnum
1133\.
::

::gatha1
Tesaṃ buddho pabyākāsi, pañhe puṭṭho yathātathaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pañhānaṃ veyyākaraṇena, tosesi brāhmaṇe muni.
::

::hangnum
1134\.
::

::gatha1
Te tositā cakkhumatā, buddhenādiccabandhunā;
::

::gathalast
Brahmacariyamacariṃsu, varapaññassa santike.
::

::hangnum
1135\.
::

::gatha1
Ekamekassa {pb:V:0.0247} pañhassa, yathā buddhena desitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tathā yo paṭipajjeyya, gacche pāraṃ apārato.
::

::hangnum
1136\.
::

::gatha1
Apārā pāraṃ gaccheyya, bhāvento maggamuttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Maggo so pāraṃ gamanāya, tasmā pārāyanaṃ iti.
::
