::

::gathalast
Namassamāno vivasemi rattiṃ, teneva maññāmi avippavāsaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1149\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saddhā ca pīti ca mano sati ca, nāpenti me gotamasāsanamhā;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ yaṃ disaṃ vajati bhūripañño, sa tena teneva natohamasmi.
::

::hangnum
1150\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jiṇṇassa {pb:P:0.0222} me dubbalathāmakassa, teneva kāyo na paleti tattha;
::

::gathalast
Saṃkappayantāya {note:saṃkappayattāya (sī.)} vajāmi niccaṃ, mano hi me brāhmaṇa tena yutto.
::

::hangnum
1151\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṅke sayāno pariphandamāno, dīpā dīpaṃ upaplaviṃ {note:upallaviṃ (syā. niddesa)};
::

::gathalast
Athaddasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ, oghatiṇṇamanāsavaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1152\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yathā ahū vakkali muttasaddho, bhadrāvudho āḷavi gotamo ca;
::

::gatha2
Evameva tvampi pamuñcassu saddhaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Gamissasi tvaṃ piṅgiya maccudheyyassa pāraṃ’’ {note:maccudheyyapāraṃ (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
1153\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Esa bhiyyo pasīdāmi, sutvāna munino vaco;
::

::gathalast
Vivaṭṭacchado {pb:T:0.0554} sambuddho, akhilo paṭibhānavā.
::

::hangnum
1154\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Adhideve {pb:V:0.0249} abhiññāya, sabbaṃ vedi varovaraṃ {note:paro varaṃ (sī. syā.), paro paraṃ (niddesa)};
::

::gathalast
Pañhānantakaro satthā, kaṅkhīnaṃ paṭijānataṃ.
::

::hangnum
1155\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Asaṃhīraṃ {pb:P:0.0223} asaṅkuppaṃ, yassa natthi upamā kvaci;
::

::gathalast
Addhā gamissāmi na mettha kaṅkhā, evaṃ maṃ dhārehi adhimuttacitta’’nti.
::

::centre
Pārāyanavaggo pañcamo niṭṭhito.
::

Suttuddānaṃ –

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
Urago {pb:M:0.0452} {note:imā uddānagāthāyo sī. pī. potthakesu na santi} dhaniyopi ca, khaggavisāṇo kasi ca;
::

::gatha2
Cundo bhavo punadeva, vasalo ca karaṇīyañca;
::

::gathalast
Hemavato atha yakkho, vijayasuttaṃ munisuttavaranti.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
Paṭhamakaṭṭhavaro varavaggo, dvādasasuttadharo suvibhatto;
::

::gathalast
Desito cakkhumatā vimalena, suyyati vaggavaro uragoti.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
Ratanāmagandho hirimaṅgalanāmo, sucilomakapilo ca brāhmaṇadhammo;
::

::gathalast
Nāvā {note:nātha (ka.)} kiṃsīlauṭṭhahano ca, rāhulo {pb:T:0.0555} ca punapi vaṅgīso.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
Sammāparibbājanīyopi cettha, dhammikasuttavaro suvibhatto;
::

::gathalast
Cuddasasuttadharo dutiyamhi, cūḷakavaggavaroti tamāhu.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
Pabbajjapadhānasubhāsitanāmo, pūraḷāso punadeva māgho ca;
::

::gathalast
Sabhiyaṃ keṇiyameva sallanāmo, vāseṭṭhavaro kālikopi ca.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
Nālakasuttavaro suvibhatto, taṃ anupassī tathā punadeva;
::

::gathalast
Dvādasasuttadharo tatiyamhi, suyyati vaggavaro mahānāmo.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
Kāmaguhaṭṭhakaduṭṭhakanāmā{pb:V:0.0250}, suddhavaro paramaṭṭhakanāmo;
::

::gathalast
Jarā mettiyavaro suvibhatto, pasūramāgaṇḍiyā purābhedo.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
Kalahavivādo {pb:M:0.0453} ubho viyuhā ca, tuvaṭakaattadaṇḍasāriputtā;
::

::gathalast
Soḷasasuttadharo catutthamhi, aṭṭhakavaggavaroti {pb:T:0.0556} tamāhu.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
Magadhe janapade ramaṇīye, desavare katapuññanivese;
::

::gathalast
Pāsāṇakacetiyavare suvibhatte, vasi bhagavā gaṇaseṭṭho.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
Ubhayavāsamāgatiyamhi {note:ubhayaṃ vā puṇṇasamāgataṃ yamhi (syā.)}, dvādasayojaniyā parisāya;
::

::gatha2
Soḷasabrāhmaṇānaṃ kira puṭṭho, pucchāya soḷasapañhakammiyā;
::

::gathalast
Nippakāsayi dhammamadāsi.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
Atthapakāsakabyañjanapuṇṇaṃ, dhammamadesesi parakhemajaniyaṃ {note:varaṃ khamanīyaṃ (ka.)};
::

::gatha2
Lokahitāya jino dvipadaggo, suttavaraṃ bahudhammavicitraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbakilesapamocanahetuṃ, desayi suttavaraṃ dvipadaggo.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
Byañjanamatthapadaṃ samayuttaṃ {note:byañjanamatthapadasamayuttaṃ (syā.)}, akkharasaññitaopamagāḷhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Lokavicāraṇañāṇapabhaggaṃ, desayi suttavaraṃ dvipadaggo.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
Rāgamale {pb:T:0.0557} amalaṃ vimalaggaṃ, dosamale amalaṃ vimalaggaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Mohamale amalaṃ vimalaggaṃ, lokavicāraṇañāṇapabhaggaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Desayi suttavaraṃ dvipadaggo.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
Klesamale {pb:M:0.0454} amalaṃ vimalaggaṃ, duccaritamale amalaṃ vimalaggaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Lokavicāraṇañāṇapabhaggaṃ, desayi suttavaraṃ dvipadaggo.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
Āsavabandhanayogākilesaṃ, nīvaraṇāni ca tīṇi malāni;
::

::gathalast
Tassa kilesapamocanahetuṃ, desayi suttavaraṃ dvipadaggo.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
Nimmalasabbakilesapanūdaṃ, rāgavirāgamanejamasokaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Santapaṇītasududdasadhammaṃ, desayi {pb:T:0.0558} suttavaraṃ dvipadaggo.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
Rāgañca {pb:V:0.0251} dosakamabhañjitasantaṃ {note:dosañca bhañjitasantaṃ (syā.)}, yonicatuggatipañcaviññāṇaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṇhāratacchadanatāṇalatāpamokkhaṃ {note:taṇhātalaratacchedanatāṇapamokkhaṃ (syā.)}, desayi suttavaraṃ dvipadaggo.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
Gambhīraduddasasaṇhanipuṇaṃ, paṇḍitavedaniyaṃ nipuṇatthaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Lokavicāraṇañāṇapabhaggaṃ, desayi suttavaraṃ dvipadaggo.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
Navaṅgakusumamālagīveyyaṃ, indriyajhānavimokkhavibhattaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Aṭṭhaṅgamaggadharaṃ varayānaṃ, desayi suttavaraṃ dvipadaggo.
::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
Somupamaṃ {pb:M:0.0455} vimalaṃ parisuddhaṃ, aṇṇavamūpamaratanasucittaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pupphasamaṃ ravimūpamatejaṃ, desayi suttavaraṃ dvipadaggo.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
Khemasivaṃ sukhasītalasantaṃ, maccutatāṇaparaṃ paramatthaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tassa sunibbutadassanahetuṃ, desayi suttavaraṃ dvipadaggoti.
::

::centre
Suttanipātapāḷi niṭṭhitā.
::
